# nlin.SI [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Orlov-Schulman symmetries of the self-dual conformal structure equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19282)
*L. V. Bogdanov*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 该论文构建了自对偶共形结构（SDCS）层次的Orlov-Schulman对称性，证明了这些额外对称性与基本Lax-Sato流的相容性，并通过基于黎曼-希尔伯特问题的dressing scheme提供了对称性的几何解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究自对偶共形结构（self-dual conformal structure, SDCS）层次中的对称性结构，特别是构建Orlov-Schulman对称性并理解其与层次基本结构的关系。

Method: 采用构造性方法构建SDCS层次的Orlov-Schulman对称性，提供额外对称性与基本Lax-Sato流相容性的显式证明，并基于黎曼-希尔伯特问题（Riemann-Hilbert problem）的dressing scheme框架描述对称性。

Result: 成功构造了SDCS层次的Orlov-Schulman对称性，证明了这些对称性与基本Lax-Sato流的相容性，并分析了包括伽利略变换（Galilean transformations）和标度变换（scalings）在内的几个简单例子。

Conclusion: 论文建立了自对偶共形结构层次中Orlov-Schulman对称性的完整理论框架，通过黎曼-希尔伯特问题的dressing scheme为这些对称性提供了清晰的几何解释，深化了对可积系统对称性结构的理解。

Abstract: We construct Orlov-Schulman symmetries for the self-dual conformal structure (SDCS) hierarchy. We provide an explicit proof of compatibility of additional symmetries with the basic Lax-Sato flows of the hierarchy, and consider several simple examples, including Galilean transformations and scalings. We also present a picture of the Orlov-Schulman symmetries in terms of a dressing scheme based on the Riemann-Hilbert problem.

</details>


<div id='astro-ph.HE'></div>

# astro-ph.HE [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Visual Characteristics of a Rotating Black Hole in $4$D Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet Gravity with Thin Accretion Disk Under EHT Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18628)
*Muhammad Israr Aslam,Manahil Ali,Abdul Malik Sultan,Xiao-Xiong Zeng,Sultan Hussain*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究在4D爱因斯坦-高斯-博内引力框架下，通过鱼眼相机模型和光线追踪方法，可视化旋转黑洞在两种照明模型（天体光球和薄吸积盘）下的阴影图像，分析耦合参数α和自旋参数a的影响，并利用M87*和Sgr A*观测数据对参数α施加约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究4D爱因斯坦-高斯-博内引力框架下旋转黑洞的视觉特征，特别是在天体光球和薄吸积盘两种照明模型下的表现。通过可视化黑洞阴影图像，分析引力理论参数对观测特征的影响。

Method: 采用鱼眼相机模型（fisheye camera model）和光线追踪方法（ray-tracing method）生成黑洞阴影图像。研究聚焦于耦合参数α和自旋参数a对阴影的影响，并利用M87*和Sgr A*的最新观测数据对参数α施加约束。

Result: 结果显示：阴影半径随α增大而减小，阴影偏差随α增大而增加；对于自旋参数a，阴影半径相比对应的阴影偏差略有增加。对于天体光球，α增大导致光子环减小，而a增大使空间拖曳效应更显著。对于薄吸积盘，阴影随a增大逐渐不对称，内阴影整体尺寸随α变化逐渐减小。

Conclusion: 研究证实了所考虑的黑洞模型与观测数据的一致性，揭示了爱因斯坦-高斯-博内引力中参数α和自旋参数a对黑洞阴影特征的显著影响，为通过黑洞阴影观测约束引力理论参数提供了理论依据。

Abstract: This study investigates the visual characteristics of a rotating black hole (BH) within the fabric of $4$D Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity illuminated with two illumination models, such as a celestial light sphere and a thin accretion disk. To visualize the BH shadow images, we use a recent fisheye camera model and ray-tracing method. And then, we focus on investigating the impact of the coupling parameter $α$ and the spin parameter $a$ on the shadow images. The results exhibit that the shadow radius decreases, while the shadow deviation increases with the aid of $α$. However, with respect to $a$, the shadow radius is slightly increased compared to the corresponding shadow deviation. For a celestial light sphere, the increasing values of $α$, lead to a decrease in the corresponding photon ring, while the space-dragging effect becomes more prominent with increasing $a$. For a thin accretion disk, we enhance its inner edge to the BH event horizon, and the particle motion is different in the regions inside and outside the innermost stable circular orbit. The result demonstrates that the shadow becomes progressively asymmetric with $a$, while the overall size of the inner shadow gradually decreases with the variations of $α$. Subsequently, we also investigated the distinct features of red-shift configurations on the disk for both direct and lensed images. Additionally, we used the latest observational data from M87* and Sgr A* to impose certain parameter constraints on $α$; the results depict the consistency of our considering the BH model.

</details>


### [3] [A comprehensive framework for phase-coherent mapping of the gravitational-wave sky with pulsar timing arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19073)
*Małgorzata Curyło,Eric Thrane,Paul D. Lasky,Dawson S. Gaynor*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种用于脉冲星计时阵列的相位相干映射技术，能够解析引力波天空的全复数极化状态，为后续分析提供统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准互相关方法无法保留信号的振幅、相位和极化信息，需要一种能够完整解析引力波天空极化状态的技术，为后续分析提供统一的数据基础。

Method: 开发了一种相位相干映射技术（phase-coherent mapping technique），能够解析引力波天空的全复数极化状态，该方法与现有脉冲星计时数据分析方法完全兼容，并通过一系列真实模拟进行验证。

Result: 该框架在不同阵列配置、噪声特性和信号类型的模拟中表现出稳健性，能够准确恢复源振幅和天空位置，并分析了极化泄漏、噪声和方向依赖性阵列灵敏度对信号恢复的影响。

Conclusion: 相位相干映射技术提供了一种紧凑、最小化处理的数据摘要，从中可以衍生出所有后续分析，包括随机背景表征、各向异性搜索和单个源识别，形成了一个统一的框架。

Abstract: We present a practical implementation of a phase-coherent mapping technique for pulsar timing arrays that resolves the full complex polarisation state of the gravitational-wave sky as a function of direction and frequency. Unlike standard cross-correlation methods, this approach preserves the amplitude, phase, and polarisation of the signal in every sky pixel. The resulting maps constitute a compact, minimally processed summary of the data from which all subsequent analyses -- characterisation of a stochastic background, searches for anisotropy, and identification of individual sources -- can be derived within a single unified framework. Our implementation is fully compatible with established pulsar timing data analysis methods. We validate the framework through a series of realistic simulations with varying array configurations, noise properties, and signal types. We demonstrate robust recovery of source amplitudes and sky locations across different scenarios, and discuss the impact of polarisation leakage, noise, and direction-dependent array sensitivity on the recovery of astrophysical signals.

</details>

# cond-mat.quant-gas [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Stabilization of bulk quantum orders in finite Rydberg atom arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18890)
*Yash M. Lokare,Matthew J. Coley-O'Rourke*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种通过驱动边界进入无序相（disordered phase）来减轻有限尺寸里德堡原子阵列（Rydberg atom arrays）边界效应的方法，使有限系统能够稳定体相（bulk-like）量子序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 里德堡原子阵列（Rydberg atom arrays）作为量子模拟平台，其有限尺寸系统的理论预测与实验实现常因边界效应（boundary effects）而存在差异，需要一种减轻边界影响的方法。

Method: 提出利用里德堡系统中普遍存在的无序相（disordered phase）特性，驱动边界进入一组无偏的构型（unbiased set of configurations），这些构型依赖于体相物理。

Result: 通过数值模拟在一维和二维系统中的有序相（ordered phases）和临界相（critical phases）上验证了该协议的有效性。

Conclusion: 该策略为有限尺寸里德堡原子阵列实现体相量子序提供了一种通用且实验上直接可行的方法，有助于弥合理论预测与实验实现之间的差距。

Abstract: Arrays of ultracold neutral atoms, also known as Rydberg atom arrays, are rapidly developing into a powerful and versatile platform for quantum simulation. However, theoretical predictions about the bulk quantum phases of matter present in these systems have often diverged from experimental realizations on finite-sized arrays due to the strong effects of the boundaries. Here we propose a general, experimentally straightforward strategy to mitigate the effects of the boundaries and thus enable finite-sized arrays to stabilize bulk-like quantum order. Our scheme makes use of the properties of the ubiquitous disordered phase in Rydberg systems, driving the boundaries into an unbiased set of configurations that depend on the bulk physics. We numerically demonstrate the efficacy of this protocol in one- and two-dimensional systems on both ordered and critical phases.

</details>

# math.AG [[Back]](#toc)

### [5] [From Finite-Node Conifold Geometry to BPS Structures I: Algebraic State Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19441)
*Abdul Rahman*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究具有有限个普通双奇点（ordinary double points）的三维复形退化（degeneration），提取其内在代数状态数据（intrinsic algebraic state data），包括有限局部商（finite localized quotient）、节点耦合空间（nodewise coupling space）及其分解、以及系数向量（coefficient vector）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在从有限节点几何、扩展理论、混合霍奇结构（mixed-Hodge）和范畴输入中提取退化所携带的内在代数状态数据。具体目标是分离出有限局部商、节点耦合空间及其规范分解，以及定义在修正反常层（corrected perverse sheaf）上的系数向量。

Method: 通过分析单参数退化（one-parameter degeneration）的中心纤维（central fiber）上的有限节点结构，提取三个核心代数对象：有限局部商 $Q_Σ$、节点耦合空间 $E_Σ$ 及其规范分解 $E_Σ≅⨁_{k=1}^r ℚe_k$，以及系数向量 $c_Σ∈ℚ^r$。这些数据从反常层、混合霍奇模（mixed-Hodge-module）和schober实现三个层面进行提取和验证。

Result: 证明了这些状态变量与修正反常层的混合霍奇模提升（mixed-Hodge-module lift）和schober实现都兼容，使得相同的有限节点架构同时出现在反常层、混合霍奇结构和范畴形式中。由此得到的包 $(V_Σ,E_Σ,c_Σ)$ 构成了附着于有限节点锥形退化（finite-node conifold degeneration）的内在代数状态数据。

Conclusion: 提取的代数状态数据 $(V_Σ,E_Σ,c_Σ)$ 为从有限节点几何到后续的关联结构（incidence）、箭图（quiver）、稳定性条件（stability）、BPS谱（BPS-spectral）和壁交叉结构（wall-crossing structures）的过渡提供了第一个代数层。这一框架统一了反常层、混合霍奇模和范畴三种表现形式中的有限节点架构。

Abstract: Let $π:X\to Δ$ be a one-parameter degeneration whose central fiber $X_0$ is a complex threefold with finitely many ordinary double points $Σ=\{p_1,\dots,p_r\}\subset X_0$. Associated with this degeneration is the corrected finite-node perverse extension, together with its mixed-Hodge-module refinement and a finite-node schober datum whose perverse-sheaf shadow is identified with the corrected perverse sheaf $\mathcal P$. The purpose of the present paper is to extract from these finite-node geometric, extension-theoretic, mixed-Hodge, and categorical inputs the intrinsic algebraic state data carried by the degeneration. More precisely, we isolate the finite localized quotient $Q_Σ:=\bigoplus_{k=1}^r i_{k*}\Q_{\{p_k\}}$, the nodewise coupling space $E_Σ:=\Ext^1_{\Perv(X_0;\Q)}(Q_Σ,IC_{X_0})$, its canonical nodewise decomposition $E_Σ\cong\bigoplus_{k=1}^r \Q e_k$, and the coefficient vector $c_Σ=(c_1,\dots,c_r)\in\Q^r$ defined by $[\mathcal P]_{\mathrm{perv}}=\sum_{k=1}^r c_k e_k$. We then prove that these state variables are compatible with both the mixed-Hodge-module lift and the schober realization of $\mathcal P$, so that the same finite-node architecture appears simultaneously in perverse, mixed-Hodge, and categorical form. The resulting package $(V_Σ,E_Σ,c_Σ)$ is the intrinsic algebraic state data attached to the finite-node conifold degeneration. It provides the first algebraic layer in the passage from finite-node geometry to later incidence, quiver, stability, BPS-spectral, and wall-crossing structures.

</details>


<div id='quant-ph'></div>

# quant-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [A direct algebraic proof for the non-positivity of Liouvillian eigenvalues in Markovian quantum dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2504.02256)
*Yikang Zhang,Thomas Barthel*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文为马尔可夫开放量子系统中Liouvillian算符特征值实部非正性提供了一个直接的代数证明，替代了传统的间接论证方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 马尔可夫开放量子系统由Lindblad主方程描述，其中Liouvillian算符的特征值实部非正性是系统稳定性的基本性质。传统上通过量子通道的收缩性进行间接论证，本文旨在提供更直接的代数证明。

Method: 基于Liouvillian算符的Lindblad形式，采用直接的代数证明方法，避免了传统间接论证中量子通道收缩性的使用。

Result: 成功构建了基于Lindblad形式的直接代数证明，确立了Liouvillian算符所有特征值实部非正性的数学性质，对应物理系统的稳定性。

Conclusion: 本文为马尔可夫开放量子系统中Liouvillian算符特征值实部非正性提供了直接的代数证明，补充了传统间接论证方法，增强了该基本性质的数学基础。

Abstract: Markovian open quantum systems are described by the Lindblad master equation $\partial_tρ=\mathcal{L}(ρ)$, where $ρ$ denotes the system's density operator and $\mathcal{L}$ the Liouville super-operator, which is also known as the Liouvillian. For systems with a finite-dimensional Hilbert space, it is a fundamental property of the Liouvillian, that the real-parts of all its eigenvalues are non-positive which, in physical terms, corresponds to the stability of the system. The usual argument for this property is indirect, using that $\mathcal{L}$ generates a quantum channel and that quantum channels are contractive. We provide a direct algebraic proof based on the Lindblad form of Liouvillians.

</details>


### [7] [Lund Plane to Bloch (LP2B) Encoding for Object and Polarization Tagging with Quantum Jet Substructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18613)
*Fabrizio Napolitano,Luca Della Penna,Tommaso Tedeschi,Livio Fanò*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将喷注（jet）子结构分析中的Lund平面映射到量子比特状态的LP2B编码方法，并基于此构建了量子树拓扑网络（QTTN）。该网络在极化标记（polarization tagging）任务上达到与大型经典深度学习架构相当的性能，同时参数数量减少三个数量级，且在低数据区域表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着NISQ硬件在量子比特数量和门深度方面的成熟，量子算法在喷注子结构分析中的应用日益受到关注。然而，现有的量子机器学习方法通常依赖于存在红外和共线不安全性、对非微扰效应敏感或可扩展性差的数据表示。

Method: 本文引入了Lund Plane to Bloch (LP2B)编码，将喷注运动学的理论清洁且稳健的表示直接映射到量子比特状态。基于此编码，实现了量子树拓扑网络（QTTN），该网络原生嵌入了Lund树的分层结构。

Result: QTTN在极化标记任务上与大型经典深度学习架构（如LundNet）性能相当，同时在W玻色子和顶夸克标记任务上保持竞争力。该架构在极化和W标记任务上相比标准1P1Q编码显示出增强的敏感性，且参数数量比LundNet少三个数量级。在低数据区域，QTTN优于经典方法，且对生成器特定的部分子簇射和强子化模型的过拟合敏感性更低。

Conclusion: QTTN展示了在触发系统中实现低延迟FPGA实现的潜力，适用于低产额的数据驱动分析。量子模型相比经典深度学习方法对系统不确定性的潜在影响更小，并在3量子比特SpinQ设备上进行了实际量子硬件验证。

Abstract: The application of quantum algorithms to jet substructure analysis is of growing interest as NISQ hardware continues to mature in qubit count and gate depth. Jet substructure remains essential for addressing demanding and complementary challenges at the LHC and beyond, notably object classification and polarization tagging. However, existing quantum machine learning approaches typically rely on data representations that suffer from infrared and collinear unsafety, sensitivity to non-perturbative effects, or poor scalability. In this work, we introduce the Lund Plane to Bloch (LP2B) encoding, designed to map a theoretically clean and robust representation of jet kinematics directly into qubit states. Leveraging this encoding, we implement a Quantum Tree-Topology Network (QTTN) that natively embeds the hierarchical structure of the Lund tree. We evaluate the QTTN across multiple benchmarks and observe that it matches the performance of large classical deep learning architectures, such as LundNet, on polarization tagging, while maintaining competitive accuracy for W boson and top quark tagging. The architecture demonstrates enhanced sensitivity compared to standard 1P1Q encodings on both polarization and W tagging, and pushes the Pareto front when compared against MLP of similar size and BDTs. Remarkably, the QTTN requires three orders of magnitude fewer parameters than LundNet, demonstrating promises for low-latency FPGA implementations in trigger systems. Furthermore, the QTTN outperforms classical methods in the low-data regime, making it suitable for low-yield, data-driven analyses. We also find that the quantum model is less susceptible to overfitting generator-specific parton shower and hadronization models than classical deep learning approaches, pointing toward potentially smaller systematic uncertainties. We validate the QTTN on real quantum hardware using a 3-qubit SpinQ device.

</details>


### [8] [Harmoniq: Efficient Data Augmentation on a Quantum Computer Inspired by Harmonic Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18691)
*Kristina Kirova,Monika Doerfler,Franz Luef,Richard Kueng*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: Harmoniq提出了一种超越变分范式的新型量子机器学习方法，利用量子调和分析的数据增强技术，通过随机混合n量子比特电路实现模块化量子数据处理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子机器学习方法大多基于变分范式，需要大量参数优化子程序。本研究旨在提出一种概念上不同的方法，超越变分范式限制。

Method: Harmoniq采用量子调和分析（quantum harmonic analysis）中的新型数据增强技术，将其近似为随机混合的n量子比特电路，每个电路深度最多为二次方。该方法具有模块化特性，可作为量子过程作用于密度矩阵。

Result: 案例研究表明，Harmoniq可与随机振幅编码（stochastic amplitude encoding）和量子主成分分析（quantum PCA）结合，构建信号去噪流程，在小样本情况下表现优异。

Conclusion: Harmoniq提供了一种超越传统变分方法的模块化量子机器学习框架，其模块化特性便于与其他量子数据处理和学习子程序结合，在小样本场景中展现出应用潜力。

Abstract: Quantum machine learning has attracted significant interest in recent years. Most existing approaches, however, are variational in nature and require extensive parameter optimization subroutines. Here, we propose a conceptually distinct quantum machine learning approach that goes beyond the variational paradigm. Harmoniq takes a novel data augmentation technique from quantum harmonic analysis and approximates it as a stochastic mixture of n-qubit circuits with (at most) quadratic depth each. A key strength of Harmoniq is its modularity: viewed as a quantum process acting on density matrices, it can readily be combined with other quantum data processing and learning subroutines. A subsequent case study demonstrates this modularity by combining Harmoniq with stochastic amplitude encoding for the input density matrix and quantum PCA on the output density matrix. This results in a promising signal denoising pipeline that works particularly well in the small sample size regime.

</details>


### [9] [Asymptotic Metrological Scaling and Concentration in Chaotic Floquet Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19017)
*Astrid J. M. Bergman,Yunxiang Liao,Jing Yang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了利用由Haar随机幺正门生成的Floquet混沌动力学进行量子传感。通过分析两种资源组织协议（控制协议和状态制备协议），发现量子费希尔信息在希尔伯特空间维度趋于无穷时呈现线性缩放，在非渐近区域则展现出超越线性的量子优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索利用Floquet混沌动力学进行量子传感的潜力，特别是分析由Haar随机幺正门生成的随机量子电路在量子计量学中的应用价值。

Method: 研究方法包括两种资源组织协议：控制协议（随机幺正门作为随机控制与确定性传感门交错作用）和状态制备协议（随机幺正门用于制备计量学有用状态）。每种协议分别考虑全局Haar随机幺正门和局部两位置Haar随机幺正门构成的Floquet随机量子电路。

Result: 主要结果包括：在希尔伯特空间维度趋于无穷的渐近极限下，量子费希尔信息呈现线性、散粒噪声缩放；在非渐近区域观察到超越线性缩放的量子优势；使用集中不等式限制了量子费希尔信息的涨落。数值模拟验证了分析结果。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，在局部希尔伯特空间维度趋于无穷的渐近极限下，Floquet随机量子电路的Floquet算符本质上表现得像全局幺正算符，这证实了关于随机量子电路的一个经验猜想。

Abstract: We study quantum sensing with Floquet chaotic dynamics generated by Haar random unitary gates. The metrological resources consist of three ingredients: A given initial state, a set number of Haar random unitary gates and the sensing gates. There are two natural ways of organizing the resources: the first one is the "control" protocol, where the random unitary gates act as random controls and intertwine with the deterministic sensing gates and the second one is the "state-preparation" protocol, where random unitary gates play the role of preparing the metrological useful states. In each protocol, we consider both global Haar random unitary gates and a set of local two-site Haar random unitary gates that forms a Floquet random quantum circuit (RQC) respectively. We find linear, shot-noise scaling of the metrological precision, quantified by the quantum Fisher information (QFI), in the asymptotic limit when the Hilbert space dimension becomes large, and quantum advantages beyond linear scaling in the non-asymptotic regimes. We also bound the fluctuation of the QFI using concentration inequalities. Our analytical findings are corroborated by numerical simulations. Finally, along the way of analyzing the precision limit, we prove an empirical conjecture of RQC: In the asymptotic limit of large local Hilbert space dimension, the Floquet operator of a Floquet RQC essentially behaves like a global unitary operator.

</details>


### [10] [Can classical theories of gravity produce entanglement?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19696)
*Anirudh Gundhi,Giorgia Infantino,Angelo Bassi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文反驳了Aziz和Howl在Nature上发表的关于经典引力相互作用产生量子纠缠的结论，指出其错误源于忽略了某些跃迁振幅，实际上经典引力不会在考虑的场景中产生纠缠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对Aziz和Howl在Nature期刊上声称经典引力相互作用能够产生量子纠缠的结论，本文旨在通过严谨分析揭示其论证中的缺陷，澄清经典引力与量子纠缠关系的误解。

Method: 通过重新分析Aziz和Howl论文中的跃迁振幅（transition amplitudes），指出他们错误地丢弃了某些振幅项，而这些项对于保持初始因子化状态（factorized state）的演化至关重要。

Result: 分析表明，当完整考虑所有跃迁振幅时，初始因子化状态随时间演化仍保持因子化，因此Aziz和Howl所声称的经典引力产生的纠缠（entanglement）实际上并不存在。

Conclusion: 在作者考虑的场景中，经典引力相互作用不会产生量子纠缠，Aziz和Howl的结论源于对跃迁振幅的不当处理，而非经典引力本身具有产生纠缠的能力。

Abstract: A recent paper published on Nature [Nature,646,813(2025)] by Aziz and Howl, claims that quantum particles become entangled when they interact gravitationally, even if the gravitational potential is treated classically. We show that the entanglement found by the authors stems from discarding some of the transition amplitudes, which, when kept, guarantee that an initially factorized state remains so over time. Therefore, no entanglement is generated by the classical gravitational interaction in the scenario considered by the authors.

</details>


### [11] [Classically Forbidden Signatures of Quantum Coherence in the Mesoscopic Lipkin-Meshkov-Glick Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18638)
*Stavros Mouslopoulos*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在自旋玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（spinor BEC）中建立了量子系统展现经典禁戒时间相关性的严格定量条件，通过Landau-Zener交叉和Leggett-Garg不等式违反两种量子判别预测，在N~370的介观尺度上验证了量子相干性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在为包含约370个自旋的集体量子系统建立严格的定量条件，以证明其展现出经典系统所禁止的时间相关性。这涉及在Lipkin-Meshkov-Glick（LMG）模型接近其Z_2破缺量子临界点时，探索介观叠加态在Goldilocks交叉区域（N ~ N_c）的量子特性。

Method: 采用Lipkin-Meshkov-Glick（LMG）模型分析接近Z_2破缺量子临界点的系统行为。通过两种量子判别方法：P4（Landau-Zener交叉）分析量子隧穿驱动的误差概率衰减，以及P5（Leggett-Garg不等式违反）进行模型无关的宏观实在性检验。使用五能级Lindblad模拟计算K_3值和退相干阈值。

Result: 研究建立了两个量子判别预测：P4显示量子隧穿使误差概率P_error指数衰减至零，而经典非遍历系统保持动力学冻结；P5得到K_3 ~ 1.32，违反Leggett-Garg不等式。在BEC目标参数下，退相干阈值γ_φ < 0.289 s^{-1}，比最优测量间隔高8.8倍，处于当前实验可达范围。涌现的集体Z_2对称性精确消除了主要退相干交叉项。

Conclusion: 该研究为自旋玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中的集体量子系统建立了严格的定量条件，证明其在介观尺度上能够展现经典禁戒的时间相关性。通过Landau-Zener交叉和Leggett-Garg不等式违反两种判别方法，验证了量子相干性的存在，且相关阈值在当前实验技术范围内可实现。所有结果可通过提供的自测试Python代码复现。

Abstract: We derive strict quantitative conditions under which a collective quantum system of N~370 spins exhibits classically forbidden temporal correlations in a spinor Bose-Einstein condensate (BEC). The Lipkin-Meshkov-Glick (LMG) model near its Z_2-breaking quantum critical point supports a mesoscopic superposition a|P> + b|R> of two macroscopic ordered phases (|P>: m_z ~ +m_*; |R>: m_z ~ -m_*) at the Goldilocks crossover N ~ N_c, where the tunnel splitting equals k_B T and macroscopic susceptibility chi ~ N coexists with finite quantum coherence. We establish two quantum-discriminating predictions. P4 (Landau-Zener crossover, proposed discriminator): quantum tunnelling drives P_error -> 0 exponentially with quench time, while the classically non-ergodic system remains kinetically frozen at P_error -> 1 - a parametrically large, computable separation that rests on a specific kinetic foil. P5 (Leggett--Garg inequality violation, strictly model-independent): K_3 > 1 is forbidden by macrorealism for all classical models satisfying non-invasive measurability. A five-level Lindblad simulation yields K_3 ~ 1.32 and dephasing threshold gamma_phi < 0.289 s^{-1} at the BEC target (gamma_phi = 0.05 s^{-1}, N = 370, Gamma/J = 0.95) - a margin of 8.8x above the optimal measurement interval, well within current experimental reach. The threshold has a precise physical origin in the emergent collective Z_2 symmetry: exact parity eliminates the dominant dephasing cross-term and renders the LGI correlator immune to T_1 population mixing without requiring ground-state preparation (2.35x improvement over the naive mean-field estimate); constructive dynamical phase alignment of higher odd-parity states at the benchmark parameters contributes a further 2.47x. All results are reproducible from the provided self-tested Python code.

### [12] [Synchronization in a dissipative quantum many-body system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18707)
*B. Çakmak,K. Sümer,S. Campbell,G. Karpat*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了XX量子比特链在局域或多局域振幅阻尼噪声下的同步现象，揭示了同步与退相干自由子空间（DFS）中单激发本征态数量的严格对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究XX量子比特链在振幅阻尼噪声下的同步行为，旨在理解噪声环境中的量子同步机制及其与退相干自由子空间结构的关系。

Method: 通过分析模型的退相干自由子空间（decoherence-free subspace, DFS）结构，该结构由噪声位点和链长相关的数论函数完全确定。推导了DFS中局域量子比特观测量（local qubit observables）的闭式表达式。

Result: 证明了边缘量子比特（edge qubits）对任意初始态稳定同步的充要条件是DFS恰好支持一个单激发本征态（single-excitation eigenstate）。该条件同时保证了边缘量子比特间的恒定渐近纠缠（constant asymptotic entanglement）。当DFS支持多个单激发本征态时，同步变为初始态依赖的且可能完全消失。

Conclusion: 稳定的量子同步与恒定渐近纠缠在DFS结构下必然共存，两者由DFS中单激发本征态的数量严格决定，揭示了量子同步与纠缠之间的深刻联系。

Abstract: We study synchronization in the XX qubit chain subject to local or multi-local amplitude-damping noise. Analyzing the decoherence-free subspace (DFS) structure of the model, we show that it is completely determined by a simple number-theoretic function involving the noise sites and the chain length. We derive a closed-form expression for local qubit observables restricted to the DFS and prove that stable synchronization of the edge qubits for arbitrary initial states occurs \textit{if and only if} the DFS supports exactly one single-excitation eigenstate. We further show that this same condition also guarantees constant asymptotic entanglement between the edge qubits, so that generic stable synchronization and constant asymptotic entanglement necessarily coexist. By contrast, when the DFS supports multiple single-excitation eigenstates, synchronization becomes initial state dependent and may be entirely absent, even though stable oscillatory entanglement can persist indefinitely.

### [13] [Quantum Decoherence of the Surface Code: A Generalized Caldeira-Leggett Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18968)
*E. Novais,A. H. Castro-Neto*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了主动纠错表面码（surface code）与连续量子环境耦合时的基本极限，揭示了仅在短程环境中存在严格的热力学阈值（thermodynamic threshold），而在临界或长程区域中，编码的宏观足迹会"武器化"连续环境，阻碍拓扑保护。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准量子纠错（quantum error correction, QEC）模型通常假设离散的马尔可夫噪声（Markovian noise），这掩盖了物理环境的连续量子本质。本研究旨在探索主动纠错表面码与连续、未重置的量子环境在零温和有限温度下耦合时的基本极限。

Method: 采用广义Caldeira-Leggett框架，将逻辑量子比特（logical qubit）的长时间演化映射到边界共形场论（boundary conformal field theory），建立了与各向异性近藤模型（anisotropic Kondo model）的精确等价性。针对有限编码距离L，评估了所有空间和时间相关性的计算时间。

Result: 分析表明，严格的热力学阈值仅存在于短程环境中（z>1/(s+1)）。在临界或长程区域中，编码的宏观足迹会"武器化"连续环境，从而阻碍拓扑保护。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了连续量子环境对量子纠错性能的基本限制，表明只有在特定条件下（短程环境）才存在真正的热力学阈值，而在更一般的环境中，拓扑保护会受到严重挑战。

Abstract: Standard quantum error correction (QEC) models typically assume discrete, Markovian noise, obscuring the continuous quantum nature of physical environments. In this manuscript, we investigate the fundamental limits of an actively corrected surface code coupled to a continuous, un-reset quantum environment at zero and finite temperature. Using the generalized Caldeira-Leggett framework, we map the long-time evolution of the logical qubit to a boundary conformal field theory, establishing an exact equivalence to the anisotropic Kondo model. We evaluate computational times for a finite code distance $L$ for all spatial and temporal correlations. Our analysis reveals that a true thermodynamic threshold exists strictly for short-range environments ($z>1/(s+1)$). In critical or long-range regimes, the macroscopic footprint of the code weaponizes the continuous bath, hindering the topological protection.

</details>


### [14] [Thermal-fluctuator driven decoherence of an oscillator resonantly coupled to a two-level system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19322)
*Thomas J. Antolin,Jonas Glatthard,Andrew D. Armour*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了热激活双能级涨落器（TLFs）如何通过与谐振双能级系统（TLS）的相互作用，导致量子振荡器相干性退化，为理解量子器件中的相干相互作用和退相干机制提供了理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验表明，相互作用的双能级系统（TLSs）在改变量子器件特性和产生涨落方面具有重要作用。研究旨在理解热激活双能级涨落器（TLFs）如何通过与谐振TLS的相互作用，导致量子振荡器相干性退化。

Method: 研究聚焦于振荡器与单个近谐振双能级系统（TLS）耦合的情况，分析TLS与低频热激活双能级涨落器（TLFs）之间的相互作用。通过数值计算，比较少数TLFs系统与大量（连续）TLF集合极限的差异。

Result: 单个TLF可产生相干振荡，伴随或取代振荡器-TLS系统的拉比振荡（Rabi oscillations）。浴驱动（bath-driven）的TLF跃迁导致不可逆相干衰减，其速率对耦合强度和跃迁速率高度敏感。对于TLF集合，研究识别并表征了振荡器可能表现出的不同非指数相位平均驱动相干衰减机制。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解超导和声子谐振器等量子器件中相干TLS相互作用与TLF诱导退相干（dephasing）之间的相互作用提供了理论框架，揭示了耦合强度和跃迁速率对相干衰减的重要影响。

Abstract: Recent experiments on a range of engineered quantum systems have highlighted the important role of interacting two-level systems (TLSs) in modifying device properties and generating fluctuations. Focusing on the case of an oscillator coupled to a single near-resonant TLS, we explore how interactions between the TLS and lower-frequency thermally activated two-level fluctuators (TLFs) degrade the oscillator's coherence. Depending on the strength of the couplings, a single TLF can give rise to coherence oscillations that appear alongside, or supplant, Rabi oscillations of the oscillator-TLS system. Bath-driven transitions in the TLF cause irreversible coherence decay at a rate that is highly sensitive to both the couplings and the transition rate. For an ensemble of TLFs, we identify and characterise the different regimes of non-exponential phase-averaging-driven coherence decay that the oscillator can display. Using numerical calculations, we examine the extent to which systems with just a few TLFs differ from the limit of a large (continuum) TLF ensemble. Our work provides a theoretical framework for understanding the interplay of coherent TLS interactions and TLF-induced dephasing in quantum devices such as superconducting and phononic resonators.

### [15] [Generating pairwise entanglement in periodically driven quantum spin chains with stochastic resetting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19333)
*Sinchan Ghosh,Manas Kulkarni,K. Sengupta,Satya N. Majumdar*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 随机重置（stochastic resetting）可在周期性驱动的自旋链稳态中产生有限的空间分离自旋对纠缠（pairwise entanglement），存在临界重置率$r_c$和最优重置率$r_m$，两者与驱动频率$ω_D$呈非单调关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究随机重置如何影响周期性驱动自旋链中的稳态纠缠特性，探索重置过程对空间分离自旋对纠缠的调控机制。

Method: 采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）方法计算可积XY模型（integrable XY model）和不可积里德堡自旋链（non-integrable Rydberg spin chains）中的并发度$C$，并在大驱动幅值区域使用微扰解析表达式进行验证。

Result: 发现存在临界重置率$r_c$，低于该值时稳态对纠缠消失；同时存在最优重置率$r_m$使并发度$C$达到最大值。这些临界和最优速率与驱动频率$ω_D$呈非单调依赖关系，并在特定驱动频率下$r_c$消失而$r_m$达到最小值。

Conclusion: 随机重置能够诱导周期性驱动自旋链中的稳态对纠缠，其特性由临界和最优重置率决定，这些参数与驱动频率存在复杂的非单调关系，为量子纠缠调控提供了新机制。

Abstract: We show that stochastic resetting may lead to finite entanglement between individual, spatially separated spins (pairwise entanglement) in the steady state of the spin chains driven periodically with frequency $ω_D$. We find the presence of a critical resetting rate $r_c$ below which the steady state pairwise entanglement, measured via concurrence $C$, vanishes. We also identify an optimal resetting rate $r_m$ at which $C$ becomes maximum. These critical and optimal rates exhibit a non-monotonic dependence on $ω_D$. Our analysis demonstrates the existence of special drive frequencies at which $r_c$ vanishes and $r_m$ attains minima. We compute $C$ in the presence of stochastic resetting using exact diagonalization for both the integrable XY model and non-integrable Rydberg spin chains, which demonstrate these features. Our numerical results match perturbative analytical expressions for the special drive frequencies in the large drive amplitude regime.

### [16] [Corneal deformation mapping and FE-based strain analysis via digital image correlation: biomechanical changes after CXL and laser refractive surgery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19289)
*Benedetta Fantaci,Alejandro Frechilla,Matteo Frigelli,Philippe Büchler,Sabine Kling,Begoña Calvo*

Main category: physics.med-ph

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种结合膨胀测试与三维数字图像相关技术（3D-DIC）的实验-计算集成方案，用于量化猪眼角膜在生理负荷下的全场应变分布，并识别其各向异性超弹性本构参数，从而评估不同治疗方式对角膜生物力学性能的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确评估角膜机械性能对于理解眼部生物力学、预测屈光手术结果以及优化角膜交联（CXL）治疗至关重要。传统的单轴拉伸测试受限于非生理边界条件和简化的应力分布，而膨胀测试虽能更真实地模拟体内应力状态，但传统上缺乏全场变形映射能力。

Method: 本研究提出了一种集成的实验-计算方案，将新鲜摘除猪眼的膨胀测试与高分辨率三维数字图像相关技术（3D-DIC）相结合。分析了三个组别的15个角膜：去上皮对照组、CXL处理组（标准德累斯顿方案）以及飞秒激光前基质消融组。样本承受高达40 mmHg的受控眼内压（IOP）升高。

Result: 3D-DIC方法提供了前表面密集的点位移和应变图，成功量化了CXL引起的局部硬化效应以及基质消融导致的顺应性增加。这些全场运动学数据被整合到膜理论有限元框架中，以解析主平面内应变，用于后续的逆建模以推导猪眼角膜组织的各向异性超弹性参数。

Conclusion: 该方法建立了从生理加载到全场应变映射再到本构参数识别的端到端路径，实现了对角膜治疗引起的生物力学变化的定量评估，为角膜生物力学研究提供了更精确的实验-计算集成框架。

Abstract: Accurate assessment of corneal mechanical properties is critical for understanding ocular biomechanics, predicting refractive surgery outcomes, and optimizing cross-linking (CXL) treatments. Conventional uniaxial tensile test is limited by non-physiological boundary conditions and simplified stress distributions. Inflation testing more closely reproduces the in vivo stress state but has traditionally lacked full-field deformation mapping. In this work, we present an integrated experimental-computational protocol combining inflation testing of freshly enucleated porcine eyes with high-resolution three-dimensional digital image correlation (3D-DIC). Fifteen corneas were analyzed across three cohorts: (i) de-epithelialized controls, (ii) CXL-treated (standard Dresden protocol), and (iii) anterior stromal ablation via femtosecond laser. Samples were subjected to controlled intraocular pressure (IOP) elevations up to 40 mmHg. The 3D-DIC approach provided dense, pointwise displacement and strain maps across the anterior surface, successfully quantifying the localized stiffening effects of CXL and the increased compliance induced by stromal ablation. These full-field kinematic data were integrated into a membrane-theory finite element framework to resolve principal in-plane strains, that were used for subsequent inverse modeling to derive anisotropic hyperelastic parameters of porcine corneal tissue. Overall, the method establishes an end-to-end route from physiologic loading to full-field strain mapping and constitutive parameter identification, enabling quantitative evaluation of treatment-induced biomechanical changes in the cornea.

### [17] [Charge Transport Capacity as a Probe of Resonances in Models of Many-Body Localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18710)
*Jessica Kaijia Jiang,Federica Maria Surace,Olexei I. Motrunich*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究通过引入电荷输运容量（CTC）这一新物理量，探讨了多体局域化（MBL）在热力学极限下的命运。研究发现，在数值可及的系统尺寸下，CTC随系统尺寸增长，这种增长源于电荷输运共振（CTRs）的出现，这解释了数值模拟中向热化漂移的现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体局域化（Many-Body Localization, MBL）在热力学极限下的命运尚不明确，部分原因是数值研究受到无法解释的有限尺寸效应的影响。需要新的物理量来理解这些有限尺寸效应及其对MBL相稳定性的影响。

Method: 研究引入了电荷输运容量（charge transport capacity, CTC）这一新物理量，它上限了一维晶格中通过中心截面的最大粒子输运数。通过数值研究相互作用安德森模型（interacting Anderson model），并采用微扰模型分析弱相互作用区域，探究电荷输运共振（charge transport resonances, CTRs）的微观起源。

Result: 在数值可及的系统尺寸下，无序平均的CTC虽小但随系统尺寸L增长，且增长速率在非常大的无序强度W下与W无关。这种增长源于随着L增加，能够输运更多电荷的多体共振（many-body resonances）变得更可能发生。CTRs对空间区域内的电荷构型敏感，该区域大小由共振范围而非W决定。

Conclusion: 短程多体共振随系统尺寸的不稳定增长导致了数值模拟中向热化的漂移。在足够强的无序下，平均乘积态只能输运O(1)的电荷。该研究为理解多体共振如何保持受控或最终破坏MBL相提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The fate of Many-Body Localization (MBL) in the thermodynamic limit remains elusive, partly because numerical studies suffer from unexplained finite-size effects. We introduce and numerically study the charge transport capacity (CTC) -- a quantity that upper bounds the number of particles that can ever be transported across a central cut of a 1D lattice. For ergodic systems, the CTC is linear with the system size $L$, while we expect it to be $O(1)$ for localized models. Surprisingly, in the interacting Anderson model for numerically accessible $L$, the disorder-averaged CTC is small, but grows with $L$ at an increasing rate. Moreover, this growth rate appears to be independent of the disorder strength $W$ at very large $W$. We find that, for these system sizes, this growth occurs because, as $L$ increases, many-body resonances that transport more charge across the cut become more likely. Using a perturbative model for the weakly interacting regime, we provide an understanding of the microscopic origins of the growth of these charge transport resonances (CTRs). We find that the CTRs are sensitive to charge configurations over a spatial region whose size is set by the range of the resonance, not by $W$, and that numerics cannot access system sizes where their behavior will converge. However, this effective model is consistent with a regime of strong disorder where, for large $L$, resonances are exponentially suppressed in their size. Finally, we study measures of average charge transport and suggest that for strong enough disorder, average product states can only transfer $O(1)$ charge. Our work suggests that the unsettled growth of short-ranged many-body resonances with $L$ contributes to the numerical drift towards thermalization at numerically accessible system sizes, and provides an understanding of how they can remain controlled or eventually destabilize the MBL phase.

</details>


### [18] [Daydreaming algorithm for Biased Patterns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19258)
*Mikiya Doi,Masayuki Ohzeki,Federico Ricci-Tersenghi*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文重新表述了Daydreaming算法以处理有偏模式（biased patterns），通过引入基于中心表示的检索动力学和能量函数，推导出中心化Daydreaming更新规则，相比中心化伪逆规则具有更大的吸引域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Daydreaming算法主要针对无偏模式（unbiased patterns），对有偏模式（biased patterns）的表述尚未充分建立。有偏模式在联想记忆模型中更具挑战性，需要专门处理。

Method: 基于伪逆规则（pseudo-inverse rule）的基本原理，重新表述Daydreaming算法以处理有偏模式。引入基于中心表示（centered representation）的检索动力学和能量函数，推导出相应的中心化Daydreaming（centered Daydreaming）更新规则。

Result: 中心化Daydreaming相比中心化伪逆规则（centered pseudo-inverse rule）产生更大的吸引域（basin of attraction）。两种方法虽然都旨在将存储模式稳定为固定点，但通过不同机制塑造能量景观（energy landscape）。

Conclusion: 研究成功建立了针对有偏模式的Daydreaming算法表述，证实了中心化Daydreaming在改善Hopfield模型存储容量方面的有效性，特别是通过不同机制优化能量景观。

Abstract: The \emph{Daydreaming} algorithm was proposed as a learning rule that simultaneously reinforces stored patterns and suppresses spurious attractors to improve the storage capacity of the Hopfield model. Its effectiveness has been reported for both uncorrelated and correlated data. However, the existing formulation has mainly assumed unbiased patterns, and the formulation for biased patterns has not yet been sufficiently established. Biased patterns are known to be much more problematic for models of associative memories. In this study, we reformulate Daydreaming for biased patterns by starting from the underlying rationale of the pseudo-inverse rule. Specifically, we introduce the retrieval dynamics and an energy function based on the centered representation, and we derive a corresponding update rule for centered Daydreaming. We compare the centered pseudo-inverse rule with centered Daydreaming for biased patterns and examine the retrieval maps and eigenvalue distributions of the coupling matrices. Our results confirm that centered Daydreaming yields a larger basin of attraction than the centered pseudo-inverse rule. Moreover, as in previous studies, although both approaches aim to stabilize the stored patterns as fixed points, our results suggest that they shape the energy landscape through different mechanisms.

</details>

### [19] [Generalized PT-symmetric nonlinear Dirac equation: exact solitary waves solutions, stability and conservation laws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19277)
*Fernando Carreño-Navas,Siannah Peñaranda,Renato Alvarez-Nodarse,Niurka R. Quintero*

Main category: nlin.PS

TL;DR: 本文推导了具有标量-标量相互作用的PT对称非线性狄拉克方程的精确孤波解，研究了幂律非线性项$|\barΨ\,Ψ|^{k}\,Ψ$下系统的守恒性质与稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究PT对称非线性狄拉克方程中精确孤波解的存在性及其性质，特别关注增益-损耗项对系统守恒律和稳定性的影响。

Method: 采用幂律非线性项$|\barΨ\,Ψ|^{k}\,Ψ$，推导了精确的孤立波解，并通过连续性方程获得定态解，分析了系统的能量、动量和电荷守恒性质。

Result: 发现系统能量守恒但电荷不守恒；PT相变点由解的存在条件定义且与非线性指数$k$无关；定态解在其静止参考系中具有非零动量，而运动孤子可通过选择速度实现零动量。

Conclusion: 增益-损耗机制和高阶非线性项共同限制了解的稳定性区域，揭示了PT对称非线性狄拉克系统中孤波解独特的守恒性质和运动特性。

Abstract: We derive an exact solitary wave solution for the $\PTb$-symmetric nonlinear Dirac equation with a scalar-scalar interaction. We consider a power-law nonlinearity of the form $|\barΨ\,Ψ|^{k}\,Ψ$ for positive values of $k$. 
The system's energy is conserved despite the presence of a gain-loss term, which is quantified by the parameter $Λ$. We show that the $\PTb$-transition point is defined by the solution's existence condition and is independent of the nonlinearity exponent $k$. Furthermore, momentum is conserved, although neither the canonical momentum nor the charge is a conserved quantity. A notable result is that the stationary solution, obtained from the continuity equations, exhibits nonzero momentum in its rest frame. We also derive a moving soliton solution, where the gain-loss parameter allows the soliton's velocity to be precisely chosen so that the moving soliton possesses zero momentum. Finally, we establish that the presence of a gain-loss mechanism and higher-order nonlinearity restrict the stability domain of the solutions.

</details>

### [20] [Estimating galactic foreground with the population of resolved galactic binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18992)
*Yang Jiang,Qing-Guo Huang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究分析了mHz频段随机引力波背景的探测挑战，特别关注银河系内致密双星系统产生的混淆前景噪声。通过分析双星系统的空间分布，推导了探测器响应的强度变化，并在Taiji Data Challenge II中测试了基于群体特性建模的前景噪声估计方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: mHz频段随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational wave background）是未来空间干涉仪的关键探测目标，但数据处理面临多重挑战。银河系内大量致密双星（compact binaries）在并合前阶段产生的引力波叠加形成了混淆前景噪声（confusion foreground），需要准确估计以探测随机背景信号。

Method: 通过分析双星系统的空间分布，推导了探测器对混淆前景噪声响应的强度变化。在Taiji Data Challenge II中，使用建模的前景噪声搜索注入的随机背景信号。该方法基于已解析银河系双星的群体特性（population properties）来描述前景噪声。

Result: 在关于前景噪声统计特性的某些假设下，结果显示基于已解析银河系双星群体特性描述前景噪声的方法能够产生初步可行的结果。该方法为mHz频段随机引力波背景探测提供了有效的前景噪声建模途径。

Conclusion: 研究证实了基于双星系统空间分布和群体特性建模混淆前景噪声的可行性，为未来空间引力波探测器处理mHz频段随机背景信号提供了重要参考。该方法能够有效处理银河系致密双星系统产生的混淆噪声挑战。

Abstract: The stochastic gravitational wave background in the mHz band is a key target for future spaceborne interferometers. Detecting such a signal presents multiple challenges for data processing, especially complicated by the presence of numerous compact binaries in our galaxy. The superposition of gravitational waves from their inspiral stages creates a confusion foreground that need to be estimated accurately. In this work, we derive the variation in the intensity of detector response to this foreground by analyzing the spatial distribution of binary systems. Subsequently, we search for an injected stochastic background using the modeled foreground within Taiji Data Challenge II. With some assumptions about the statistical properties of foreground, the results show that the approach of describing foreground based on the population properties of resolved Galactic binaries can yield preliminary feasible results.

### [21] [A practical theorem on gravitational-wave background statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19701)
*Yacine Ali-Haïmoud*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究推导了超大质量黑洞双星系统产生的纳赫兹引力波背景特征应变平方的概率分布函数，在源数量大但有限的情况下，该分布呈现普适的自相似形式，由反射的map-Airy分布描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旋近的超大质量黑洞双星（SMBHBs）是脉冲星计时阵列（PTAs）探测的纳赫兹引力波背景（GWB）主要来源。需要理解GWB特征应变平方的概率分布特性，特别是在PTAs最敏感的低频波段，当有效源数量大但有限时的统计行为。

Method: 推导了在有效源数量N远大于1的极限下，重标度变量y≡h_c^2/¯h_c^2的概率分布函数（PDF）的普适解析表达式。该方法基于新的统计量——立方散粒噪声应变尺度¯h_0^3，该统计量仅依赖于SMBHB群体的局部特性。

Result: 发现PDF呈现普适的自相似形式：P(y)≃N^{1/3}𝒫(N^{1/3}(y-1))，其中𝒫为反射的map-Airy分布。这一结果具有普适性，适用于任何SMBHB群体，无论其轨道是圆形还是偏心，也不受主导轨道硬化机制的影响。

Conclusion: 该解析表达式为PTA数据分析提供了实用工具，通过有效源数量N、平均特征应变平方¯h_c^2和立方散粒噪声应变尺度¯h_0^3三个参数，即可完全描述GWB的统计特性，简化了引力波背景的统计推断过程。

Abstract: Inspiralling supermassive black-hole binaries (SMBHBs) are expected to be the main source of the nanohertz gravitational-wave background (GWB) targeted by pulsar timing arrays (PTAs). We provide a simple and general analytic expression for the probability distribution function (PDF) of the GWB characteristic strain squared $h_c^2$ in the limit of a large but finite effective number of sources, $N$, relevant for the lowest-frequency bands where PTAs are most sensitive. Explicitly, we show that for $N \gg 1$, the PDF of the rescaled variable $y \equiv h_c^2/\overline{h_c^2}$ takes the universal self-similar form $P(y) \simeq N^{1/3} \mathcal{P}(N^{1/3} (y -1))$, where $\mathcal{P}$ is the reflected map-Airy distribution. The effective number of in-band sources $N$ is fully specified by the mean $\overline{h_c^2}$ and the cubic shot-noise strain scale $\overline{h_0^3}$, a new summary statistic of the GWB that depends only on the local properties of the SMBHB population. This result is universal: it applies to any population of SMBHBs, regardless of whether they are circular or eccentric, and of the mechanism dominating orbital hardening. We explicitly quantify the accuracy of the large-source-count PDF for a simple but physically realistic SMBHB model, and outline its practical application to PTA data analysis.

</details>

### [22] [AI scientists produce results without reasoning scientifically](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18805)
*Martiño Ríos-García,Nawaf Alampara,Chandan Gupta,Indrajeet Mandal,Sajid Mannan,Ali Asghar Aghajani,N. M. Anoop Krishnan,Kevin Maik Jablonka*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究评估了基于大语言模型（LLM）的自主科研代理，发现其虽然能执行科学工作流，但缺乏科学推理应有的认识论模式，证据常被忽视且信念修正不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着基于大语言模型（LLM）的系统越来越多地用于自主科学研究，但其推理过程是否遵循使科学探究具备自我修正能力的认识论规范尚不清楚。需要评估这些代理是否真正具备科学推理所需的认知结构。

Method: 研究通过超过25,000次代理运行，在八个领域评估LLM-based科学代理，采用两种互补视角：系统性性能分析（分解基础模型和代理框架的贡献）以及代理推理认识论结构的行为分析。

Result: 基础模型是性能和行为的首要决定因素（解释方差占比41.4% vs. 框架的1.5%）。68%的追踪中证据被忽视，仅有26%出现反驳驱动的信念修正，收敛性多测试证据罕见。这些模式在计算工作流执行和假设驱动探究中均存在。

Conclusion: 当前基于LLM的代理能执行科学工作流，但未展现科学推理的特征性认识论模式。仅基于结果的评估无法检测这些失败，仅靠框架工程也无法修复。在推理本身成为训练目标之前，此类代理产生的科学知识无法通过其生成过程获得正当性。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based systems are increasingly deployed to conduct scientific research autonomously, yet whether their reasoning adheres to the epistemic norms that make scientific inquiry self-correcting is poorly understood. Here, we evaluate LLM-based scientific agents across eight domains, spanning workflow execution to hypothesis-driven inquiry, through more than 25,000 agent runs and two complementary lenses: (i) a systematic performance analysis that decomposes the contributions of the base model and the agent scaffold, and (ii) a behavioral analysis of the epistemological structure of agent reasoning. We observe that the base model is the primary determinant of both performance and behavior, accounting for 41.4% of explained variance versus 1.5% for the scaffold. Across all configurations, evidence is ignored in 68% of traces, refutation-driven belief revision occurs in 26%, and convergent multi-test evidence is rare. The same reasoning pattern appears whether the agent executes a computational workflow or conducts hypothesis-driven inquiry. They persist even when agents receive near-complete successful reasoning trajectories as context, and the resulting unreliability compounds across repeated trials in epistemically demanding domains. Thus, current LLM-based agents execute scientific workflows but do not exhibit the epistemic patterns that characterize scientific reasoning. Outcome-based evaluation cannot detect these failures, and scaffold engineering alone cannot repair them. Until reasoning itself becomes a training target, the scientific knowledge produced by such agents cannot be justified by the process that generated it.

</details>

### [23] [Gibbs Equivalence and SRB Measures for Axiom A Diffeomorphisms: Transfer Operators, Structural Stability, and Physical Measures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18929)
*Abdoulaye Thiam*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文为六部曲系列的第四部分，针对Axiom A微分同胚建立了Ruelle转移算子理论，构造了Sinai-Ruelle-Bowen测度，并将第一部分的符号谱结果通过第三部分的Markov分割编码推广到光滑动力学中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用Markov分割编码将符号谱结果转移到光滑动力学；在Hölder空间上分析转移算子的拟紧性；通过几何势构造SRB测度作为唯一平衡态；应用Nagaev-Guivarc'h谱扰动方法。

Result: 证明了四个主要定理：Axiom A微分同胚的结构稳定性；转移算子的拟紧性与谱间隙；SRB测度的构造与不稳定叶层的绝对连续性；Pesin熵公式的建立。

Conclusion: 通过四个主要定理与第一、三部分的结果，建立了混合基本集上平衡态的符号、变分、谱和几何特征之间的等价关系，形成了完整的定量表述。

Abstract: We develop the Ruelle transfer operator theory for Axiom A diffeomorphisms and construct Sinai-Ruelle-Bowen measures, carrying the symbolic spectral results of Part I over to smooth dynamics through the Markov partition coding established in Part III. This paper contains four Main Theorems. The first proves structural stability of Axiom A diffeomorphisms satisfying the strong transversality condition, with an explicit Hölder exponent for the conjugating homeomorphism computed in terms of the hyperbolicity data, refining the classical results of Robbin and Robinson. The second establishes quasi-compactness of the transfer operator on Hölder spaces, with a quantitative spectral gap bound; as consequences we obtain exponential decay of correlations with explicit rate, the central limit theorem for Hölder observables via the Nagaev-Guivarc'h spectral perturbation method, real-analyticity of the pressure in the potential direction, and meromorphic continuation of the Ruelle dynamical zeta function. The third constructs SRB measures on mixing basic sets as the unique equilibrium states for the geometric potential given by minus the logarithm of the unstable Jacobian, proves absolute continuity of the unstable foliation, and derives an explicit product-formula for the conditional densities along unstable manifolds. The fourth establishes the Pesin entropy formula identifying the Kolmogorov-Sinai entropy of the SRB measure with the sum of its positive Lyapunov exponents. The Gibbs Equivalence Theorem, assembling the symbolic, variational, spectral, and geometric characterizations of the equilibrium state on a mixing basic set into a single quantitative statement, follows from these four Main Theorems together with the imported results of Parts I and III. This paper constitutes Part IV of a six-part series on the thermodynamic formalism for hyperbolic dynamical systems.

### [24] [Statistical Limit Theorems for Axiom A Diffeomorphisms: Mixing, Central Limit Theorem, and Large Deviations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18930)
*Abdoulaye Thiam*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 该论文基于Ruelle转移算子的谱间隙，为Axiom A微分同胚的平衡态建立了统计极限定理，包含五个主要结果：体积引理、指数衰减相关性、中心极限定理、几乎必然不变原理和大偏差原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在从单一谱机制推导双曲动力系统的统计极限定理，明确展示结果对双曲性数据的依赖关系，从而统一先前由多位学者独立证明的相关定理。

Method: 方法基于Ruelle转移算子（Ruelle transfer operator）的谱间隙性质，利用双曲动力系统的热力学形式体系（thermodynamic formalism），通过显式依赖双曲性数据（hyperbolicity data）的谱分析机制推导统计极限定理。

Result: 论文建立了五个主要结果：1) 具有明确双边界的体积引理（Volume Lemma）；2) 具有显式混合率的指数衰减相关性；3) 具有最优速率Berry-Esseen界的中心极限定理（Central Limit Theorem）；4) 具有多项式误差的几乎必然不变原理（Almost Sure Invariance Principle）；5) 由压力Legendre变换给出的速率函数的大偏差原理（large deviations principle）。

Conclusion: 该研究从单一谱机制统一推导了双曲动力系统平衡态的统计极限定理，明确展示了结果对双曲性数据的依赖关系，构成了关于双曲动力系统热力学形式体系的六部分系列研究的第五部分。

Abstract: We establish statistical limit theorems for equilibrium states of Axiom A diffeomorphisms, derived from the spectral gap of the Ruelle transfer operator. This paper contains five main results. The first proves the Volume Lemma with explicit two-sided bounds on the Riemannian volume of dynamical Bowen balls. The second establishes exponential decay of correlations with explicit mixing rates. The third proves the Central Limit Theorem with Berry-Esseen bounds at the optimal rate, with an explicit spectral formula for the asymptotic variance and a characterization of its degeneracy through the Livshits coboundary condition. The fourth establishes the Almost Sure Invariance Principle, providing pathwise Brownian approximation with polynomial error. The fifth proves a large deviations principle with rate function given by the Legendre transform of the pressure. The individual results are due to Sinai, Ruelle, Ratner, Denker-Philipp, Gouezel, Kifer, Melbourne-Nicol, and Young; the contribution is their derivation from a single spectral mechanism with explicit dependence on hyperbolicity data. This constitutes Part V of a six-part series on the thermodynamic formalism for hyperbolic dynamical systems.

### [25] [Rigidity, Fluctuations, and Multifractal Structure of Axiom A Systems: SRB Measures, Livshits Rigidity, and Fluctuation Theorems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18931)
*Abdoulaye Thiam*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文作为双曲动力系统热力学形式主义六部曲的终篇，发展了Axiom A微分同胚热力学形式主义的四个核心结构结果：Pesin熵公式、多重分形形式主义、Livshits定理和Gallavotti-Cohen涨落定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在系统发展Axiom A微分同胚（Axiom A diffeomorphisms）热力学形式主义（thermodynamic formalism）的结构性推论，作为双曲动力系统（hyperbolic dynamical systems）热力学形式主义系列研究的最终部分。

Method: 采用热力学形式主义框架，结合动力系统理论方法，包括SRB测度（SRB measure）、李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponents）、豪斯多夫维数（Hausdorff dimension）和勒让德变换（Legendre transform）等工具。

Result: 获得四个主要结果：Pesin熵公式建立了SRB测度的度量熵与正李雅普诺夫指数和的等式；多重分形形式主义通过压力的勒让德变换计算Birkhoff平均水平集的豪斯多夫维数；Livshits定理通过周期轨道数据刻画上同调；Gallavotti-Cohen涨落定理建立了熵产生率相反值处速率函数的线性对称性。

Conclusion: 本文完成了双曲动力系统热力学形式主义的系统研究，为Axiom A微分同胚提供了完整的结构理论框架，包含熵公式、多重分形分析、上同调刻画和涨落对称性等核心结果。

Abstract: This paper develops structural consequences of the thermodynamic formalism for Axiom A diffeomorphisms, with four main results. The Pesin Entropy Formula equates the metric entropy of the SRB measure to the sum of positive Lyapunov exponents, with complete proofs of absolute continuity of conditional measures along unstable manifolds. The Multifractal Formalism computes the Hausdorff dimension of Birkhoff average level sets via the Legendre transform of the pressure, extending earlier work of Barreira, Pesin, and Schmeling. The Livshits Theorem characterizes coboundaries through periodic orbit data with optimal Holder regularity and an explicit norm bound in terms of the contraction rate and the Holder exponent. The Gallavotti-Cohen Fluctuation Theorem establishes the linear symmetry relating the rate function at opposite values of the entropy production rate, with explicit bounds from the spectral gap. This constitutes Part VI, the final installment, of a six-part series on the thermodynamic formalism for hyperbolic dynamical systems.

</details>

### [26] [Tree Amplitudes with Charged Matter in Pure Gauge Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18672)
*Jacob L. Bourjaily,Michael Plesser,Philip Velie*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 开发了一个名为`fermionic_amplitudes.m`的Mathematica软件包，用于计算纯（非超对称）规范理论中任意数量规范玻色子和任意电荷无质量费米子的树级振幅。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要计算涉及任意数量规范玻色子和任意电荷无质量费米子的树级振幅，这些费米子可能具有不同味道（flavours）。该软件包旨在为纯（非超对称）规范理论提供此类计算工具。

Method: 通过将不同味道的部分振幅（partial amplitudes）表示为仅涉及单一味道振幅的线性组合来实现。这些单一味道振幅可作为（最大）超对称杨-米尔斯理论（supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory）的分量振幅进行计算。所有相关色张量（colour tensors）可实现为显式的数值数组。

Result: 成功实现了`fermionic_amplitudes.m`软件包，能够计算任意规范理论（包括$u_1$）中涉及任意电荷生成元（charge generators）的树级振幅。所有与截面计算相关的色收缩（colour contractions）均可方便计算。

Conclusion: 该软件包为计算纯规范理论中涉及任意费米子味道和规范玻色子的树级振幅提供了有效工具，相关代码和使用演示已作为arXiv提交的辅助文件提供。

Abstract: We describe the implementation and usage of `fermionic_amplitudes.m', a Mathematica package for the computation of tree amplitudes involving arbitrary numbers of gauge bosons and arbitrarily-charged massless fermions of (possibly) distinct flavours in pure (non-supersymmetric) gauge theory. These are given in terms of a basis of partial amplitudes involving distinct-flavoured fermions dressed by specific colour tensors. Distinct-flavour partial amplitudes are expressed as linear combinations of those involving only a single flavour, which may be evaluated as component amplitudes of (maximally) supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory. All relevant colour tensors can be realized as explicit, numeric arrays given any choice of charge generators (for any gauge theory -- including $u_1$); from these, all colour contractions relevant to cross sections may be readily computed.
  The complete package and a notebook demonstrating its primary usage and functionality are included in this work's submission's ancillary files on the arXiv.

</details>


### [27] [Neural Networks Reveal a Universal Bias in Conformal Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18673)

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出使用在交叉对称性（crossing symmetry）上训练的简单神经网络（NNs）能够高精度重建限制在一条线上的共形关联函数（conformal correlators）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索一种新的计算框架来重构共形场论（conformal field theory）中的关联函数，这为研究非微扰量子场论（non-perturbative quantum field theory）提供了新途径。

Method: 方法基于在交叉对称性上训练的简单神经网络，输入仅需外部标度维度（external scaling dimension）、谱隙（spectral gap）以及关联函数在单点的值。该方法适用于多种共形理论和维度，包括四点函数和热两点函数。

Result: 结果显示神经网络能够以显著精度重建共形关联函数。这种成功归因于基于梯度的神经网络训练中的谱偏置（spectral bias），该偏置与共形场论的内在平滑性（intrinsic smoothness）特性相吻合。

Conclusion: 结论表明这为共形关联函数提出了一种新的变分原理（variational principle），并为非微扰量子场论开辟了强大的新计算框架路径。

Abstract: We propose that simple neural networks (NNs) trained on crossing symmetry can reconstruct conformal correlators restricted to a line to remarkable accuracy. The input is minimal: an external scaling dimension, a spectral gap, and the value of the correlator at a single point. We present evidence across a wide range of conformal theories and dimensions, for both four-point and thermal two-point functions. We attribute these observations to the spectral bias of gradient-based NN training, which appears to align with an intrinsic smoothness property of conformal field theory. This suggests a novel variational principle for conformal correlators and opens a path towards a powerful new computational framework for non-perturbative quantum field theory.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 成功将流体动力学自由度嵌入到模型的微观描述中，计算了流体动力学有效作用量（hydrodynamic effective action）的高阶导数展开项，并确定了所有相应的输运系数（transport coefficients）。

Conclusion: 该工作首次从强耦合量子多体系统的微观描述中推导出流体动力学，建立了SYK晶格模型与波动流体动力学有效场论之间的直接对应关系。

Abstract: The SYK model has played an important role in recent developments in many-body quantum chaos. We study a spatially local generalisation of it: the SYK lattice. Starting from the nonlinear action of pseudo-Goldstone bosons that dominate its dynamics at low temperatures, in the long wavelength limit we reorganise this action as the effective field theory for fluctuating hydrodynamics, thereby showing how the hydrodynamic degrees of freedom embed into the microscopic description of the model. We compute the hydrodynamic effective action to high orders in the derivative expansion and determine all the corresponding transport coefficients. Hence this work derives hydrodynamics from the microscopic description of a strongly coupled quantum many-body system.

### [29] [The perturbative Ricci flow in gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18678)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在建立引力中里奇流的微扰表述，借鉴量子色动力学（QCD）中梯度流（gradient flow）的方法，为引力理论发展基于几何流的重整化方案。

Method: 采用与QCD梯度流类似的步骤，在通常的引力微扰费曼规则基础上补充了流传播子（flowed propagators）、流顶点（flowed vertices）以及描述引力沿里奇流演化的引力子流线（graviton flow lines）。

Result: 通过计算多个独立算符在双圈水平的真空期望值，推导了流动作作用量所需的抵消项（counterterms），建立了基于里奇流的牛顿常数重整化方案，并发现了与已知非微扰考虑一致的非高斯固定点（non-Gaußian fixed point）。

Conclusion: 本文成功发展了引力中里奇流的微扰表述，为牛顿常数定义了基于里奇流的重整化方案，其重整化群行为揭示了与渐近安全引力理论一致的非高斯固定点。

Abstract: We develop a perturbative formulation of the Ricci flow in gravity. Following steps analogous to the gradient flow in QCD, we supplement the usual Feynman rules for perturbative gravity by flowed propagators and vertices as well as graviton flow lines which describe the evolution of gravity along the Ricci flow. By calculating vacuum expectation values of a number of independent operators at the two-loop level, we derive the required counterterms of the flowed action. Our results allow us to define a Ricci-flow based renormalization scheme for Newton's constant $G_N$. Studying its renormalization group behavior, we recover a non-Gaußian fixed point in accordance with well-known non-perturbative considerations

### [30] [Mapping Tachyon effective field theory to a subsector of Klein-Gordon theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18679)
*P. V. Athira,Ashik H,Priyadarshi Paul*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过集体场论方法将不稳定D膜（D-brane）附近的有效场论映射到一致的量子描述，发现量子希尔伯特空间由静止粒子的相干态及其激发组成，这对应于克莱因-戈登理论的一个子空间，并表明在量子水平上开放弦与闭合弦描述之间存在等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不稳定D膜上快子（tachyon）从势能最大值滚动的动力学由弦论中的时间依赖解描述，后续分析通过有效场论理解快子真空附近的物理。经典解在晚期极限下与非旋转、非相互作用的尘埃粒子构型一一对应。

Method: 使用集体场论方法（collective field theory methods）将势能最小值附近的有效理论映射到一致的量子描述，从而获得希尔伯特空间描述。

Result: 获得的希尔伯特空间描述由静止粒子的相干态（coherent state）及其激发组成，即克莱因-戈登理论（Klein-Gordon theory）的一个子空间。这与已知结果一致：衰变D膜作为闭合弦的时间依赖源，产生的最终闭合弦态是相干态。

Conclusion: 在量子水平上，不稳定D膜衰变的开放弦描述与闭合弦描述之间存在等价性，集体场论方法为理解快子真空附近的量子物理提供了有效框架。

Abstract: On an unstable D-brane, the rolling of the tachyon away from the maximum of its potential is described by time-dependent solutions in string theory. Subsequent analysis leads to an understanding of physics around the tachyon vacuum in terms of an effective field theory. The classical solutions of this effective field theory in the late time limit are in one-to-one correspondence with configurations of non-rotating, non-interacting dust particles. In this work, we map this effective theory near the minimum of the potential to a consistent quantum description using collective field theory methods. The Hilbert space description we obtain in this way consists of a coherent state of particles at rest and excitations on top, i.e., a subsector of Klein-Gordon theory. This is in accordance with known results where one considers a decaying D-brane as providing a time-dependent source for closed strings, and the final closed string state produced is a coherent state. It also suggests, at the quantum level, an equivalence between the open string description and the closed string description regarding the decay of an unstable D-brane.

### [31] [Neural Spectral Bias and Conformal Correlators I: Introduction and Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18686)
*Kausik Ghosh,Sidhaarth Kumar,Vasilis Niarchos,Andreas Stergiou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究证明简单前馈神经网络（feed-forward neural networks）仅需交叉对称性（crossing symmetry）、主导非平庸算符的标度维度（scaling dimension）及单个"锚点"（anchor point）相关函数值，即可在多个维度精确重建共形场论（conformal field theories）的相关函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索神经网络与共形场论之间的深层联系，特别是如何利用神经网络基于极少量数据重建物理相关函数。研究旨在理解神经网络为何能有效捕捉共形场论的结构特性。

Method: 通过优化神经网络仅满足交叉对称性约束，输入主导非平庸算符的标度维度和单个锚点处的相关函数值。使用分数索博列夫半范数（fractional Sobolev semi-norms）、切比雪夫谱分解（Chebyshev spectral decompositions）和曲率度量分析共形相关函数的平滑性。

Result: 该方法在广泛的理论和维度中表现出鲁棒性，包括广义自由场、AdS₂中的接触和一环维腾图（Witten diagrams）、二维最小模型（minimal models）、三维伊辛模型（3d Ising model）和4d $\mathcal{N}=4$超杨-米尔斯理论（super-Yang-Mills theory）的半BPS相关函数，重建误差在几个百分点内。

Conclusion: 神经网络与共形场论之间的显著对齐源于基于梯度的训练的光谱偏置（spectral bias），该偏置强烈偏好平滑函数。该技术通过扩展到线对角运动学之外，展现了更广泛的重建能力。

Abstract: We demonstrate that simple feed-forward neural networks (NNs) can accurately compute correlation functions of conformal field theories (CFTs) on a line. Strikingly, by optimising a NN solely on crossing symmetry and providing only the scaling dimension of the leading non-trivial operator and the correlator's value at a single "anchor point", we can reconstruct target physical correlators to within a few percent. We establish the robustness of this minimal-data approach across a broad class of theories and dimensions, including generalised free fields, contact and one-loop Witten diagrams in AdS$_2$, unitary and non-unitary 2d minimal models, the 3d Ising model, and half-BPS correlators in 4d $\mathcal{N}=4$ super-Yang-Mills theory, together with several thermal two-point functions, notably including those of the 3d Ising model. We argue that this remarkable alignment between NNs and CFTs stems from the spectral bias of gradient-based training, which heavily favours smooth functions. To ground this connection, we analyse the smoothness of conformal correlators using fractional Sobolev semi-norms, Chebyshev spectral decompositions, and a measure based on curvature. Finally, we establish the broader reconstructive power of this technique by extending it beyond the diagonal kinematics of the line.

</details>


### [32] [Non-supersymmetric heterotic strings on $AdS_{4}\times S^{3}\times S^{3}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18692)
*Ivano Basile,Daniel Robbins,Hassaan Saleem*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文分析了十维无超对称异弦理论中一类反德西特（anti-de Sitter）通量紧致化的稳定性特性。与简单解不同，这些解包含两个独立无界通量，导致更丰富的失稳现象，包括微扰谱中的快子模（tachyonic modes）和非微扰的膜成核（brane nucleation）失稳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析无超对称异弦理论中具有两个独立无界通量的反德西特通量紧致化的稳定性特性。与简单解相比，这种更复杂的通量配置可能导致更丰富的失稳现象，需要系统研究其稳定性行为。

Method: 研究方法包括分析十维无超对称异弦理论中一类反德西特通量紧致化解。特别关注包含两个独立无界通量的配置，并采用轨道折叠（orbifold）作用来投影掉某些模式。通过分析微扰谱和非微扰效应来研究稳定性。

Result: 研究结果显示：当两个通量大小足够接近时，微扰谱会发展出快子模，这些模可通过轨道折叠作用投影掉。当通量差异较大时，快子模消失，几何呈现逆尺度分离（inverse scale separation），即内部流形因子参数化地大于反德西特因子。然而，膜成核形式的非微扰失稳始终存在。

Conclusion: 结论表明，这类反德西特通量紧致化总是存在非微扰失稳通道，特别是膜成核过程。这些失稳倾向于使两个通量相互靠近，当存在快子模时最终触发快子失稳。即使在没有快子模的情况下，非微扰失稳仍然存在。

Abstract: We analyze the stability properties of a family of anti-de Sitter flux compactifications of the tachyon-free non-supersymmetric heterotic string in ten dimensions. In contrast with simpler such solutions, the solutions include two independent unbounded fluxes, leading to richer instability phenomena. In particular, when the two fluxes are sufficiently close in magnitude, the perturbative spectrum develops tachyonic modes, which can be projected out by an orbifold action. When the fluxes are far apart, tachyonic modes are absent, and the geometry displays inverse scale separation, where a factor of the internal manifold becomes parametrically larger than the anti-de Sitter factor. Still, non-perturbative instabilities in the form of brane nucleation are always available decay channels, and tend to drive the two fluxes closer together, eventually triggering the tachyonic instability when present.

### [33] [Confinement in a finite duality cascade](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18702)
*Fabrizio Aramini,Riccardo Argurio,Matteo Bertolini,Pietro Moroni,Valdo Tatitscheff*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过全息对偶（holographic duality）研究了一个四维N=1超对称规范理论的禁闭动力学，验证了Wilson loop的面积律、畴壁（domain wall）的场论描述以及轴子弦（axionic strings）的不稳定性，确认了该理论从UV的共形流形流向IR的完全能隙真空。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在验证最近提出的一个四维N=1超对称规范理论全息对偶中的禁闭动力学一致性。该理论从紫外（UV）的共形流形（conformal manifold）流向红外（IR）的完全能隙（fully gapped）孤立真空。

Method: 通过在锥形奇点（conifold singularity）处考虑带有O7-膜（O7-plane）的D3-膜（D3-branes），构建了所有超引力场都具有非平凡背景的全息对偶。计算了基本表示中Wilson loop的期望值，并构造了畴壁作为包裹内部流形紧致三环（compact three-cycle）的D5-膜。

Result: Wilson loop的期望值遵循面积律（area law），证实了禁闭行为。畴壁动力学由(2+1)维N=1 Yang-Mills-Chern-Simons理论描述，在深红外（deep infrared）约化为拓扑量子场论（TQFT），其流入作用（inflow action）正确再现了四维理论的混合反常（mixed anomaly）。轴子弦在该背景下不稳定，表明不存在相应的无质量轴子（massless axion）。

Conclusion: 该全息模型成功验证了禁闭动力学的多个一致性条件：Wilson loop的面积律、畴壁的场论描述与混合反常匹配、以及轴子弦的不稳定性与完全能隙真空的一致性。这些结果为该四维N=1超对称规范理论的全息对偶提供了有力支持。

Abstract: We provide several consistency checks of confining dynamics in a recently conjectured holographic dual of a four-dimensional ${\cal N}=1$ supersymmetric gauge theory that flows from a conformal manifold in the UV to a finite set of isolated, fully gapped vacua in the IR. This is obtained by considering D3-branes at the conifold singularity in the presence of an O7-plane, leading to a background where all supergravity fields have a non-trivial profile. We compute holographically the expectation value of a Wilson loop in the fundamental representation and show that it obeys an area law. We then construct the domain walls which interpolate between different vacua in terms of D5-branes wrapping a compact three-cycle of the internal manifold. Their dynamics is governed by the (2+1)-dimensional ${\cal N}=1$ Yang-Mills-Chern-Simons theory predicted by field theory arguments, that reduces in the deep infrared to a TQFT whose inflow action correctly reproduces the mixed anomaly of the four-dimensional theory. Finally, we argue that, unlike in previous models in the literature, axionic strings are unstable in this background. This implies that the corresponding massless axion that would couple to them is absent, in agreement with the fact that the vacua are fully gapped.

</details>


### [34] [Gauging in superconductors and other electronic systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18733)
*Marcus Berg,Andrea Cappelli,Riccardo Villa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出s波超导体（s-wave superconductors）本质上是拓扑相（topological phases），其规范场（gauge field）需为spin_c联络（spin_c connection），并具有引力-磁异常（gravito-magnetic anomaly），这源于其费米子起源（fermionic origin）且与Gaiotto-Kapustin-Thorngren玻色化（bosonization）相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统s波超导体已被识别为拓扑相，但其规范场所蕴含的全局特征尚未被充分理解。研究旨在利用拓扑场论（topological field theories）和广义对称性（generalized symmetries）工具，提供对这些系统的更新描述。

Method: 采用拓扑场论和广义对称性框架进行分析。在极低能标下，希格斯模型（Higgs model）约化为BF理论（BF theory），该理论展现拓扑序（topological order）。规范场必须为spin_c联络以描述形成库珀对（Cooper pairs）的费米子自旋。

Result: 超导体本质上是玻色系统，但具有引力-磁异常，这是其费米子起源的残余。该异常与通过规范费米子宇称（fermion parity）$(-1)^F$实现的Gaiotto-Kapustin-Thorngren玻色化相关。此异常在三维和四维时空（spacetime dimensions）中普遍禁止低能下的平凡有质量相（trivial massive phases）。

Conclusion: 该异常特征超越了希格斯模型的有效性范围，也适用于其他类型的超导体。它同样出现在最近被理解的三维电动力学（three-dimensional electrodynamics）的非平凡无质量相（nontrivial massless phase）中。

Abstract: Ordinary, s-wave superconductors have been recognized as being topological phases of matter, in which the dynamical gauge field implies less understood global features. Using the tools of topological field theories and generalized symmetries, we provide an updated description of these systems. At very low energies, the Higgs model reduces to the BF theory, which exhibits topological order. Furthermore, the gauge field must be a spin$_c$ connection, to describe the spin of fermions forming Cooper pairs. Gauging implies that superconductors are inherently bosonic systems, yet they are endowed with a gravito-magnetic anomaly that is the remnant of their fermionic origin. We recognize that this anomaly is related to the Gaiotto-Kapustin-Thorngren bosonization, achieved via gauging fermion parity $(-1)^F$, now included in the gauge dynamics. This anomaly characterizes gauged electronic matter in great generality in three and four spacetime dimensions, forbidding trivial massive phases at low energy. It holds beyond the validity of the Higgs model, nd in other kinds of superconductors as well. It also appears in the nontrivial massless phase of three-dimensional electrodynamics, recently understood.

</details>


### [35] [Thermal Phase Structure of the Attractive Fermi Hubbard Model with Imaginary Chemical Potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18798)
*Evangelos G. Filothodoros*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在一维晶格上研究了大N吸引费米-哈伯德模型（large N attractive Fermi-Hubbard model）在虚化学势（imaginary chemical potential）存在下的BCS-BEC交叉（BCS-BEC crossover）。研究发现交叉由三个参数控制，并在幺正点（unitarity point）发现了一个热窗口（thermal window），其中能隙（gap）消失而费米子数（fermion number）出现极值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用平均场近似方法，在一维晶格上研究大N吸引费米-哈伯德模型，特别关注虚化学势iθ的存在。分析中考虑了三个控制参数：虚化学势iθ、通过热核（thermal kernel）g(βE_k,βθ)表示的温度，以及区分弱耦合和强耦合区域的参数δ_u。

Result: 在幺正点（U=U_c）发现了一个热窗口φ=βθ=2π/3,4π/3，其中能隙消失而费米子数N_f（量化类粒子激发和类空穴激发平衡）出现局部极大/极小值。在此热窗口内，BCS和BEC物理等待耦合变化来选择主导区域。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，通过虚化学势和热窗口的分析，能够更好地理解晶格多体物理中的配对关联，并为BCS-BEC交叉现象提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: We study the BCS--BEC crossover of the large $N$ attractive Fermi-Hubbard model on a one-dimensional lattice using the mean field approximation in the presence of an imaginary chemical potential. We show that the crossover is governed by three parameters. The imaginary chemical potential $iθ$, the temperature via a thermal kernel $g(βE_k,βθ)$ and the parameter $δ_u$ whose sign controls the weak and strong coupling regimes. At the unitarity point ($U=U_c$), we find a thermal window $φ=βθ=2π/3,4π/3$ where the gap vanishes while the fermion number $N_f$, which quantifies the balance between particle-like and hole-like excitations, has a local maximum/minimum. Inside this thermal window BCS and BEC physics are await changes in the coupling to be selected as the dominant regime. We expect that our results will unveil a better understanding of pairing correlations in lattice many-body physics.

### [37] [Symmetry resolved entanglement in Lifshitz field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19082)
*M. Reza Mohammadi Mozaffar,Ali Mollabashi*

Main category: hep-th

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索非相对论量子场论中的对称性分辨纠缠特性，为实验平台（如冷原子装置和介观系统）提供理论框架，其中粒子数分辨测量可用于探测对称性分辨纠缠。

Method: 采用带电矩（charged moments）和相关函数方法（correlator method），计算对称性分辨Renyi熵和冯·诺依曼熵（von Neumann entropies），并分析它们对子系统尺寸、电荷、质量和动力学指数z的依赖关系。

Result: 研究结果揭示了非相对论纠缠的独特特征：在Lifshitz标量理论中，大z区域出现电荷扇区间的近似均分（approximate equipartition），构型熵（configurational entropy）占主导；而Lifshitz费米子模型仅在相对论极限下展现真正的均分，涨落熵（fluctuation entropy）占主导。

Conclusion: 研究强调了守恒电荷、子系统尺寸、质量和动力学标度之间的丰富相互作用，为非相对论系统中可操作访问的纠缠提供了理论框架，对冷原子和介观系统等实验平台具有重要启示。

Abstract: We investigate symmetry-resolved entanglement in non-relativistic quantum field theories, including complex Lifshitz scalar chains and Lifshitz fermionic models. Using charged moments and the correlator method, we compute symmetry-resolved Renyi and von Neumann entropies and analyze their dependence on subsystem size, charge, mass, and the dynamical exponent z. Our results reveal distinct features of non-relativistic entanglement. In Lifshitz scalar theories, approximate equipartition among charge sectors emerges in the large-z regime, with configurational entropy dominating, whereas Lifshitz fermionic models exhibit genuine equipartition only in the relativistic limit, with fluctuation entropy prevailing. These findings highlight a rich interplay between conserved charges, subsystem size, mass, and dynamical scaling, and provide a framework to explore operationally accessible entanglement in non-relativistic systems. Our study offers insights relevant to experimental platforms such as cold atom setups and mesoscopic systems, where particle-number-resolved measurements can probe symmetry-resolved entanglement.

Abstract: We develop a systematic Hamiltonian formulation for a gravitating topological matter system in three-dimensional spacetime, coupling a scalar gauge field and a rank-2 antisymmetric gauge field to Einstein--Cartan gravity. We perform the Dirac--Bergmann analysis, systematically finding the full structure of the constraints, classifying them into first- and second-class ones, and computing their Poisson bracket algebra. Furthermore, we write down the explicit expression for the Hamiltonian generator of gauge symmetries on the full set of canonical variables, containing the exact number of gauge parameters, and demonstrate that, through a mapping of the gauge parameters, these gauge transformations reproduce on-shell the spacetime diffeomorphism and local Poincaré symmetries, thereby establishing the full symmetry structure of the coupled model. Our canonical analysis further reveals that the reduced phase-space admits exactly three reducibility conditions for the first-class constraints, which guarantee the consistency of the gravitating matter system by ensuring a correct count of physical degrees of freedom. The fundamental symplectic structure on the reduced phase-space is established through the explicit computation of the Dirac brackets.

To illustrate the formalism, we also construct, for the first time, massive gauge-invariant 3D ${\cal N}=2$ supersymmetric counterparts of the linearised actions for the old and new minimal supergravity theories. Our off-shell ${\cal N}=2$ supermultiplets carry a non-zero central charge, and are formulated in 3D ${\cal N}=2$ central charge superspace. The models can be reduced to 3D ${\cal N}=1$ superspace, by integrating out two Grassmann variables, and then consistent reality conditions on the superfields can be imposed. As a result, only two supercharges remain unbroken.

### [40] [On Global Embedding of Assisted Fibre Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19250)
*George K. Leontaris,Pramod Shukla*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文回顾了纤维暴胀（fibre inflation）模型在多场辅助下的实现可能性，通过多个纤维模（fibre moduli）共享超普朗克距离（trans-Planckian distance）来规避Kähler锥（Kähler cone）条件对单场暴胀的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准单场纤维暴胀需要暴胀子在有效模空间中穿越约${\cal O}(5-8)$M$_p$的超普朗克距离，但在具体CY orientifold设置中，Kähler锥条件通常对暴胀子范围施加严格限制，特别是在CY三倍体中存在瑞士奶酪结构（Swiss-Cheese structure）时，这些限制会阻碍暴胀平台的形成。

Method: 采用多场辅助方法，让多个纤维模共同分担所需的超普朗克距离，从而在接近各自Kähler锥边界前实现成功暴胀。该方法基于具有K3纤维化的Calabi-Yau三倍体（Calabi-Yau threefolds having K3-fibration），并嵌入大体积情景（Large Volume Scenarios）框架。

Result: 通过多场辅助机制，暴胀所需的超普朗克距离可以由多个纤维模共同承担，这有助于避免单个场因Kähler锥边界限制而无法产生足够efolds的问题，从而为纤维暴胀的全局嵌入提供了可行方案。

Conclusion: 多纤维模辅助方法为解决纤维暴胀模型中Kähler锥条件对场范围的限制提供了有效途径，使得在具体CY orientifold设置中实现成功暴胀成为可能，特别是在存在瑞士奶酪结构的情况下。

Abstract: Fibre inflation is one of the most attractive models realized in the type IIB orientifold compactification. It is embedded in the framework of L(arge) V(olume) S(cenarios) using a class of compactifying Calabi-Yau (CY) threefolds having K3-fibration. The standard single-field fibre inflation is driven by a fibre modulus which needs to travel a trans-Planckian distance of the order of ${\cal O}(5-8)$M$_p$ in the effective moduli space. The global embedding attempts using concrete CY orientifold setups have shown that Kähler cone conditions can generically induce some significantly tight bounds on the inflaton range, especially in the presence of a Swiss-Cheese structure via an exceptional rigid divisor in the CY threefold. Such field range bounds usually obstruct the inflationary plateau, leading to insufficient number of efolds during the inflationary dynamics. In this context, we review our recent work about the possibility of assisting multiple fibre moduli such that the burden of traveling the required trans-Planckian distance could be shared by multiple fields, and successful inflation could be realized before hitting (or being too close to) their respective individual Kähler cone boundaries.

  We prove that the Fourier-Mukai transform introduced by Lau-Tseng-Yau exchanges type-A supersymmetric cycles, which are given by special Lagrangian sections equipped with flat $\mathrm{U}(1)$ connections, with type-B cycles, corresponding to line bundles whose connections satisfy the deformed Hermitian-Yang-Mills (dHYM) equation.
  We provide pure Lie-theoretic criteria for the existence of non-Kähler SYZ mirror pairs whose base manifolds are solvmanifolds.   To contextualize the role of the Tseng-Yau cohomology, we link it to noncommutative geometry. We introduce the Tseng-Yau and Bott-Chern mirror bicomplexes. We show that (some of) their enclosed cohomologies reduce to the primitive Tseng-Yau and Bott-Chern cohomologies and that for basic forms they are isomorphic under the Fourier-Mukai transform.
  As a last contribution, we discuss how to explicitly compute the Tseng-Yau and the Bott-Chern cohomology for the non-Kähler SYZ mirror pairs constructed here.

### [42] [Spatially modulated instabilities of an AdS black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19306)

Abstract: We analyze instabilities of an Einstein-Maxwell theory obtained from an N=2, D=5 supergravity. The theory admits a gauge Chern-Simons term in presence of which we consider perturbative instability of an AdS black hole solution. We find that the strength of the gauge Chern-Simons coupling saturates the threshold value for which the instability occurs, which we have observed both in the near horizon limit as well as analysis of the normal modes. Inclusion of terms upto fourth order in derivatives admits a mixed gauge-gravitational Chern-Simons term as well. Considering both the Chern-Simons terms, we find that momentum dependent instability sets in below a critical temperature giving rise to a bell-curve phase diagram which implies this would lead to a spatially modulated solution. We have considered all the terms upto quartic order of the derivatives and discuss the possible approach for further analysis.

</details>

*Ren Ito,Akio Nago,Shou Tanigawa*

Abstract: We study asymmetric orbifolds of the $E_8\times E_8$ heterotic string from the perspective of worldsheet Dai-Freed anomalies. In the fermionic description, these conditions are exactly the familiar level-matching constraints, together with the additional mod-2 conditions that appear for even $m$. ### [45] [Unitarity Quadratic Quantum Gravity in 4D](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19707)
*K. Sravan Kumar,João Marto*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 在二次引力理论中，当Weyl平方系数为正时，额外的自旋-2（spin-2）部分对应一个对偶倒置谐振子（dual inverted harmonic oscillator），而非鬼态（ghost）。该理论满足光学定理（optical theorem）且保持幺正性（unitarity），同时与可重整性（renormalizability）一致。
