  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在解决二次引力理论中自旋-2（spin-2）部分的物理诠释问题。传统上，当Weyl平方系数为正时，该部分常被解释为鬼态（ghost），但本文提出了一种不同的理解框架。

Method: 采用Wightman谱条件（Wightman spectrum condition）证明Källén-Lehmann谱密度（spectral density）为零。通过分析传播子极点（propagator pole）的类空（spacelike）性质，将传播子唯一固定为主值形式（principal value form）。

Result: 证明了对偶倒置谐振子（dual IHO）自旋-2不是渐近态（asymptotic state），在所有圈阶（loop orders）仅提供虚贡献（virtual contributions）。光学定理（optical theorem）得到满足，幺正性（unitarity）得以保持，且与可重整性（renormalizability）一致。

Conclusion: 二次引力理论中额外的自旋-2（spin-2）部分对应对偶倒置谐振子（dual inverted harmonic oscillator），而非鬼态（ghost）。传播子的主值形式（principal value form）是定理而非预设，该理论框架同时保持了幺正性（unitarity）和可重整性（renormalizability）。

Abstract: In quadratic gravity, with a positive Weyl squared coefficient, the extra spin-2 sector is shown to correspond to a dual inverted harmonic oscillator, instead of a ghost. Using the Wightman spectrum condition, we prove that the associated Källén--Lehmann spectral density vanishes, reflecting the absence of a normalizable ground state and the spacelike nature of the propagator pole. This uniquely fixes the propagator to a principal value form as a theorem, not a prescription. The optical theorem is satisfied, the dual IHO spin-2 is not an asymptotic state, and gives only virtual contributions at all loop orders. As a result, unitarity is preserved consistently with renormalizability.

Method: 提出"自举法结合正定性（bootstrapping with positivity）"方法，将Dyson-Schwinger方程与矩的正定性约束相结合来近似张量模型的矩。该方法借鉴了$U(N)$不变随机矩阵的处理方式，并将其推广到更高维度的张量情形。

Abstract: This work proposes a bootstrapping with positivity methodology to study random $U(N)^{D}$ invariant tensors in the large $N$ limit. As has been done for $U(N)$ invariant random matrices, we combine the Dyson-Schwinger equations and positivity constraints of moments to approximate the moments of such tensor models. As examples, we bootstrap the quartic and two hexic rank three tensor models. All models studied converge quickly, and for those which have known analytic formulae, they converge to such solutions. Abstract: Precise and flexible control of structured light fields is essential for applications ranging from optical trapping and quantum simulation to microscopy and materials processing. Acousto-optical deflectors (AODs) are widely used in these settings due to their high speed, large damage threshold, and ability to generate steerable optical tweezers. Multi-tone driving offers a powerful alternative to slow sequential scanning, enabling the projection of complex patterns with high accuracy as rapid acoustic modulation averages out inter-spot interference. In two dimensions, however, intermodulation between tones in orthogonal AODs can reintroduce coherent artifacts. We present a fast, feedback-free AOD projection scheme based on an incommensurately staggered frequency lattice that intrinsically suppresses such artifacts. For separable two-dimensional target patterns, our method removes the need for scanning entirely, enabling substantially faster and highly accurate projections. We further extend the approach to non-separable images using a minimal scanning strategy that maintains rather high projection speeds. These results demonstrate that appropriately engineered multi-tone AOD driving offers an efficient and robust route to high-speed, high-fidelity generation of arbitrary intensity patterns.

Abstract: Exciton-polariton lasers are coherent light sources which do not require the population inversion (transparency) condition to be fulfilled. They have been conceptualized at the end of the XXth century but until now they operate almost exclusively under optical injection, which severely limits the widespread integration of the polariton-based devices implemented so far. Here we tackle this issue by reporting an electrically-pumped exciton-polariton laser based on GaN and operating at room temperature in a mode-locked regime. The laser architecture is close to the geometry of commercial ridge-waveguide GaN lasers, but based on a bulk GaN active region instead of quantum wells. Unique features of polariton lasers are demonstrated, in particular the breakdown of the transparency condition, which enables our polariton lasers to operate even when only a small fraction (20\%) of the cavity length is injected. Moreover, the large polaritonic gain allows for the operation of a short cavity length (60$μm$) compared to commercial lasers. From the very same sample, we also achieve polariton lasing under optical injection, confirming that the doped layers necessary for electrical injection do not prevent strong-coupling nor polariton lasing. Our results open a new perspective for polariton-based devices.

### [50] [Investigating the formation channel of GW231123: Population III stars or hierarchical mergers?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18709)
*Federico Angeloni,Konstantinos Kritos,Raffaella Schneider,Emanuele Berti,Luca Graziani,Stefano Torniamenti,Michela Mapelli,Ataru Tanikawa*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究通过耦合星系形成模型与星团种群合成代码，系统分析了GW231123引力波事件的起源。研究发现孤立双星演化无法解释观测到的合并红移，而动力学层次合并机制能自然再现黑洞质量与自旋特征，支持该事件源于早期宇宙贫金属环境中球状星团的连续合并。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GW231123引力波事件中黑洞组分质量位于或超过对不稳定性质量间隙（pair-instability mass gap），这对当前恒星演化模型构成重大挑战。研究旨在通过自洽的宇宙学模拟框架，探究该事件的可能起源机制。

Method: 研究耦合了星系形成模型GAMESH与星团种群合成代码RAPSTER，并整合了两个独立的双星种群合成代码（SEVN和BSEEMP）。该框架首次能够在同一宇宙学模拟中重建GW231123类候选体的完整生命周期，实现不同形成通道的自洽比较。

Result: 孤立双星演化无法复现推断的合并红移：SEVN中形成的黑洞双星半长轴过大（>10^3太阳半径），无法在哈勃时间内并合；BSEEMP中候选体仅出现在极低金属丰度（Z=10^{-10}），在模拟的过密区域对恒星形成率密度贡献可忽略。相反，动力学层次起源得到强有力支持：观测黑洞质量可通过致密球状星团中的连续合并自然再现，高无量纲自旋与此层次种群一致。局域合并率密度为0.78 Gpc^{-3} yr^{-1}，峰值出现在红移z=4-6，追踪了贫金属环境（Z=0.006）中球状星团的最大形成率。

Conclusion: GW231123可能代表了早期宇宙中形成的稳健层次黑洞种群的基准事件。研究结果强烈支持该引力波事件源于动力学层次合并机制，而非孤立双星演化通道。

Abstract: The gravitational wave event GW231123, with component black hole masses lying within or above the pair-instability mass gap, poses a significant challenge to current stellar evolution models. In this Letter, we investigate its origin by coupling the galaxy formation model GAMESH with the cluster population synthesis code RAPSTER, and with two distinct binary population synthesis codes (SEVN and BSEEMP). This framework allows us, for the first time, to reconstruct the life cycle of GW231123-like candidates within the same cosmological simulation, enabling a self-consistent comparison between different formation channels. We find that, although both population synthesis codes can in principle produce black holes compatible with GW231123, isolated binary evolution fails to reproduce the inferred merger redshift. In SEVN, massive black hole binaries form with semi-major axes > 10^3 Rsun , preventing coalescences within a Hubble time. In BSEEMP, candidates arise only at extremely low metallicities (Z = 10^{-10}), which contribute negligibly to the star formation rate density in our overdense simulated volume. Our results instead strongly support a dynamical, hierarchical origin. The observed black hole masses are naturally reproduced through successive mergers in dense globular clusters. The high dimensionless spins reported by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA Collaboration are consistent with this hierarchical population. We find a local merger rate density of 0.78 Gpc^{-3} yr^{-1}, with a peak at z = 4 - 6, tracing the maximum formation rate of globular clusters in metal-poor environments (Z = 0.006). Overall, GW231123 may represent a benchmark event for a robust population of hierarchical black holes formed in the early Universe.

</details>

### [51] [Non-extensive entropy of Vinen quantum turbulence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19478)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究[1]已在非可加熵（non-additive entropy）框架下考虑了湍流级联的统计结构。本研究旨在探索超流体中Vinen量子湍流的涡旋线系综（vortex line ensemble）的统计特性。

Method: 研究采用非广延Tsallis-Cirto统计（non-extensive Tsallis-Cirto statistics）来描述涡旋线系综，特别设定参数δ=3。该方法扩展了传统统计力学框架，适用于具有长程相互作用和非可加性的系统。

Result: 研究发现Vinen量子湍流（Vinen quantum turbulence）中的涡旋线系综可由δ=3的Tsallis-Cirto统计精确描述。这一结果将非广延统计力学成功应用于超流体湍流系统。

Conclusion: 超流体量子湍流的涡旋线系综遵循δ=3的非广延Tsallis-Cirto统计，为理解量子湍流的统计特性提供了新的理论框架，并扩展了非可加熵在湍流研究中的应用范围。

Abstract: In Ref. [1] the statistical structure of the turbulent cascade in the context of non-additive entropy was considered. Here we suggest that the vortex line ensemble in the Vinen quantum turbulence in superfluids is described by the non-extensive Tsallis-Cirto statistics with $δ=3$.

</details>


### [52] [Energy landscape of the kagome antiferromagnet: Characterization of multiple energy scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18902)
*Brandon B. Le,Seung-Hun Lee,Gia-Wei Chern*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过精确枚举和统计方法分析了kagome海森堡反铁磁体（kagome Heisenberg antiferromagnet）在其共面基态流形（coplanar ground-state manifold）中的能垒景观（energy landscape），揭示了由不同尺寸天气风向环（weathervane-loop）旋转所主导的多尺度能垒层次结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究kagome海森堡反铁磁体在其简并的共面基态流形中的动力学特性。虽然共面态在谐波阶（harmonic order）是简并的，但态间转变需要集体天气风向环旋转，其能垒随环尺寸增大而显著增长。

Method: 研究方法采用两种互补方法构建断连图（disconnectivity graphs）：对小晶格使用精确枚举和最小最大能垒计算（minimax-barrier calculations），对大系统基于构型空间随机游走（random walks through configuration space）进行统计构造，其中环长度（loop length）作为能垒高度的代理变量。

Result: 精确能垒景观揭示了主导的低能垒尺度与基本六自旋环（six-spin loops）相关，以及来自更长重排的更宽高能垒区域。统计分析显示能垒尺度的层次结构，包括显著的六自旋环峰和中间的无标度环长区域（scale-free regime of loop lengths）。

Conclusion: 该研究表明共面流形在动力学上是崎岖的（dynamically rugged），其低能动力学由环介导能垒（loop-mediated barriers）的层次结构主导，六自旋环控制最快的局域弛豫，而更慢的集体动力学源于更长环的激活。

Abstract: We investigate the energy landscape of the kagome Heisenberg antiferromagnet within its coplanar ground-state manifold. Although coplanar states are degenerate at harmonic order, transitions between them require collective weathervane-loop rotations whose barriers grow strongly with loop size. To characterize this structure, we construct disconnectivity graphs using two complementary approaches: exact enumeration and minimax-barrier calculations for small lattices, and a statistical construction for large lattices based on random walks through configuration space, with loop length used as a proxy for barrier height. The exact landscape reveals a dominant low-barrier scale associated with elementary six-spin loops and a broader higher-barrier sector from longer rearrangements. For large systems, the statistical analysis exposes a hierarchy of barrier scales, including a pronounced six-spin-loop peak and an intermediate scale-free regime of loop lengths. This hierarchy provides a natural basis for multiple dynamical time scales: six-spin loops govern the fastest local relaxation, while slower collective dynamics arise from activation of longer loops. These results show that the coplanar manifold is dynamically rugged, with its low-energy dynamics governed by a hierarchy of loop-mediated barriers.

</details>


### [53] [Coordination-number dependent universality in Mixed Wet Percolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18915)
*Jnana Ranjan Das,Santanu Sinha,Alex Hansen,Sitangshu Bikas Santra*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了混合润湿渗流（mixed-wet percolation）在双三角和双蜂窝晶格上的几何量标度性质。研究发现，在配位数（coordination number）较高的双三角晶格（z=6）上，该模型表现出普通点渗流（ordinary site percolation）特性；而在配位数较低的双蜂窝晶格（z=3）上，则表现出普通点渗流簇的壳（hull）特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合润湿渗流模型最近在孔隙介质两相流研究中被引入，该模型中主晶格（primal lattice）的格点以概率p被占据，而在对偶晶格（dual lattice）上相邻的占据与未占据格点之间放置键（bond）。对偶晶格上的占据键形成周界簇（perimeter clusters），本文旨在研究这些周界簇几何量的标度性质。

Method: 研究在双三角晶格（dual triangular lattice）和双蜂窝晶格（dual honeycomb lattice）上分析混合润湿渗流的周界簇。通过比较不同配位数（coordination number）晶格上模型的标度行为，探究普适性（universality）的破坏机制。

Result: 双三角晶格（z=6）表现出普通点渗流特性，而双蜂窝晶格（z=3）则表现出普通点渗流簇的壳特性。这种依赖于配位数的普适性破坏在渗流文献中较为罕见。三角晶格中的周界簇代表主晶格中点簇的边界，而蜂窝晶格中的周界则代表其壳。

Conclusion: 由于蜂窝晶格的低配位数，外部和内部周界保持隔离。然而，组合的外部与内部周界形成属于点渗流普适类的点簇边界。这种配位数依赖的普适性破坏揭示了混合润湿渗流模型在不同晶格结构下的不同物理表现。

Abstract: Mixed-wet percolation was introduced recently in the context of two-phase flow in porous media. In this model, the sites of the primal lattice are occupied with a certain probability $p$, and bonds are placed on the dual lattice between two adjacent occupied and unoccupied sites of the primal lattice. The occupied bonds on the dual lattice form perimeter clusters. In this paper, we investigate the scaling properties of the geometric quantities associated with the perimeter clusters of mixed-wet percolation on the dual triangular and dual honeycomb lattices. Although mixed-wet percolation on the dual triangular lattice with a higher coordination number ($z=6$) exhibits ordinary site percolation, the model on the dual honeycomb lattice with a lower coordination number ($z=3$) exhibits the properties of the hull of ordinary site percolation clusters. Such a $z$ dependent breakdown of universality in mixed-wet percolation is rare in the percolation literature. The perimeter clusters in the triangular lattice represent the boundary of the site clusters in the primal lattice, whereas the perimeters in the honeycomb lattice represent their hulls. Because of the low $z$ of the honeycomb lattice, the external and internal perimeters remain isolated. However, the combined external and internal perimeters form cluster boundaries of the site clusters that belong to the site percolation universality class.

</details>


### [54] [Spectral Signatures of Third-Order Pseudo-Transitions in Finite Systems: An Eigen-Microstate Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19244)
*Wei Liu,Songzhi Lv,Xin Zhang,Fangfang Wang,Kai Qi,Zengru Di*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于特征微态（eigen-microstate）框架的谱广义响应方法，通过构建三阶比率R₃来探测有限系统中的三阶伪相变（third-order pseudo-transitions），该方法无需依赖通常难以获得的微正则熵。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限系统中的三阶伪相变反映了超越传统临界性的重组现象，但传统识别方法通常依赖微正则熵（microcanonical entropy），而该量在实际中往往难以获取。因此需要开发一种不依赖微正则熵的替代方法。

Method: 在特征微态框架内引入了谱广义响应（spectral generalized response）。通过归一化谱权重（spectral weights）的分布构建了三阶比率R₃=K₃/(K₂)³，该比率能够探测超越主导模式凝聚（leading-mode condensation）的涨落模式间的不对称再分配。结合谱投影（spectral projection）方法进一步区分了依赖分支和独立分支。

Result: 在规则晶格和随机正则网络（random regular networks）上的Ising和Potts模型中，R₃的极值（extrema）始终追踪高阶异常（higher-order anomalies）。有效谱维度（effective spectral dimension）R_eff提供了这些异常发展的参与背景（participation background）。谱投影方法成功区分了与主导有序通道（dominant ordering channel）相关的依赖分支和源于次主导涨落子空间（subleading fluctuation subspace）内再分配的独立分支。

Conclusion: 研究结果为三阶伪相变提供了几何特征描述，将其视为构型空间（configuration space）中统计权重的重组。该方法建立了一条无需序参数（order-parameter-free）的途径来研究有限尺寸结构临界性（finite-size structural criticality）。

Abstract: Third-order pseudo-transitions in finite systems reflect reorganization beyond conventional criticality, yet their identification usually relies on microcanonical entropy, which is often inaccessible in practice. Here we introduce a spectral generalized response within the eigen-microstate framework. From the distribution of normalized spectral weights, we construct the third-order ratio $R_3=K_3/(K_2)^3$, which probes asymmetric redistribution among fluctuation modes beyond leading-mode condensation. Across Ising and Potts models on regular lattices and random regular networks, extrema of $R_3$ consistently track higher-order anomalies. Combined with spectral projection, the method further distinguishes dependent and independent branches: the former remain tied to the dominant ordering channel, whereas the latter arise from redistribution within the subleading fluctuation subspace. The effective spectral dimension $R_{\mathrm{eff}}$ provides the participation background in which these anomalies develop. These results establish a geometric characterization of third-order pseudo-transitions as reorganizations of statistical weight in configuration space and provide an order-parameter-free route to finite-size structural criticality.

</details>


### [55] [Self-propulsion protocols for swift non-equilibrium state transitions and enhanced cooling in active systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19252)
*Kristian Stølevik Olsen,Hartmut Löwen*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 提出了一种控制框架，利用自推进（self-propulsion）统计作为唯一控制参数，诱导受限活性物质（confined active matter）的非平衡态转变。噪声振幅的正定性及位置-推进相关性的基本界限定义了容许控制空间，并对非平衡态间转变施加了速度限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在开发一种控制框架，专门用于诱导受限活性物质系统中的非平衡态转变（non-equilibrium state transitions）。其核心动机是利用自推进统计作为唯一的控制参数，探索活性系统状态转变的基本限制。

Method: 提出了一种控制框架，其中自推进的统计特性作为唯一控制参数。该方法通过噪声振幅的正定性（positivity of noise amplitudes）和位置-推进相关性的基本界限（fundamental bounds on position-propulsion correlations）来定义容许控制空间。

Result: 研究发现非平稳初始状态（non-stationary initial states）能够促进额外的加速，这对应于用负相关性预加载状态。这使得活性冷却协议（active cooling protocols）能够超越其被动对应物（passive counterparts）的性能。

Conclusion: 该控制框架成功揭示了活性物质系统中非平衡态转变的基本速度限制，并展示了通过非平稳初始状态和负相关性预加载实现加速的机制，为设计超越被动系统的活性冷却协议提供了理论基础。

Abstract: A control framework is proposed for inducing non-equilibrium state transitions in confined active matter, where the statistics of self-propulsion serve as the only control parameter. Positivity of the noise amplitudes and fundamental bounds on position-propulsion correlations define the admissible control space and impose speed-limits on transitions between non-equilibrium states. We show that non-stationary initial states facilitate additional speed-ups, corresponding to pre-loading the state with negative correlations. This enables active cooling protocols that outperform their passive counterparts.

</details>

### [56] [Information-to-energy trade-offs and the optimal alphabet of polymer replication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19563)
*Damián G. Hernández*

Main category: q-bio.QM

TL;DR: 该研究将聚合物复制粗粒化模型构建为模板与副本间的通信信道，通过计算长链稳态极限下的互信息，揭示了准确复制区域中信息传输与能量效率的权衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在分析聚合物复制过程中的信息传输特性，通过通信信道框架理解模板与副本间的信息传递机制，为评估复制保真度与能量效率提供理论依据。

Method: 将聚合物复制模型构建为通信信道（communication channel），计算长链稳态极限下的互信息（mutual information），分析信息-能量成本比（information-to-energy cost ratio）与单体字母表大小（monomer alphabet size）的关系。

Result: 在准确复制区域，每个单体的信息量仅取决于模板特异性；即使小误差分数也会导致显著信息损失。信息-能量比随单体字母表大小呈现非单调变化，最优值主要由单体组装自由能决定。DNA的四碱基字母表系统远离信息传输最优状态。

Conclusion: 生物复制可能优先抑制自发随机组装而非追求信息-能量效率最优。研究使用香农界限（Shannon bounds）表征可实现的速率-保真度权衡，为评估群体模型中的校对机制提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We analyze information transmission in a recently proposed coarse-grained model of polymer replication by framing it as a communication channel between templates and copies. By calculating the mutual information in the steady-state limit of long chains, we recover the accurate-random phase diagram and establish that the information per-monomer depends solely on template specificity within the accurate regime. Crucially, even in the accurate region, small error fractions lead to substantial information loss due to the nonlinear relationship between errors and mutual information. Examining the information-to-energy cost ratio reveals non-monotonic behavior as a function of monomer alphabet size, with an optimum determined primarily by the per-monomer assembly free energy. For DNA's four-base alphabet, we find that the observed effective assembly energy (at least $14\,k_B T$) places the system far from the information-transmission optimum, suggesting that biological replication may prioritize the suppression of spontaneous random assembly over information-to-energy efficiency. We also characterize achievable rate-fidelity trade-offs using Shannon bounds, providing a theoretical framework for evaluating future proofreading mechanisms in ensemble models.

</details>

### [59] [Search for quantum black holes in lepton+jet final states using proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13.6$ TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19495)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究在ATLAS探测器记录的13.6 TeV质子-质子碰撞数据中，搜索电子+喷注或μ子+喷注末态中的量子黑洞（quantum black holes），未发现超出标准模型背景的显著信号，并设定了迄今最强的量子黑洞产生排除限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider）Run 3阶段中心质心能量（centre-of-mass energy）较Run 2增加0.6 TeV，导致最高质量量子黑洞的产生截面（production cross-section）可能提升达一个数量级，为探测此类新物理现象提供了重要机遇。

Method: 分析方法使用ATLAS探测器在2022-2024年Run 3期间记录的13.6 TeV质子-质子碰撞数据，对应积分亮度（integrated luminosity）为164 fb⁻¹。搜索针对电子+喷注或μ子+喷注（electron+jet or muon+jet）高不变质量（high invariant mass）末态进行。

Result: 未观察到超出标准模型（Standard Model）背景的显著过剩信号。研究在多个基准模型（benchmark models）中设定了95%置信水平（95% CL）的产生截面与分支比（branching ratio）乘积上限，质量尺度达到9.4 TeV。

Conclusion: 这些排除限代表了迄今对量子黑洞产生的最强约束，为额外维度（extra dimensions）和量子引力（quantum gravity）理论提供了重要的实验限制。

Abstract: A search for quantum black holes in electron+jet or muon+jet final states with high invariant mass is performed. The analysis uses data from $\sqrt{s}=13.6~\textrm{TeV}$ $pp$ collisions recorded by the ATLAS detector between 2022 and 2024 during Run~3 of the Large Hadron Collider, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of $164~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$. This search is strongly motivated by a dramatic increase of the production cross-section by up to an order of magnitude for the highest masses considered, thanks to the small increase of $0.6~\textrm{TeV}$ in centre-of-mass energy between Run~2 and Run~3. No significant excess above the Standard Model background is observed, and 95\% CL upper limits are set on the production cross-section times branching ratio in several benchmark models, reaching a mass scale of $9.4~\textrm{TeV}$. These represent the strongest exclusion limits to date on quantum black hole production.

Nygren,E. Oblak,I. Osborne,J. Palacio,B. Palmeiro,A. Para,I. Parmaksiz,A. Pazos,J. Pelegrin,M. Pérez Maneiro,M. Querol,J. Renner,I. Rivilla,C. Rogero,L. Rogers,B. Romeo,C. Romo-Luque,E. Ruiz-Chóliz,P. Saharia,F. P. Santos,J. M. F. dos Santos,M. Seemann,I. Shomroni,A. L. M. Silva,P. A. O. C. Silva,A. Simón,S. R. Soleti,M. Sorel,J. Soto-Oton,J. M. R. Teixeira,S. Teruel-Pardo,J. F. Toledo,C. Tonnelé,S. Torelli,J. Torrent,A. Trettin,P. R. G. Valle,M. Vanga,P. Vázquez Cabaleiro,J. F. C. A. Veloso,J. D. Villamil,L. M. Villar Padruno,J. Waiton,A. Yubero-Navarro*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: NEXT-100探测器在3.95巴压力下测量了氡诱导本底，发现内部Rn-222活度为0.95 Bq/m³，通过拓扑选择可将本底指数降低至约4×10⁻⁵ counts/(keV·kg·yr)，比总放射性本底预期低一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: NEXT-100探测器旨在利用高压氙-136电致发光时间投影室首次进行有竞争力的无中微子双贝塔衰变（\bbnonu）搜索。首次低本底运行致力于测量影响该搜索的氡诱导本底贡献。

Method: 在3.95巴压力下运行NEXT-100探测器，评估内部和外部空气中氡的贡献。通过分析氡子体在探测器阴极表面的沉积，测量Rn-222活度和Bi-214产生率，并应用拓扑选择要求事件中仅包含一个双电子样径迹。

Result: 内部Rn-222活度为(0.95±0.04(stat)±0.09(sys)) Bq/m³，未观察到Rn-220痕迹。Rn诱导的Bi-214产生率为(0.97±0.05(stat)±0.10(sys)) Hz（可见能量>400 keV）。\bbnonu感兴趣区域的本底指数为(7.3±1.5(stat)±0.8(sys))×10⁻⁴ counts/(keV·kg·yr)，拓扑选择后降至~4×10⁻⁵ counts/(keV·kg·yr)。

Conclusion: 通过分析空气中氡活度与NEXT-100测量事件率的相关性，证实探测器在LSC氡减排系统支持下运行于近乎无氡环境。拓扑选择后的本底指数比NEXT-100总放射性本底预期低一个数量级，为\bbnonu搜索创造了有利条件。

Abstract: The NEXT-100 detector at the LSC aims at the first competitive search for the \bbnonu decay using a high-pressure \Xe{136} electroluminescent time projection chamber. The first low-background run of NEXT-100 at 3.95 bar has been devoted to the measurement of the radon-induced backgrounds impacting this search. The contributions from both the internal and external airborne radon have been evaluated. The internal \Rn{222} activity is found to be (0.95$\pm$0.04(stat)$\pm$0.09(sys)) Bq/m$^3$, while no traces of \Rn{220} have been observed. Most of the \Rn{222} progeny plate-out on the surface of the cathode of the detector, leading to a rate of Rn-induced \Bi{214} of (0.97$\pm$0.05(stat)$\pm$0.10(sys)) Hz for visible energies above 400 keV. The corresponding background index in the \bbnonu region of interest is evaluated as (7.3$\pm$1.5(stat)$\pm$0.8(sys))$\times10^{-4}$ counts/(keV$\cdot$kg$\cdot$yr) after selection of the fully contained events. This background index is reduced to $\sim$4$\times10^{-5}$ counts/(keV$\cdot$kg$\cdot$yr) by applying a topological selection requiring only one double-electron-like track in the events. This value is one order of magnitude below the total radiogenic background expectation in NEXT-100. By analyzing the correlation of the airborne radon activity and the measured rate of events in NEXT-100, it is concluded that the detector operates in a virtualy radon-free environment thanks to the radon abatement system of the LSC.

### [61] [Cycle holonomy induces higher-order constraints and controls remote synchronization transitions via twisted Laplacian spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19682)
*Lluís Torres-Hugas,Jordi Duch,Sergio Gómez,Alex Arenas*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 该研究证明高阶动力学约束自然出现在图的1-骨架中，当相互作用具有非平凡拓扑结构时。通过相位振荡器动力学与U(1)值连接模型，建立了谱框架将动力学挫败与网络上同调联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高阶相互作用网络通常使用超图或单纯复形建模，但本研究旨在证明有效的（effective）高阶动力学约束可以自然出现在图的1-骨架（1-skeleton）中，前提是相互作用具有非平凡拓扑结构（nontrivial topological structure）。

Method: 研究采用相位振荡器（phase-oscillator）动力学，将边相位滞后（edge phase lags）建模为U(1)值连接（U(1)-valued connection）。该结构诱导出梯度Sakaguchi-Kuramoto型流（gradient Sakaguchi-Kuramoto-type flow）和相关的扭曲拉普拉斯算子（twisted Laplacian），其谱依赖于连接的上同调类（cohomology class）。

Result: 证明扭曲拉普拉斯算子存在零模（zero mode）当且仅当连接是上同调平凡（cohomologically trivial）的，即所有循环和乐（cycle holonomies）消失。同步受阻不是由局部成对失配引起，而是由循环上的内在拓扑挫败（intrinsic topological frustration）导致。扭曲拉普拉斯算子的最小特征值随和乐大小缩放，其谱跃迁（spectral transitions）准确预测了相位锁定态（phase-locked state）随挫败增加而失稳。

Conclusion: 研究建立了将动力学挫败与网络上同调联系起来的谱框架，表明远程同步（remote synchronization）中的跃迁由循环级拓扑约束（cycle-level topological constraints）塑造。对于恒定相位滞后的特定情况，解析推导出五边形循环的临界跃迁点α_c = π/3，与先前报告的数值阈值定量一致。

Abstract: Higher-order interaction networks are typically modeled using hypergraphs or simplicial complexes, where interactions explicitly involve more than two nodes. Here we demonstrate that effective higher-order dynamical constraints emerge naturally on the 1-skeleton of a graph, provided the interaction carries nontrivial topological structure. We study phase-oscillator dynamics with edge phase lags modeled as a $U(1)$-valued connection. This structure induces a gradient Sakaguchi--Kuramoto-type flow and an associated twisted Laplacian whose spectrum depends on the cohomology class of the connection. We prove that the associated twisted Laplacian admits a zero mode if and only if the connection is cohomologically trivial, that is, when all cycle holonomies vanish. Consequently, synchronization is obstructed not by local pairwise mismatches, but by intrinsic topological frustration on cycles. We derive that the smallest eigenvalue of the twisted Laplacian scales with the magnitude of the holonomy, and its spectral transitions accurately predict the loss of stability of the phase-locked state as frustration is increased. For the specific case of constant phase lag, we analytically derive the critical transition point, $α_c = π/3$ for a pentagonal cycle, which is in quantitative agreement with previously reported numerical thresholds. Our results establish a spectral framework linking dynamical frustration to network cohomology, and show that transitions in remote synchronization are shaped by cycle-level topological constraints.

</details>

### [62] [RL-ABC: Reinforcement Learning for Accelerator Beamline Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19146)
*Anwar Ibrahim,Fedor Ratnikov,Maxim Kaledin,Alexey Petrenko,Denis Derkach*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RLABC是一个开源Python框架，可将Elegant束流线配置自动转换为强化学习环境，用于加速器束流线的高维控制优化，通过验证实验实现了与传统方法相当的粒子传输性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粒子加速器束流线优化是一个传统上需要大量专家干预的高维控制问题。研究旨在通过开发自动化框架，减少对专家干预的依赖，实现更高效的束流线优化。

Method: RLABC框架通过SDDS接口与Elegant束流动力学模拟代码集成，自动将束流线调谐问题表述为马尔可夫决策过程。该方法自动预处理晶格文件，在每个可调元件前插入诊断监视点，构建包含束流统计、协方差信息和孔径约束的57维状态表示，并提供可配置的奖励函数用于传输优化。

Result: 在基于VEPP-5注入复合体的测试束流线上验证（包含11个四极磁铁和4个二极磁铁的37个控制参数），深度确定性策略梯度（Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient）智能体实现了70.3%的粒子传输率，性能与微分进化等传统方法相当。框架的分阶段学习能力可将复杂优化问题分解为可管理的子问题，提高训练效率。

Conclusion: RLABC框架成功实现了基于强化学习的束流线优化，提供了一种通用的自动化方法。该开源框架包括配置文件和使用示例，旨在促进相关技术的采用和进一步研究。

Abstract: Particle accelerator beamline optimization is a high-dimensional control problem traditionally requiring significant expert intervention. We present RLABC (Reinforcement Learning for Accelerator Beamline Control), an open-source Python framework that automatically transforms standard Elegant beamline configurations into reinforcement learning environments. RLABC integrates with the widely-used Elegant beam dynamics simulation code via SDDS-based interfaces, enabling researchers to apply modern RL algorithms to beamline optimization with minimal RL-specific development.
  The main contribution is a general methodology for formulating beamline tuning as a Markov decision process: RLABC automatically preprocesses lattice files to insert diagnostic watch points before each tunable element, constructs a 57-dimensional state representation from beam statistics, covariance information, and aperture constraints, and provides a configurable reward function for transmission optimization. The framework supports multiple RL algorithms through Stable-Baselines3 compatibility and implements stage learning strategies for improved training efficiency.
  Validation on a test beamline derived from the VEPP-5 injection complex (37 control parameters across 11 quadrupoles and 4 dipoles) demonstrates that the framework successfully enables RL-based optimization, with a Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient agent achieving 70.3\% particle transmission -- performance matching established methods such as differential evolution. The framework's stage learning capability allows decomposition of complex optimization problems into manageable subproblems, improving training efficiency. The complete framework, including configuration files and example notebooks, is available as open-source software to facilitate adoption and further research.

</details>


### [63] [Fine-Tuning Small Reasoning Models for Quantum Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18936)
*Nathaniel S. Woodward,Zhiqi Gao,Yurii Kvasiuk,Kendrick M. Smith,Frederic Sala,Moritz Münchmeyer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究首次对小型（70亿参数）推理模型在理论物理领域进行学术性微调，重点关注量子场论（QFT）问题解决能力的开发，通过构建数据生成管道创建了2500多个合成问题，并分析了强化学习（RL）和监督微调（SFT）对推理能力的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型（LLMs）在理论物理中的应用日益增长，但学术界对于这些模型在训练过程中如何发展领域特定的物理推理能力缺乏深入探索。本研究旨在填补这一空白，特别关注理论物理领域的推理能力开发。

Method: 研究开发了稳健的数据生成管道，既能创建合成问题，也能将现有的人工编写问题适配为适合模型训练的形式。以量子场论（QFT）为主要领域，生成了2500多个合成问题，并收集了来自arXiv和标准教学资源的人工适配问题。进行了强化学习（RL）和监督微调（SFT）实验。

Result: 研究对微调前后的模型思维链（chains-of-thought）进行了广泛分析，以理解推理错误在RL和SFT过程中的演变。同时评估了性能提升以及向其他物理领域的泛化能力。研究公开了数据管道、可验证的QFT训练数据以及约2亿token的QFT推理轨迹。

Conclusion: 本研究为理论物理领域的大语言模型微调提供了首个学术性探索，建立了专门的数据生成方法和评估框架，为后续研究提供了可复现的基础设施和数据集，有助于深入理解物理推理能力在模型训练中的发展机制。

Abstract: Despite the growing application of Large Language Models (LLMs) to theoretical physics, there is little academic exploration into how domain-specific physics reasoning ability develops while training these models. To investigate this, we perform the first academic fine-tuning study of small (7B-parameter) reasoning models dedicated specifically to theoretical physics. Because open-source verifiable training data required to train such capabilities is scarce, we developed a robust data generation pipeline that can both create synthetic problems and make existing human-authored problems suitable for model training. Selecting Quantum Field Theory (QFT) as our primary domain, we generated over 2,500 synthetic problems alongside a curated collection of human-adapted problems sourced from arXiv and standard pedagogical resources. We conduct both Reinforcement Learning (RL) and Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) experiments, benchmarking performance gains as well as generalization to other physics domains. We perform an extensive analysis of model chains-of-though before and after fine-tuning, to understand how reasoning errors evolve during RL and SFT. Finally, we publicly release our data pipeline, verifiable QFT training data, and $\sim$200M tokens of QFT reasoning traces.

</details>


### [64] [Ultrametric OGP - parametric RDT \emph{symmetric} binary perceptron connection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19712)
*Mihailo Stojnic*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文建立了参数化重整化去噪理论（parametric RDT）与重叠间隙性质（OGPs）之间的理论联系，通过分析超度量OGPs（ult_s-OGPs）并推导其约束密度上界，发现这些界限与参数化RDT估计值高度一致，从而提出两者可能存在同构关系的猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究引入了fl-RDT框架来刻画统计计算间隙（statistical computational gaps, SCGs），并在对称二元感知机（symmetric binary perceptrons, SBPs）中获得了算法阈值估计。本文旨在进一步连接参数化RDT与重叠间隙性质（overlap gap properties, OGPs），这是解空间的另一关键几何特征。

Method: 针对任意正整数s，考虑s级超度量OGPs（ult_s-OGPs）并严格上界其关联约束密度α_{ult_s}。开发了一个包含组合与概率分量的解析联合边界程序：将组合部分转化为凸优化问题，概率部分转化为嵌套积分，并进行数值评估。

Result: 数值评估显示，前两个级别的最紧界限（ᾱ_{ult_1}≈1.6578和ᾱ_{ult_2}≈1.6219）与第三和第四提升级别的参数化RDT估计值（α_c^{(3)}≈1.6576和α_c^{(4)}≈1.6218）高度接近。在其他关键参数（包括重叠值和超度量簇的相对大小）上也观察到极好的一致性。

Conclusion: 基于观察结果，提出了连接ult-OGP与参数化RDT的若干猜想：算法阈值α_a等于两个极限的收敛值，且α_{ult_s}≤α_c^{(s+2)}（可能对某些或所有s成立等式）。最后讨论了ult-OGP与参数化RDT所有关键参数之间可能存在完全同构关系。

Abstract: In [97,99,100], an fl-RDT framework is introduced to characterize \emph{statistical computational gaps} (SCGs). Studying \emph{symmetric binary perceptrons} (SBPs), [100] obtained an \emph{algorithmic} threshold estimate $α_a\approx α_c^{(7)}\approx 1.6093$ at the 7th lifting level (for $κ=1$ margin), closely approaching $1.58$ local entropy (LE) prediction [18].
  In this paper, we further connect parametric RDT to overlap gap properties (OGPs), another key geometric feature of the solution space. Specifically, for any positive integer $s$, we consider $s$-level ultrametric OGPs ($ult_s$-OGPs) and rigorously upper-bound the associated constraint densities $α_{ult_s}$. To achieve this, we develop an analytical union-bounding program consisting of combinatorial and probabilistic components. By casting the combinatorial part as a convex problem and the probabilistic part as a nested integration, we conduct numerical evaluations and obtain that the tightest bounds at the first two levels, $\barα_{ult_1} \approx 1.6578$ and $\barα_{ult_2} \approx 1.6219$, closely approach the 3rd and 4th lifting level parametric RDT estimates, $α_c^{(3)} \approx 1.6576$ and $α_c^{(4)} \approx 1.6218$. We also observe excellent agreement across other key parameters, including overlap values and the relative sizes of ultrametric clusters.
  Based on these observations, we propose several conjectures linking $ult$-OGP and parametric RDT. Specifically, we conjecture that algorithmic threshold $α_a=\lim_{s\rightarrow\infty} α_{ult_s} = \lim_{s\rightarrow\infty} \barα{ult_s} = \lim_{r\rightarrow\infty} α_{c}^{(r)}$, and $α_{ult_s} \leq α_{c}^{(s+2)}$ (with possible equality for some (maybe even all) $s$). Finally, we discuss the potential existence of a full isomorphism connecting all key parameters of $ult$-OGP and parametric RDT.

</details>

### [65] [A physicist-friendly primer on the Hamiltonian for quantum sensing in proteins: analytical expressions and insights for a toy model of the radical-pair mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18608)
*Clarice D. Aiello,Brian L. Ross,Alessandro Lodesani,Morgan L. Sosa*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文为物理学家提供了关于自由基对（radical-pair）机制的最简化哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）的入门教程，通过完整的解析解和新的亮-暗态（bright-dark）分解视角，澄清了该模型的关键物理特征，特别是低场效应（low-field effect）和零场的特殊作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蛋白质中电子自旋依赖的化学反应（常称为"自由基对机制"）是生物学中磁场感应的主要微观机制，但实际模型的复杂性往往掩盖了其基本物理原理。本文旨在通过最简单的自由基对哈密顿量，为物理学家提供一个清晰的概念框架。

Method: 在实验相关的单重态-三重态（singlet-triplet）基中，推导了该玩具模型（toy model）的完整解析解，获得了瞬时单重态布居（singlet population）和时间平均单重态产率（singlet yields）的闭式表达式。引入了新的亮-暗态分解（bright-dark decomposition）视角，并借鉴技术量子传感（quantum sensing）的方法进一步分析模型。

Result: 研究表明，动力学允许类似原子物理中研究的亮-暗态分解结构。低场效应源于亮暗扇区间的相干项，而零场的特殊作用应理解为相位锁定（phase-locking）现象而非简单的混合增强。通过量子传感方法阐明了初始态制备的作用以及相干相位积累与时间平均惩罚之间的权衡关系。

Conclusion: 该玩具模型既可作为解析可处理的基准，也可作为未来工作的概念起点。新的亮-暗态分解视角使自由基对物理学的多个熟悉特征变得透明，为理解磁场感应的微观机制提供了更清晰的物理图像。

Abstract: Electron spin-dependent chemical reactions in proteins, often discussed under the 'radical-pair mechanism', remain the leading microscopic proposal for magnetic field sensing in biology. Yet the essential physics is often obscured by the complexity of realistic models. In this work, we present a physicist-friendly primer on the simplest radical-pair Hamiltonian that already captures many of the mechanism's best-known qualitative features. The contributions of this work are fourfold. First, we place on record a complete analytical solution of this toy model, which has previously been studied extensively, mostly through numerical and partial analytical approaches. Working in the experimentally relevant singlet-triplet basis, we derive closed-form expressions for the instantaneous singlet population and for two related time-averaged singlet yields. Second, we introduce a new interpretation of these results that makes several familiar features of radical-pair physics transparent. In particular, we show that the dynamics admit a bright-dark decomposition (in the sense of spin mixing), similar to structures studied in atomic physics. Third, through this bright-dark perspective, we clarify experimentally relevant features of the toy model. In particular, we show that the so-called 'low-field effect' arises from a coherence term between bright and dark sectors, and that the special role of zero field is best understood as a phase-locking phenomenon rather than merely as enhanced mixing. Fourth, we import methods developed in the context of technological quantum sensing to obtain further insight into the model. This allows us to clarify the role of initial state preparation and the trade-off between coherent phase accumulation and time-averaging penalties. The resulting toy model serves both as an analytically tractable benchmark and as a conceptual starting point for future work.

</details>

### [66] [The influence of the inverse Compton effect on the transverse momentum spectra of particles produced in pp collisions at \sqrt{s}=14 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18654)
*M. Alizada,M. Suleymanov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了QED逆康普顿效应（inverse Compton effect）的QCD类比对质子-质子碰撞中粒子横向动量谱的影响，发现在统计误差范围内，逆康普顿散射事件仅导致粒子产额适度增加约10%，且未观察到谱线显著展宽。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究QED逆康普顿效应的QCD类比（即胶子-夸克散射过程 g + q --> g + q）对高能质子-质子碰撞中粒子横向动量谱的影响，该过程类似于光子-电子康普顿散射中的能量重分布机制。

Method: 采用PYTHIA事件生成器（版本8.316）进行数值模拟，分析了5×10^5次质心能量为√s=14 TeV的质子-质子碰撞事件。通过初始夸克和胶子的相对能量对事件进行分类，区分康普顿散射（DCE）和逆康普顿散射（ICE）事件，并在p_T < 10 GeV/c范围内获取粒子横向动量谱。

Result: 分析表明，包含逆康普顿散射事件导致粒子产额适度增加，ICE与DCE事件的谱比在统计误差范围内保持近似恒定，约为1.1。未观察到横向动量谱的显著展宽现象。

Conclusion: 质子-质子碰撞可作为研究致密QCD介质（如夸克-胶子等离子体）中能量重分布机制的可靠基准，逆康普顿散射效应的影响相对有限，为后续复杂介质环境研究提供了对照基准。

Abstract: The influence of the QED-analog of the inverse Compton effect on the transverse momentum spectra of particles produced in proton-proton collisions at energies of \sqrt{s}=14 TeV has been investigated. The analysis is based on the quark-gluon scattering process g + q --> g + q, which is the QCD analogue of Compton scattering of a photon on an electron and can lead to energy redistribution between partons, analogous to the mechanism of the inverse Compton effect. Data obtained numerically using the PYTHIA event generator (version 8.316) were used. A total of 5*10^5 proton-proton collisions at \sqrt{s}=14 TeV were analyzed. Events were classified based on the relative energies of the initial quark and gluon, which allowed us to distinguish Compton scattering (DCE) events from inverse Compton scattering (ICE) events. Particle transverse momentum spectra were obtained in the region: p_{T} < 10 GeV/c. The results showed that including inverse Compton scattering events in the analysis leads to a moderate increase in particle yield. The ratio of the spectra for ICE and DCE events remains approximately constant and is about 1.1 within statistical errors. No significant broadening of the transverse momentum spectra is observed. These results show that proton-proton collisions can serve as a reliable baseline for studies of energy redistribution mechanisms in a dense QCD medium, such as quark-gluon plasma.

</details>


### [67] [A new approach to long-lived particle detection at hadron colliders: the $\textsf{DELIGHT-SHIELD}$ concept](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18693)
*Biplob Bhattacherjee,Arnav Chauhan,Swagata Mukherjee,Rhitaja Sengupta,Anand Sharma*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于未来100 TeV环形对撞机的新型探测器设计$\textsf{DELIGHT-SHIELD}$，通过多层复合屏蔽层优先抑制标准模型背景，而非依赖传统内径迹探测，为长寿命粒子搜索提供了革命性策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解决高亮度强子对撞机中长寿命粒子（long-lived particles, LLPs）搜索面临的挑战，传统方法依赖内径迹探测，但标准模型背景干扰严重。需要从根本上改变探测策略，优先物理背景抑制而非传统跟踪技术。

Method: 提出$\textsf{DELIGHT-SHIELD}$探测器设计，在专用相互作用点用于LLP搜索。核心创新是用多层复合屏蔽层（multi-layered composite shield）替换探测器内部部件，随后布置径迹体积，通过Geant4全模拟验证设计有效性。

Result: 分析估计显示标准模型强子和电磁背景抑制可达七个数量级。Geant4模拟验证了设计有效性，虽然实际抑制略低于分析估计（主要因屏蔽层内次级粒子产生），但剩余背景水平对LLP分析仍可管理。基于暗标量模型基准测试显示，在零背景条件下对$h\rightarrowφφ$过程的分支比灵敏度可达$\mathcal{O}(10^{-9})$。

Conclusion: 这种基于屏蔽的探测器概念不仅扩展了中性长寿命粒子的发现范围，还为区分新物理与标准模型穿透背景提供了严格的实验手段。建议在高亮度LHC分阶段实施作为该新颖探测概念的关键测试平台。

Abstract: We propose a fundamental shift in the search for beyond the Standard Model long-lived particles (LLPs) at high-luminosity hadron colliders by prioritizing physical background suppression over traditional inner tracking. We introduce $\textsf{DELIGHT-SHIELD}$, a dedicated detector design for a 100 TeV Future Circular Collider at a dedicated interaction point for LLP searches. By replacing the inner parts of the detector with a multi-layered composite shield, followed by tracking volumes, we estimate a suppression of Standard Model hadronic and electromagnetic backgrounds by up to seven orders of magnitude analytically. Full Geant4 simulations validate the effectiveness of this design. Although the achieved suppression is somewhat lower than the analytical estimate, primarily due to secondary particle production within the shield, the residual background remains at a level that is manageable for LLP analyses. It can be further mitigated by applying energy thresholds, as well as vertexing and timing cuts in the downstream detector. Benchmarking against dark scalar model, we show that this shielding based detector concept achieves sensitivity to branching ratios as low as $\mathcal{O}(10^{-9})$ for $h\rightarrowφφ$ process under zero background condition $-$ outperforming general-purpose detector baselines. This strategy not only expands the discovery reach for neutral LLPs but also provides a rigorous experimental handle to distinguish new physics from Standard Model punch-through backgrounds. We further discuss a phased implementation at the High-Luminosity LHC as a critical testbed for this novel detection concept.

### [68] [A Scientific Human-Agent Reproduction Pipeline](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18752)
*Joschka Birk,Gregor Kasieczka,Siddharth Mishra-Sharma,Benjamin Nachman,Dennis Noll,Tanvi Wamorkar*

TL;DR: SHARP（Scientific Human-Agent Reproduction Pipeline）是一个通过人机协作（human-agent collaboration）复现科学分析的结构化框架，将复现任务分解为离散步骤，由AI代理（AI agent）自主执行代码生成、测试和质量保证，研究人员在检查点（checkpoints）进行评审和指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学分析复现对于知识保存、代码库扩展和深化研究者理解至关重要，但相关努力往往超出其学术认可。作者认为科学数据分析复现本质上是翻译任务：将人类可读知识转换为机器可读分析代码，这使其特别适合AI代理处理。

Method: SHARP框架将复现任务分解为离散步骤，由AI代理使用专门的子代理（subagents）自主执行代码生成、测试和质量保证。研究人员在定义的检查点评审进展、提供反馈并指导分析，保持对科学判断的控制。

Result: 通过复现粒子物理学中已发表论文的喷注分类任务（jet classification task）进行演示。评估沿三个维度展开：分析性能与原结果的对比、代码质量和忠实度，以及人机对话性质，后者使用新颖的人机交互特征化框架进行评估。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了AI辅助科学复现的实用模型，其中研究者的角色从编写代码转变为理解、评估和指导，提升人类理解而非替代它。

Abstract: Reproducing scientific analyses is essential for preserving knowledge, building extensible codebases, and deepening researcher understanding - yet the effort often outweighs its academic recognition. We argue that the reproduction of scientific data analyses is fundamentally a translation task: converting human-readable knowledge (papers, documentation) into machine-readable analysis code. This makes it uniquely well-suited for AI agents. We present SHARP (Scientific Human-Agent Reproduction Pipeline), a structured framework for reproducing scientific analyses through human-agent collaboration. SHARP decomposes a reproduction task into discrete steps, which an AI agent executes autonomously using specialized subagents for code generation, testing, and quality assurance. At defined checkpoints, the researcher reviews progress, provides feedback, and steers the analysis - keeping the human firmly in control of scientific judgment while the agent handles implementation. We demonstrate SHARP by reproducing a jet classification task in particle physics from a published paper. We evaluate the reproduction along three axes: analysis performance against the original results, code quality and faithfulness, and the nature of the human-agent conversation. The latter is evaluated with a novel framework for characterizing human-agent interactions. Our work highlights a practical model for AI-assisted scientific reproduction where the researcher's role shifts from writing code to understanding, evaluating, and directing - elevating human understanding rather than replacing it.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于夸克-双夸克近似的非相对论性组分夸克模型，考虑所有三种可能的双夸克组合。模型参数通过拟合实验测量的B_c介子谱（B_c meson spectrum）确定，从而将重子预测锚定在实验约束的输入上，并在重介子和重子领域间建立一致性联系。

Conclusion: 非相对论性夸克-双夸克框架为三重味重子提供了可靠的描述，可作为未来实验搜索的有用参考。结果表明该模型能够一致地描述重介子和重子体系，特别适用于LHCb等实验的探测准备。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the mass spectra, magnetic moments, and Regge trajectories of the triply heavy baryons $Ω_{ccb}$ and $Ω_{cbb}$ within a nonrelativistic constituent quark model based on the quark--diquark approximation, which reduces the three-body problem to an effective two-body system. For each baryon, all three possible diquark clusterings are considered, providing a qualitative indication of the sensitivity of the results to the quark--diquark decomposition. The model parameters are fixed by a fit to the measured $B_c$ meson spectrum, thereby anchoring the baryon predictions to experimentally constrained inputs and establishing a consistent link between the heavy meson and baryon sectors. We obtain ground-state masses of approximately $8.0$~GeV for $Ω_{ccb}$ and $11.0$~GeV for $Ω_{cbb}$, with radial and orbital excitation patterns in good agreement with the results reported in the literature. The computed magnetic moments of the spin-$\tfrac{1}{2}$ and spin-$\tfrac{3}{2}$ states are consistent with the results of various approaches. A radial Regge analysis in the $(n_r, M^2)$ plane reveals approximately linear $P$-wave trajectories and mildly curved $S$-wave trajectories, with slope and intercept parameters that scale systematically with the heavy-quark content of the baryon. These results suggest that the nonrelativistic quark--diquark framework provides a reliable description of triply heavy baryons and serves as a useful reference for future experimental searches, particularly at LHCb.

Abstract: Neutrino trident scattering is a rare process in the Standard Model characterized by two charged leptons in the final state. ### [71] [Inflation from a Weyl-flat null origin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18641)
*Malaika Arshad,Jehanzad Zafar,Ahdab Althukair,Bilal Ahmad*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明具有Weyl平坦零点的暴胀起源与当前观测数据并不矛盾。通过研究渐近幂律背景，作者构建了一个可计算的单场框架，其中Penrose兼容的Weyl平坦暴胀起源作为现实且可检验的可能性得以保留。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解决Weyl平坦零点（Weyl-flat null origin）的暴胀起源与当前观测数据之间的潜在矛盾。传统观点认为此类起源可能与观测存在张力，但作者试图证明这种几何结构在现实暴胀模型中仍然可行。

Method: 作者研究规范单场暴胀（canonical single-field inflation）中具有渐近慢滚参数$ε(N)\to ε_\infty\in(0,1)$的背景，这些背景呈现渐近幂律行为。采用最小变形参数化$ε(N)=ε_\infty+(1-ε_\infty)\left(\frac{N_0}{N+N_0}\right)^p$（$p>1$），该参数化保持渐近几何结构并允许平滑退出。通过在e-fold时间中直接求解标量和张量模式方程进行分析。

Result: 研究发现存在可行的参数区域，其中标量谱指数$n_s$处于Planck优先范围，张量标量比$r\sim10^{-3}-10^{-2}$。该框架包含与再加热（reheating）兼容的基准点，表明Weyl平坦暴胀起源在现实暴胀模型中具有可行性。

Conclusion: Weyl平坦零点暴胀起源应被视为渐近普适性类（asymptotic universality class）而非刚性精确解。该研究提供了一个可计算的单场框架，证明Penrose兼容的Weyl平坦暴胀起源作为现实且可检验的可能性得以保留。

Abstract: We show that a Weyl-flat null origin of inflation need not be in tension with present observations. For canonical single-field inflation, any background with $ε(N)\to ε_\infty\in(0,1)$ as $N\to\infty$ is asymptotically power-law, inherits the same Weyl-flat null past boundary, and reconstructs an exponential tail in field space. This identifies the origin as an asymptotic universality class rather than a rigid exact solution. We study a minimal deformation, $ε(N)=ε_\infty+(1-ε_\infty)\left(\frac{N_0}{N+N_0}\right)^p$ with $p>1$, which preserves the asymptotic geometry, yields a smooth exit, and produces realistic finite-$N$ phenomenology. Solving the scalar and tensor mode equations directly in e-fold time, we find a viable corridor with $n_s$ in the Planck-preferred range and $r\sim10^{-3}-10^{-2}$, including reheating-compatible benchmarks. The result is a calculable single-field framework in which a Penrose-compatible Weyl-flat inflationary origin survives as a realistic and testable possibility.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用数据驱动分析方法，利用分支比、直接CP不对称性和混合诱导CP不对称性的实验信息。在味SU(3)对称性破缺（flavour-SU(3) breaking）的处理上，考虑了跃迁形状因子（transition form factors）、衰变常数（decay constants）和相空间因子（phase space factors）的修正。

Result: 研究发现当前实验数据与理论框架拟合良好，最佳拟合点对应的QCD因子化振幅中心值与QCD因子化框架内的动力学预测具有许多相似特征。特别地，未发现湮灭振幅（annihilation amplitudes）在数值上超出朴素ΛQCD/mb标度（naïve ΛQCD/mb scaling）的强烈证据。

Conclusion: 该分析验证了QCD因子化框架对无粲非轻子B衰变的适用性，并随后探讨了多个唯象应用，包括解决非轻子B衰变中长期存在的味疑难问题。

Abstract: Using experimental information on branching ratios as well as direct and mixing-induced CP asymmetries, we perform a data-driven analysis of charmless non-leptonic $B \to PP$ decays, where $P$ is any of the light pseudoscalar mesons. Implementing flavour-$SU(3)$ breaking at the level of transition form factors, decay constants and phase space factors, we find a good fit to the current experimental data. Our best-fit point materializes in QCD-factorization amplitudes whose central values resemble many features of the dynamical predictions obtained within the QCD factorization framework. Moreover, we do not find any strong indications that the size of annihilation amplitudes is numerically enhanced beyond the naïve $Λ_{\textrm{QCD}}/m_b$ scaling. Subsequently, we address a number of phenomenological applications, among which are various flavour puzzles that have been persisting in non-leptonic $B$ decays for quite some time.

### [73] [Probing the Tau Anomalous Magnetic Moment at Colliders: From Ultra-Peripheral Collisions to the Precision Frontier](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19665)
*Natascia Vignaroli*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该综述系统回顾了τ轻子反常磁矩（a_τ）的实验研究进展，重点分析了从LEP时代约束到LHC时代精度突破的范式转变，并展望了未来对撞机设施（Belle II、FCC、μ子对撞机）的探测前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: τ轻子的反常磁矩（a_τ）是检验标准模型（Standard Model）的重要基准，也是探测第三代轻子中新物理（New Physics）的高灵敏度探针。由于τ轻子寿命极短，传统的自旋进动测量方法无法实现，因此需要在高能对撞机上开发创新的实验策略。

Method: 综述重点分析了两种主要实验方法：超周边重离子对撞（Ultra-Peripheral Heavy-Ion Collisions, UPCs）和质子-质子对撞。UPCs利用铅-铅（PbPb）相互作用中相干光子流的Z^4增强效应，提供了一个理论上稳健的"准静态"环境，本质上相当于一个极高强度的"光子-光子对撞机"。

Result: LHC实验实现了从LEP时代约束到前所未有的精度的范式转变。CMS观测到了γγ→ττ过程，ATLAS从高质量Drell-Yan尾部获得了约束。UPCs提供了理论上干净的环境，而质子-质子对撞结果则面临TeV能标下有效场论（Effective Field Theory）有效性的挑战。

Conclusion: 未来FCC-hh在PbPb模式下的灵敏度约为O(10^{-2})，而下一代轻子设施（Belle II和FCC-ee）的目标是达到O(10^{-5})量级，这是探测标准模型电弱圈修正所必需的。长期来看，高能μ子对撞机（Muon Collider）可能达到O(10^{-6})的探测精度。

Abstract: The anomalous magnetic moment of the tau lepton, $a_τ$, represents a fundamental test of the Standard Model (SM) and a high-sensitivity probe for New Physics in the third generation of leptons. Due to the tau's extremely short lifetime, traditional spin-precession measurements remain inaccessible, necessitating innovative experimental strategies at high-energy colliders. This review provides a comprehensive overview of the current experimental landscape, highlighting the recent paradigm shift from LEP-era constraints to the unprecedented precision reached at the LHC. We emphasize the importance of Ultra-Peripheral Heavy-Ion Collisions (UPCs), which act as a ``photon-photon collider'' of extreme intensity. By leveraging the $Z^4$ enhancement of the coherent photon flux in Lead-Lead ($PbPb$) interactions, these collisions provide a theoretically robust ``quasi-static'' environment. These results are critically compared with the latest measurements from proton-proton collisions, including the recent CMS observation of the $γγ\to ττ$ process and the ATLAS constraints from the high-mass Drell-Yan tail. We evaluate their complementarity and the challenges related to Effective Field Theory validity at the TeV scale. Finally, we outline the future prospects for $a_τ$ at Belle II and the Future Circular Collider (FCC) stages. While FCC-hh in $PbPb$ mode provides a theoretically clean environment, its sensitivity remains limited to $\mathcal{O}(10^{-2})$. Conversely, the next generation of lepton facilities, specifically Belle II and FCC-ee, aims for the $\mathcal{O}(10^{-5})$ level, required to probe SM electroweak loop corrections. Long-term projections for a high-energy Muon Collider suggest a potential reach of $\mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$.

</details>


### [74] [Implications of the First JUNO Results for Dirac Neutrino Texture Zeros](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19122)
*Priya,Ranjeet Kumar,Labh Singh,Surender Verma*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受JUNO首次振荡结果（first oscillation results from JUNO）的启发，研究狄拉克中微子质量矩阵（Dirac neutrino mass matrix）中纹理零点（texture zeros）的现象学可行性。太阳混合角$\sin^2{θ_{12}}$和太阳质量平方差$Δm_{21}^2$精度的提高为检验预测性纹理零点框架提供了严格探针。

Method: 对两零点纹理（two-zero textures）的允许参数空间进行系统扫描，识别由减少的参数空间产生的振荡可观测量之间的尖锐相关性（sharp correlations）。分析当前JUNO测量对可行纹理结构施加的约束。

Result: 当前JUNO测量对可行纹理结构施加严格约束。虽然纹理C、A₂和A₁先前可行，但当前JUNO数据强烈不利于纹理C，仅纹理A₂和A₁与数据兼容。这些发现突显了狄拉克纹理零点情景对太阳扇区（solar sector）的显著敏感性。

Conclusion: JUNO数据对狄拉克中微子质量矩阵纹理零点框架提供了严格检验，显著限制了可行纹理结构。纹理C被强烈排除，仅纹理A₂和A₁保持兼容，突显了此类模型对太阳扇区参数的敏感性。

Abstract: Motivated by the first oscillation results from JUNO, we study the phenomenological viability of texture zeros in the Dirac neutrino mass matrix. The improved precision on the solar mixing angle $\sin^2{θ_{12}}$ and the solar mass-squared difference $Δm_{21}^2$ provide a stringent probe for scrutinizing predictive texture zero frameworks. We perform a systematic scan of the allowed parameter space for two-zero textures, identifying sharp correlations among oscillation observables arising from the reduced parameter space. Our analysis reveals that current JUNO measurements impose stringent constraints on the viable texture structures. In particular, although textures $C$, $A_2$, and $A_1$ were previously viable, current JUNO data strongly disfavor $C$, leaving only textures $A_2$ and $A_1$ compatible with the data. These findings underscore the remarkable sensitivity of Dirac texture zero scenarios to the solar sector.

### [75] [Progress on the soft anomalous dimension in QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19232)
*Einan Gardi,Zehao Zhu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文综述了多腿QCD振幅中红外奇点（IR singularities）的研究现状，提出了一种基于区域方法（Method of Regions）和半无限威尔逊线（semi-infinite Wilson lines）关联函数光锥展开的新策略，并成功计算了包含单个有质量色粒子与任意数量无质量粒子的振幅的三圈软反常维度（soft anomalous dimension）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探讨多腿QCD振幅中红外奇点的最新研究进展，特别关注软反常维度（soft anomalous dimension）显著简单性的关键原因。通过理解这一简单性的根源，可以开发更有效的计算方法来推进高阶计算。

Method: 作者提出了一种新颖的计算策略：利用区域方法（Method of Regions），通过对半无限威尔逊线（semi-infinite Wilson lines）关联函数进行光锥展开（lightcone expansion）来计算软反常维度。这种方法将复杂的振幅计算转化为更易处理的关联函数分析。

Result: 该策略已成功应用于计算包含单个有质量色粒子（massive coloured particle）与任意数量无质量粒子（massless ones）的振幅的三圈软反常维度。这一结果为更复杂情况的计算奠定了基础。

Conclusion: 新开发的计算策略为计算涉及两个重粒子（two heavy particles）的三圈软反常维度开辟了道路，并有望进一步推广到更高圈阶（higher loop orders）。该方法展示了在QCD红外奇点研究中推进高阶计算的潜力。

Abstract: We review the state-of-the-art knowledge of IR singularities in multileg QCD amplitudes, identifying the key reasons for the remarkable simplicity of the soft anomalous dimension. We then present a novel strategy to compute this quantity using a lightcone expansion of correlators of semi-infinite Wilson lines by the Method of Regions. Recently, this strategy allowed us to determine the three-loop soft anomalous dimension for amplitudes consisting of a single massive coloured particle with any number of massless ones. It opens the way to computing this quantity for amplitudes involving two heavy particles at three loops and potentially going to higher loop orders.

</details>


### [76] [Vortex structures in electron-positron pair production by two-colored fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19002)
*Adiljan Sawut,Ying-Jun Li,Hong-Hao Fan,Bai-Song Xie*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了在时间延迟双色电磁场中，电子-正电子对从真空中产生时的自旋分辨涡旋特性。通过将时间延迟G作为连续调谐参数，发现了从G=0时的干涉主导模式到G=0.5时量子化涡旋晶格成核的动态转变，这些拓扑结构呈现类似流体力学中冯·卡门涡街的交错排列。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索强场量子电动力学（QED）中，时间延迟双色电磁场作用下真空激发产生的电子-正电子对的自旋分辨涡旋特性。通过分析这些拓扑特征，为真空激发的量子动力学提供高保真诊断工具。

Method: 将时间延迟G作为连续调谐参数，研究电子-正电子对在时间延迟双色电磁场中的产生过程。通过分析动量空间形态，揭示其受自旋轨道选择规则（spin orbit selection rules）的严格支配，并探讨总角动量Jz守恒对轨道角动量Lz的影响。

Result: 研究发现从G=0时的干涉主导域模式到G=0.5时量子化涡旋晶格成核的动态转变，这些拓扑结构呈现类似冯·卡门涡街（von Karman vortex streets）的交错排列。平行自旋配置强制偶极子样连接，而反平行配置则解析为不同的四极子结构。大延迟时（G>1），宏观涡旋相干性因多通道干涉而溶解为混沌相景观，但自旋依赖的节点几何结构保持稳健。

Conclusion: 这些拓扑特征为强场量子电动力学中真空激发的量子动力学提供了高保真诊断工具。自旋分辨涡旋特性严格受自旋轨道选择规则支配，总角动量Jz守恒决定了产生对所需的轨道角动量Lz，揭示了量子真空激发的基本拓扑性质。

Abstract: We investigate the spin resolved vortex properties of electron positron pairs created from vacuum in time delayed, two color electromagnetic fields. By treating the temporal delay G as a continuous tuning parameter, we reveal a dynamic transition from interference-dominated domain patterns at G=0 to the nucleation of quantized vortex lattices at G=0.5. These topological structures exhibit a staggered arrangement analogous to von Karman vortex streets in fluid dynamics. We demonstrate that the momentum-space morphology is strictly governed by spin orbit selection rules, i.e., parallel spin configurations enforce a dipole-like connectivity, while anti-parallel configurations resolve into distinct quadrupole structures. This difference originates from the conservation of total angular momentum Jz, where the spin projection determines the required orbital angular momentum Lz of the created pairs. At large delays (G greater than 1), macroscopic vortex coherence dissolves into a chaotic phase landscope due to multi-channel interference, yet the spin-dependent nodal geometries remain robust. Our findings suggest that these topological signatures provide a high-fidelity diagnostic for the quantum dynamics of vacuum excitations in strong field QED.

### [77] [Thermo-mechanically coupled phase-field fracture model considering elastocaloric effect of shape memory alloy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18666)
*Shen Sun,Wei Tang,Weiwei He,Igor Polozov,Min Yi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种考虑形状记忆合金（SMA）弹热效应（eCE）的热-力耦合相场断裂模型，用于模拟与非等温马氏体相变及弹热效应耦合的裂纹扩展过程。该模型通过有限元方法验证，并模拟了Mn-Cu SMA的拉伸断裂特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模拟形状记忆合金（shape memory alloy, SMA）中与马氏体相变（martensitic transformation）及弹热效应（elastocaloric effect, eCE）相互作用的断裂行为仍具挑战性。需要开发能够耦合这些复杂物理过程的断裂模型。

Method: 提出了一种考虑SMA弹热效应的热-力耦合相场断裂模型（thermo-mechanically coupled phase-field fracture model）。该模型同时考虑了由eCE引起的热应变（thermal strain）和由相变引起的本征应变（eigen strain），并采用经验退化函数描述热导率随断裂序参数的变化。模型通过有限元方法（finite element method）进行验证。

Result: 模拟发现，马氏体变体（martensite variant）在裂纹萌生的应力集中处形核，并通常以45度角扩展。由eCE引起的热膨胀应变可增强临界载荷能力。大的相变动力学参数和取向角能增强eCE的强度和温度变化，但会降低变形能力。

Conclusion: 该相场模型展示了其在SMA热-力耦合增韧方面的能力。它也为弹热器件（elastocaloric devices）提供了一种利用eCE实现抗断裂的可能策略。

Abstract: Modelling fracture behavior of the shape memory alloy (SMA) that interacts with martensitic transformation and the associated elastocaloric effect (eCE) still remains challenging. Herein, a thermo-mechanically coupled phase-filed fracture model considering elastocaloric effect of SMA is proposed to simulate the cracking process coupled with the non-isothermal martensitic transformation and the associated eCE. In the phase-field model, both the thermal strain induced by eCE and the eigen strain induced by the phase transition are considered. An empirical degradation function is adopted to describe the thermal conductivity decreasing with the fracture order parameter. The model is validated with the finite element method and tensile fracture properties of Mn-Cu SMA are simulated. It is found that the martensite variant nucleates at the stress concentration where the crack initiates, and commonly spreads with an angle of 45 degree. The thermal expansion strain caused by the eCE could strengthen the critical load capacity. A large kinetic parameter for phase transition and the large orientation angle could enhance the strength and temperature change of eCE while the deformation capacity is reduced. The phase-field model demonstrates its ability in the thermal-mechanically coupled toughening of SMA. It also provides a possible fracture-resistance strategy by the utilization of eCE for elastocaloric devices.

</details>

*Poulomi Chakraborty,Brian Skinner,Penghao Zhu*

TL;DR: 该研究建立了轴依赖传导极性（ADCP）现象的通用定量判据，通过分析热电功率推导出判别金属、半金属和半导体中ADCP行为的必要充分条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴依赖传导极性（Axis-Dependent Conduction Polarity, ADCP）指单一材料中沿不同晶向分别呈现p型和n型传导的现象，这种特性使得无需异质结即可实现多种热电应用。研究旨在建立识别和预测ADCP材料的通用定量标准。

Method: 通过理论分析推导ADCP的通用判据，具体方法包括分析金属、半金属和半导体的热电功率（thermopower），获得ADCP出现的透明不等式条件。同时回顾已知ADCP材料，验证其能带结构特征和弛豫参数与推导不等式的一致性。

Result: 研究获得了判别ADCP现象的必要充分不等式条件，这些透明不等式适用于多种材料体系。验证表明已知ADCP材料的能带结构特征和弛豫参数均符合推导出的不等式判据。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了识别和预测轴依赖传导极性（ADCP）材料的通用定量框架，推导出的不等式判据为寻找新型ADCP材料提供了理论指导，有助于开发无需异质结的热电应用器件。

Abstract: Axis-Dependent Conduction Polarity (ADCP) refers to the phenomenon in which electrical transport within a single material is p-type along one crystallographic direction and n-type along the perpendicular direction. This behavior enables a variety of thermoelectric applications that do not require a heterojunction between two different materials. In this work, we investigate ADCP theoretically and derive a set of generic and quantitative criteria for identifying and predicting materials that exhibit ADCP. Specifically, by analyzing the thermopower for generic metals, semimetals, and semiconductors, we obtain transparent inequalities that are both necessary and sufficient for the emergence of ADCP. Moreover, we review known ADCP materials and verify that their band-structure characteristics and relaxation parameters are consistent with the inequalities derived here.

### [79] [Proximity Magnetism in Mn(Bi,Sb)2Te4-(Bi,Sb)2Te3/MnTe Natural Heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18935)
*Owen A. Vail,Shu-Wei Wang,Yasen Hou,Dinura Hettiarachchi,Jean-Felix Milette,Tim B. Eldred,Wenpei Gao,Wendy Sarney,Haile Ambaye,Jong Keum,Valeria Lauter,George J. de Coster,Matthew J. Gilbert,Don Heiman,Jagadeesh S. Moodera,Hang Chi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用扫描透射电子显微镜（scanning transmission electron microscopy）和深度敏感极化中子反射仪（depth-sensitive polarized neutron reflectometry）观察界面结构；通过磁输运实验（magnetotransport experiments）和量子磁性模拟（quantum magnetism simulations）研究磁性与拓扑性质。

Result: Mn(Bi,Sb)₂Te₄在自身奈尔温度（Neel temperature）20K以上仍能传递交换场，在(Bi,Sb)₂Te₃/MnTe界面产生反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect），界面奈尔温度超过200K；实现了无外磁场下的自旋轨道力矩（spin-orbit torque）翻转，临界电流密度仅为300 kA cm⁻²。

Conclusion: Mn(Bi,Sb)₂Te₄-(Bi,Sb)₂Te₃/MnTe的反铁磁耦合架构在硫族化物骨架上展现出独特的磁性与拓扑邻近效应，富含基础界面物理，在自旋电子学（spintronics）中具有实际应用潜力。

Abstract: Magnetic topological insulators and their heterostructures provide great opportunities in coupling band topology with nontrivial spin configuration for enhanced spintronic device performance as well as designing totally new magnetoelectric systems and functionalities. We find that Mn interdiffusion from MnTe when interfaced with (Bi,Sb)2Te3 stabilizes as self-organized Mn(Bi,Sb)2Te4 septuple lamellae amongst alternating (Bi,Sb)2Te3 quintuple layers, as observed using scanning transmission electron microscopy and depth-sensitive polarized neutron reflectometry. We further demonstrate a valuable combination of magnetic and topological orders in these naturally formed Mn(Bi,Sb)2Te4-(Bi,Sb)2Te3 heterostructures that are exchange coupled with MnTe. Magnetotransport experiments and quantum magnetism simulations reveal that, above its own Neel temperature TN of 20 K, Mn(Bi,Sb)2Te4 mediates the exchange field leading to an anomalous Hall effect at the (Bi,Sb)2Te3/MnTe interface, with an enhanced interfacial TN exceeding 200 K. This novel magnetic interface in turn allows a robust and deterministic spin-orbit torque switching without an external magnetic field at a low critical current density of 300 kA cm-2. The antiferromagnetically coupled architecture of Mn(Bi,Sb)2Te4-(Bi,Sb)2Te3/MnTe, featuring unique magnetic and topological proximity effects across a chalcogenide backbone, is rich in fundamental interface physics and holds potential for practical applications in spintronics.

### [80] [Magnetic Polarons Enable Exceptional Magnetocaloric Response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18938)
*Joshua Ancheta,Caeli Benyacko,Fanghao Zhang,Stephen D. Wilson,Bolin Liao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统磁热材料通常受限于磁熵与磁场响应性之间的权衡约束。本研究旨在探索能够缓解这一约束的新机制，以提升磁热性能。

Method: 以EuB₆为模型系统，结合热力学和磁性测量方法，研究居里温度附近出现的纳米尺度铁磁簇对磁场诱导熵塌缩的增强效应。

Result: EuB₆表现出巨大的低温磁热响应，在技术上重要的10-40 K范围内同时具有大的等温熵变和绝热温度变化。磁性极化子通过其大有效磁矩和小尺寸动态涨落，实现了高效的磁场响应性和保留的熵。

Conclusion: 磁性极化子为优化磁热性能提供了一条未被充分探索的途径，中等磁性长度尺度（intermediate magnetic length scale）应作为高性能低温冷却材料的设计原则。

Abstract: Magnetocaloric materials are typically limited by a trade-off between magnetic entropy and field responsiveness. Here we show that magnetic polarons provide an intermediate regime that mitigates this constraint and enables an exceptional magnetocaloric response. Using EuB$_6$ as a model system, we combine thermodynamic and magnetic measurements to demonstrate that nanoscale ferromagnetic clusters emerging near the Curie temperature strongly enhance the field-induced entropy collapse. These clusters possess large effective moments that respond efficiently to applied fields while retaining substantial entropy due to their small size and dynamic fluctuations. As a result, EuB$_6$ exhibits a giant cryogenic magnetocaloric response, with both large isothermal entropy change and adiabatic temperature change in the technologically important 10-40 K range. Our results identify magnetic polarons as an underexplored route for optimizing magnetocaloric performance and establish an intermediate magnetic length scale as a design principle for high-performance cryogenic cooling materials.

Furthermore, Energy Dispersive X-ray Analysis (EDAX) provides the richness of carbon (C) in graphene as well as in the micro-oval structure. *Anzar Ali,Md Ezaz Hasan Khan,Mahmoud Abdel-Hafiez*

Motivation: 过渡金属二硫化物展现出广泛的半导体、金属、关联和拓扑电子态，这些态源于晶格结构、维度和电子自由度之间的强耦合。在这些材料中，晶体生长不仅是制备步骤，更是建立化学势、缺陷分布、多型稳定性和亚稳相可达性的热力学边界条件。

Method: 该综述发展了统一的热力学和动力学框架，将生长条件与相稳定性、缺陷能量学和微观结构联系起来。作者考察了化学势约束如何定义稳定性窗口，过饱和度和质量传输机制如何控制成核和形貌，以及非平衡路径如何实现动力学俘获和多型选择。

Result: 通过将块体和薄膜合成方法（包括化学气相传输、助熔剂生长、物理气相传输、溶剂辅助结晶、化学气相沉积和分子束外延）置于共同的热力学和动力学图谱中，阐明了不同生长机制如何产生特征性的无序分布和结构相。

Conclusion: 该综述通过明确连接合成变量与电荷密度波序、超导性、能带拓扑和关联效应，确立了晶体生长作为决定实验中实现的有效电子哈密顿量的核心参数。这一视角为改善可重复性和指导层状材料中涌现量子相的确定性控制提供了物理基础框架。

Abstract: Transition metal dichalcogenides exhibit a wide range of semiconducting, metallic, correlated, and topological electronic states that arise from strong coupling between lattice structure, dimensionality, and electronic degrees of freedom. In these materials, crystal growth is not merely a preparative step but a thermodynamic boundary condition that establishes chemical potentials, defect populations, polytype stability, and access to metastable phases. As a result, synthesis determines the structural and defect landscape from which collective electronic behavior emerges.
  In this Review, we develop a unified thermodynamic and kinetic framework that connects growth conditions to phase stability, defect energetics, and microstructure. We examine how chemical potential constraints define stability windows, how supersaturation and mass-transport regimes govern nucleation and morphology, and how nonequilibrium pathways enable kinetic trapping and polymorph selection. Bulk and thin-film synthesis approaches, including chemical vapor transport, flux growth, physical vapor transport, solvent-assisted crystallization, chemical vapor deposition, and molecular beam epitaxy, are placed within a common thermodynamic and kinetic map to clarify how distinct growth regimes produce characteristic disorder profiles and structural phases.
  By explicitly linking synthesis variables to charge-density-wave order, superconductivity, band topology, and correlation effects, this Review establishes crystal growth as a central parameter in determining the effective electronic Hamiltonian realized in experiment. This perspective provides a physically grounded framework for improving reproducibility and guiding deterministic control of emergent quantum phases in layered materials.

### [83] [Electronic-Entropy-Driven Crossover to Close-Packed Phases in Transition Metals under Strong Electronic Excitation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19222)
*S. Azadi,S. M. Vinko,A. Principi,T. D. Kuehne,M. S. Bahramy*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 研究发现电子熵（electronic entropy）可在固定密度下驱动金属的固-固相变，揭示了高温下结构稳定性向密堆积相（fcc为主，hcp次之）收敛的普适规律，为极端电子激发条件下的相稳定性提供了统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统金属固-固相变（solid-solid phase transition）主要受密度变化或外压控制，本研究旨在探索电子熵作为独立热力学控制参数对结构稳定性的影响，特别是在固定密度条件下驱动相变的能力。

Method: 采用有限温度密度泛函理论（finite-temperature density functional theory）构建了15种金属的压力-温度相图，涵盖hcp、fcc和bcc基态结构；对锰（manganese）进行详细分析，使用Hubbard U修正的自旋相关计算来研究磁性、电子局域化和晶格稳定性的相互作用。

Result: 所有系统均表现出共同的高温响应：结构稳定性向以密堆积相（close-packed phases）为主、fcc占主导、hcp为次要相、bcc稳定性显著抑制的简化流形（reduced manifold）坍缩；电子熵产生显著的热电子热压（hot-electron thermal pressure），在固定密度下驱动结构重排，产生类似静水压缩的晶格动力学效应。

Conclusion: 电子熵是金属结构转变的基本热力学控制参数，其驱动的熵致交叉（entropy-driven crossover）在强电子激发下逐渐消除基态结构特异性，为理解极端电子激发条件下的相稳定性提供了统一框架。

Abstract: Solid-solid phase transitions in metals are traditionally governed by changes in density or external pressure. Here, we show that electronic entropy alone can control structural stability and drive phase transitions at fixed density across transition metals. Using finite-temperature density functional theory, we construct pressure-temperature phase diagrams for 15 metals spanning hcp, fcc, and bcc-ground-state structures. Despite their diverse ground-state behavior, all systems exhibit a common high-temperature response: structural stability collapses toward a reduced manifold dominated by close-packed phases, with fcc emerging as the predominant structure, hcp persisting as a secondary phase, and bcc stability strongly suppressed. This identifies a robust entropy-driven crossover that progressively erases ground-state structural specificity under strong electronic excitation. To elucidate the microscopic origin of this behavior, we perform a detailed analysis of manganese, where spin-dependent calculations with a Hubbard U correction capture the interplay between magnetism, electronic localization, and lattice stability. At low temperatures, phase competition is governed by magnetic order and on-site Coulomb interactions, whereas increasing electronic temperature leads to demagnetization, phonon hardening, and the emergence of an entropy-dominated regime consistent with the universal trends. We show that electronic entropy generates a substantial hot-electron thermal pressure that modifies interatomic forces and drives structural rearrangements at fixed density, producing lattice-dynamical effects analogous to hydrostatic compression. These results establish electronic entropy as a fundamental thermodynamic control parameter for structural transformations in metals and provide a unified framework for understanding phase stability under extreme electronic excitation.

Such devices are difficult to scale up with precision and operate with long-term stability. Here, we show that a micrometer size pore, generally expected to exhibit a linear ion transport, can display a pronounced memory effect, if its rim is wrapped by strongly curved and tightly stacked graphene. We attribute the observation to slow ion dynamics confined in the rippled graphene edges. The devices are easy to scale up and integrate into fluidic circuits. The memory effect is ion-selective and exhibits long endurance comparable to the lifetime of synaptic proteins, which enables reversible modification of the conductance states using programmable voltage spikes and various electrolytes over a long time, akin to biological synaptic plasticity. Our results highlight nanoscale morphology of the pore wall as an important parameter regulating ion transport and indicate that the stringent nanoconfinement for ionic memory can be lifted from restricting the pore size to designing its rim structure. Our results reveal that electric-field-induced Poole-Frenkel (PF) emission, localized by patterned oxygen vacancies, plays a decisive role in redistributing the internal electric field to trigger a deterministic Mott transition. Furthermore, we observe that the coupling of thermal and elastic energies governs a discrete domain evolution, characterized by step-wise and period-doubling configurational resets, which is a hallmark of non-equilibrium phase dynamics in constrained geometries. By integrating experimental imaging with phase-field simulations, we establish a comprehensive framework for the electrically-driven IMT and predict sub-100-ps switching kinetics. These findings provide a fundamental basis for the rational design of ultrafast, low-energy functional devices through nanoscale defect and strain engineering in correlated systems.

Here we introduce Experimental X-ray Diffraction Integrated Transformer (EXIT), a multimodal transformer for sample-aware prediction of MOF properties that combines MOFid with X-ray diffraction (XRD). *Erwin Hueger,Daniel Uxa,Lars Doerrer,Jochen Stahn,Harald Schmidt*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究引入基于同位素多层膜作为活性材料的方法，利用operando中子反射法（operando neutron reflectometry）实时追踪电极体积变化。使用natGe-73Ge多层膜作为模型系统，通过同位素调制在中子反射谱中产生布拉格峰（Bragg peak），该方法仅对电极活性材料内部的体积变化敏感，排除了电池副反应的影响。

Conclusion: 该方法能够直接从布拉格峰的散射矢量位置推导出体积变化与Li含量x的函数关系，无需拟合复杂的反射谱。这为实时监测锂离子电池电极材料的体积变化提供了一种有效工具，有助于深入理解电池性能与安全性的关系。

Abstract: This study reports on advancements in operando characterization of volume changes in lithium-ion battery (LIB) electrode materials during electrochemical cycling. Volume changes are crucial for LIB operation because they are related to the amount of stored energy as well as LIB integrity, performance, and safety. The study introduces a method based on isotope multilayers as active material to track the intrinsic modification of electrode volume in real time under operating conditions with operando neutron reflectometry. A natGe-73Ge multilayer film is used as a model system to measure the volume change of amorphous germanium electrodes during charging and discharging. Isotope modulation produces a Bragg peak in the neutron reflectivity pattern, sensitive only to the modification of volume within the active material of the electrode. Battery side reactions, such as the growth and reduction of the solid-electrolyte interphase is excluded. Using this method, the volume modification as a function of Li content x in LixGe can easily be derived from the scattering vector position of the Bragg peak without fitting numerous complex reflectivity patterns. The experiments show a reversible volume change of amorphous germanium of up to 250 percent for x = 3, which appears to be largely independent of current density, cycle number, and the thickness of the individual Ge layers. Also, there are tentative indications that the crystallization and re-amorphization of LixGe are not influencing the volume change.

### [90] [Electronic structure and oxidation states in high-pressure synthesized isostructural CeCN$_5$ and TbCN$_5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19629)
*Amanda Ehn,Florian Trybel,Talha Bin Masood,Leonid V. Pourovskii,Igor A. Abrikosov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，结合DFT+U和DFT+DMFT方法，分析了极端压力下合成的同构化合物CeCN₅和TbCN₅的电子性质，揭示了铈和铽的不同氧化态（4+ vs 3+）导致绝缘体与金属的差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解稀土元素中4f电子的行为是凝聚态物理的基本问题之一。研究旨在探索极端压力下合成的同构镧系碳氮化合物（LnCN）中4f电子行为与结构复杂性之间的相互作用。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（Density Functional Theory, DFT）计算，在静态DFT+U框架中考虑局域4f态之间的在位库仑排斥。DFT+U结果与准原子（Hubbard-I）近似下的DFT+动态平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory, DMFT）计算进行交叉验证。

Result: 尽管CeCN₅和TbCN₅是同构化合物，但铈和铽表现出不同的氧化态（分别为4+和3+），导致截然不同的电子性质：前者为绝缘体，后者为金属。铈向聚合C-N网络贡献的额外电子分布在整个网络中，导致CeCN₅的键长相比TbCN₅发生改变。

Conclusion: 高压下的镧系碳氮化合物（LnCN）为探索4f电子行为与结构复杂性之间的相互作用提供了独特平台。聚合C-N网络能够适应同构镧系化合物中不同的氧化态。

Abstract: Understanding the behavior of 4$f$ electrons in materials containing rare earth elements is one of the fundamental questions within condensed matter physics. In this work the electronic properties of isostructural CeCN$_5$ and TbCN$_5$, both recently synthesized at extreme pressure, are investigated using Density Functional Theory (DFT) calculations. We include the on-site Coulomb repulsion between localized 4$f$ states within the static DFT+U framework; the DFT+U results are cross-checked with DFT+dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT) calculations within the quasi-atomic (Hubbard-I) approximation. Despite CeCN$_5$ and TbCN$_5$ being isostructural compounds Ce and Tb show different oxidation states, 4+ and 3+ respectively. This leads to distinctly different electronic properties: the former compound is an insulator, while the latter is a metal. An extra electron which is donated by Ce to the polymeric C-N network is distributed across the network. This leads to a modification of the bond length in CeCN$_5$ compared to TbCN$_5$. Still, the polymeric C-N networks can accommodate the different oxidation states in isostructural lanthanide-carbon-nitrogen (LnCN) compounds. Our results underline that LnCN compounds under high pressure offer a unique platform for probing the interplay between 4$f$-electron behavior and structural complexity.

</details>


### [91] [Atomic-scale origin of charge density wave-driven metal-semiconductor transition in an incommensurately modulated metal-organic framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19640)
*Ling Zhang,Zeyue Zhang,Liu He,Bin Jiang,Yingchao Wang,Jiaxiang Zhang,Huimin Qi,Chao Zhang,Jinkun Guo,Hao Chen,Yunlong Fan,Yanran Shen,Hongli Jia,Guobao Li,Yu-Qing Zheng,Julius J. Oppenheim,Tianyang Chen,Jian Wang,Lei Sun,Junliang Sun,Jin-Hu Dou*
