<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金属有机框架（metal-organic frameworks, MOF）中的本征非公度电荷密度波（incommensurate charge density wave）一直缺乏直接证据，需要建立原子尺度结构调制与宏观电子性质之间的明确关联。

Method: 以高质量Pr3HHTP2单晶为模型体系，通过变温单晶X射线衍射（temperature-dependent single-crystal X-ray diffraction）在100 K下精确解析了非公度调制结构（调制矢量q = 0.39143(12) c*）。

Result: 首次在导电金属有机框架中观察到可逆的金属-半导体转变（reversible metal-semiconductor transition）约在350 K发生，该转变与结构调制的消失完全同步，证实了晶格畸变的电子起源。客体水分子通过协同调控连接体的相对旋转和层间距来稳定调制相。

Conclusion: 该工作为金属有机框架中一维电荷密度波（one-dimensional charge density wave）建立了具体的实验判据，并为探究耦合的电子-晶格调制提供了理想平台。

Abstract: The intrinsic incommensurate charge density wave in metal-organic frameworks has remained elusive due to the lack of direct evidence linking atomic-scale structural modulation to macroscopic electronic properties. Using high-quality Pr3HHTP2 (HHTP = 2,3,6,7,10,11-hexahydroxytriphenylene) single crystals as a model system, we precisely resolve, for the first time, the incommensurately modulated structure of a conductive metal-organic framework at 100 K (modulation vector q = 0.39143(12) c*) via temperature-dependent single-crystal X-ray diffraction. The subsequent observation of a reversible metal-semiconductor transition around 350 K, which perfectly synchronizes with the disappearance of the structural modulation, provides convincing evidence for the electronic origin of the lattice distortion. Guest water molecules stabilize the modulated phase by synergistically regulating the relative rotation of the linkers and the interlayer spacing, thereby optimizing the inter-linker interactions. This work establishes a concrete experimental criterion for one-dimensional charge density wave in metal-organic frameworks and provides an ideal platform for probing coupled electronic-lattice modulations.

*Cuiju Yu,Jose L. Lado*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然过渡金属基的d波交变磁体已被广泛提出，但石墨烯结构中的碳基交变磁体仍然难以实现，尽管石墨烯纳米结构中的磁性已被广泛证实。研究旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 结合第一性原理方法和原子紧束缚模型，建立了对称性指导的设计原则，用于在石墨烯反点超晶格中设计i波交变磁体。

Result: 研究证明了特定单层和双层石墨烯超晶格中交变磁态的出现，展示了由二维石墨烯反点超晶格本征磁不稳定性引起的相互作用诱导的i波交变磁分裂。

Abstract: Altermagnets feature unconventional magnetism due to their momentum-dependent spin splitting purely driven by magnetic order, for which a variety of transition-metal-based d-wave altermagnets have been proposed. However, carbon-based altermagnets in graphene structures remain elusive, even though magnetism in graphene nanostructures has been widely demonstrated. Here, we establish a symmetry-guided design principle to engineer i-wave altermagnets in graphene antidot superlattices and demonstrate the emergence of altermagnetic states in specific monolayer and bilayer graphene superlattices. By combining first principles methods and atomistic tight binding models, we show the appearance of an interaction-induced i-wave altermagnetic splitting, stemming from the intrinsic magnetic instability of 2D graphene antidot superlattices. Our work establishes a strategy to engineer i-wave altermagnetism in a graphene platform, putting forward a carbon-based platform for altermagnetic spintronics.

### [93] [Signatures of Quantum Gravity In Relativistic Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18625)
*Soham Sen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在线性化量子引力框架下研究引力子对物质系统的影响，提出了基于引力子-物质相互作用的探测器模型，包括两粒子模型和玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体系统，旨在探测引力子诱导的信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索引力子对物质系统的影响，并开发能够探测引力子信号的探测器模型。通过量子引力与物质系统的相互作用，为实验验证量子引力效应提供理论框架。

Method: 采用线性化量子引力理论，首先构建两粒子模型探测器系统，该系统与量子化引力涨落相互作用且服从广义不确定原理（GUP）。随后考虑系统置于谐振势阱中，研究引力子的受激吸收和自发发射。最后使用相对论性标量玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）替代标准物质探测器，研究其对入射引力子的响应。

Result: 研究暗示了量子引力诱导的记忆效应存在，并获得了量子引力修正的不确定关系。提出了基于引力子介导的纠缠BEC退相干机制的引力子探测器模型，为在几年内探测引力子诱导信号提供了理论可能性。

Conclusion: 该论文在线性化量子引力框架下建立了多种引力子探测器模型，从简单两粒子系统到复杂BEC系统，为实验探测引力子效应提供了理论方案，并揭示了量子引力可能诱导的新物理效应。

Abstract: In this thesis, we have used a linearized quantum gravity setting to investigate the effects of gravitons on matter systems. Based on the graviton-matter interaction, we have then proposed detector models that may be able to pick up graviton-induced signatures in a matter of a few years. We start with the simple model of a two-particle model detector system interacting with quantized gravitational fluctuations while the detector degrees of freedom obey the generalized uncertainty principle (GUP). For the first part we have hinted at the existence of quantum gravity induced memory effect as well as obtained a quantum gravity modified uncertainty relation. For the next part of the thesis, we have mainly focused on the phenomenological aspects of a linearized quantum gravity theory. For the initial phenomenological model, we have considered the same two-particle model detector system interacting with gravitational fluctuations where the entire set-up is placed inside a harmonic trap potential and looked at the stimulated absorption and spontaneous emission scenario for gravitons. In order to inspect a more involved phenomenological aspect, instead of the standard matter-detector system, we make use of a relativistic scalar Bose-Einstein condensate (BEC) and investigated the response of the BEC based model towards incoming gravitons and proposed a graviton detector based on graviton mediated decoherence from entangled BECs.

### [94] [Quantum-Deformed Phase-Space Geometry and Emergent Inflation in Effective Four-Dimensional Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18647)
*Swapnil Kumar Singh,Saleh O. Allehabi,Azzah A. Alshehri,Mahmoud Nasar,Abdel Nasser Tawfik*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文发展了一种相空间（phase-space）方法研究量子变形引力（quantum-deformed gravity），并将其应用于重新分析宇宙暴胀动力学和量子引力。通过将构造从余切丛（cotangent bundle）约化到有效四维时空结构，建立了量子变形相空间几何与有效暴胀动力学之间的协变联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在发展一种相空间方法来研究量子变形引力，并将其应用于重新分析宇宙暴胀动力学和量子引力。通过建立量子变形相空间几何与有效四维时空结构之间的联系，探索量子引力效应如何编码为相空间几何的变形。

Method: 方法从余切丛（cotangent bundle）开始构造，通过零齐次标量（zero-homogeneous scalar）变形引力哈密顿量，该标量由投影动量方向（projective momentum directions）和量子相空间性质决定。这诱导出非零锥域（non-null conic domain）上的各向异性哈密顿几何（anisotropic Hamilton geometry），通过截面拉回程序（section-pullback procedure）获得有效时空度规。

Result: 在均匀各向同性（homogeneous and isotropic）情形下，拉回一致地约化为由标量变形场（scalar deformation field）控制的共形变形FLRW几何。推导了相应的修正爱因斯坦方程、克莱因-戈尔登方程、测地线偏离方程和雷乔杜里方程。构建了暴胀背景动力学、慢滚机制、e-折叠数以及标量和张量扰动。

Conclusion: 该模型建立了量子变形相空间几何与有效四维暴胀动力学之间的协变且可控的联系。研究表明，量子引力效应可以一致地编码为投影相空间几何的变形，有效时空度规仅在截面依赖的约化后出现。主导的暴胀修正源于相空间变形及其时间依赖性，而宇宙扰动的正则量子化在适当的背景重定义后保持标准形式。

Abstract: A phase-space approach to quantum-deformed gravity is developed. Following its reduction to an effective four-dimensional spacetime structure, we utilize it in reanalyzing the cosmic inflationary dynamics and quantum gravity. The construction starts on cotangent bundle, where the gravitational Hamiltonian is deformed by a zero-homogeneous scalar determined by projective momentum directions and quantum phase-space properties. This induces an anisotropic Hamilton geometry on a non-null conic domain, from which an effective spacetime metric is obtained through a section-pullback procedure. In the homogeneous and isotropic sector, the pullback consistently reduces to a conformally deformed FLRW geometry governed by a scalar deformation field. We derive the corresponding modified Einstein, Klein-Gordon, geodesic-deviation, and Raychaudhuri equations. This allows for the construction of inflationary background dynamics, slow-roll regime, number of e-folds, as well as scalar and tensor perturbations. The resulting framework shows that leading inflationary corrections arise from the phase-space deformation and its time dependence, while the canonical quantization of cosmological perturbations remains standard after suitable background redefinitions. In this way, the model provides a covariant and controlled link between quantum-deformed phase-space geometry and effective four-dimensional inflationary dynamics. The present construction shows that effects of quantum gravity can be consistently encoded as a deformation of projective phase-space geometry, from which an effective spacetime metric emerges only after a section-dependent reduction.

</details>


### [95] [Hawking area law in quantum gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18669)
*Gianluca Calcagni*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究证明，若假设霍金面积定律（Hawking area law）精确成立，则LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA观测到的黑洞合并事件对量子引力理论施加了严格限制，显著简化了Stelle引力和非局域量子引力理论的参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探讨LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA（LVK）对霍金面积定律的验证对量子引力理论的影响。若该定律被假设为精确成立，则可为量子引力理论提供强有力的约束条件。

Method: 研究方法基于分析LVK观测到的黑洞合并事件在两类量子引力理论框架下的可解释性：局部Stelle引力和具有完整或分数形式因子的非局域量子引力理论。研究考察了这些理论产生观测信号所需的特定条件。

Result: 研究结果表明，观测到的合并事件仅能在非常严格的条件下产生：要么通过奇异的Ricci平直黑洞，要么通过可能规则的黑洞，但要求作用量中不含$R^2$和(Riemann)${}^2$项，引力子传播子无额外实极点，且其谱表示为正。这显著简化了此类理论的模糊性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了经典标准黑洞熵-面积定律是霍金面积定律的推论，并为Barrow分形黑洞提供了严格的实现方案。这些发现代表了对此类量子引力理论模糊性的最强简化。

Abstract: We show that the LIGO--Virgo--KAGRA (LVK) verification of Hawking area law carries profound consequences for quantum gravity if such a law is postulated to hold exactly. The observed mergers can be produced in local Stelle gravity and in nonlocal quantum-gravity theories with entire or fractional form factors either by (i) singular Ricci-flat black holes or (ii) possibly regular classical black holes under very restrictive conditions: absence of $R^2$ and (Riemann)${}^2$ terms in the action, absence of extra real poles in the graviton propagator, and positivity of its spectral representation. To date, this is the strongest simplification of the ambiguities of this class of theories. We also prove that the classical standard black-hole entropy-area law holds as a consequence of Hawking area law, and provide a rigorous realization of Barrow's fractal black holes otherwise.

</details>


### [96] [Beyond Three Terms: Continued Fractions for Rotating Black Holes in Modified Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18680)
*Georgios Karikos,Jayana A. Saes,Pratik Wagle,Nicolás Yunes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种通用约化方案，将任意标量和矩阵N项递推关系映射为三项形式，从而将连分式方法扩展到修正引力中的广泛微扰问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞环降（black-hole ringdown）为强引力提供了精确探针，但最准确工具之一的Leaver连分式方法需要三项递推关系。在广义相对论之外和非Kerr时空（non-Kerr spacetimes）中，微扰方程的Frobenius展开通常产生高阶递推关系，且常伴有级数系数间的耦合，阻碍了Leaver方法的直接应用。

Method: 本文开发了一种通用约化方案（general reduction scheme），可将任意标量和矩阵N项递推关系映射为三项形式。该框架将连分式扩展到修正引力中的广泛微扰问题，并应用于动态Chern-Simons引力（dynamical Chern-Simons gravity）中慢速旋转黑洞的准正规模（quasinormal-mode）谱计算。

Result: 对于动态Chern-Simons引力中的慢速旋转黑洞，极向扇区（polar sector）产生16项解耦标量递推关系，轴向扇区（axial sector）产生12项耦合矩阵递推关系。应用约化方案后，两个系统都能用连分式求解。对于基本(ℓ,m)=(2,2)模式，结果与基于特征值微扰和度量/谱方法的独立计算在参数范围内良好吻合。

Conclusion: 该框架为超越标准三项设置的精确环降计算提供了稳健实用的途径，支持利用当前和未来引力波观测进行引力测试。扩展后的连分式方法能够处理更广泛的微扰问题，特别是在修正引力理论中。

Abstract: Black-hole ringdown offers a clean probe of strong gravity, but one of its most accurate tools--Leaver's continued-fraction method--requires a three-term recurrence relation. Beyond general relativity, and more generally in non-Kerr spacetimes, Frobenius expansions of the perturbation equations generically produce higher-order recurrence relations and, often, couplings among the series coefficients, obstructing a direct application of Leaver's method. Here we develop a general reduction scheme that maps arbitrary scalar and matrix $N$-term recurrence relations to a three-term form, thereby extending continued fractions to a broad class of perturbation problems in modified gravity. As an application, we compute the quasinormal-mode spectrum of slowly-rotating black holes in dynamical Chern-Simons gravity, where the polar sector yields a 16-term, decoupled, scalar recurrence relation, and the axial sector yields a 12-term, coupled, matrix recurrence relation. After applying our reduction scheme, both systems can be solved with continued fractions. For the fundamental $(\ell,m)=(2,2)$ mode, our results agree well with independent calculations based on eigenvalue-perturbation and metric/spectral methods across the parameter range studied. This framework provides a robust and practical route to precision ringdown calculations beyond the standard three-term setting and supports tests of gravity with current and future gravitational-wave observations.

</details>


### [97] [String-inspired Gauss-Bonnet Gravity Inflation and ACT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18861)
*S. D. Odintsov,V. K. Oikonomou,Pyotr Tsyba,Olga Razina,Dauren Rakhatov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究对无鬼弦启发的$f(R,\mathcal{G})$模型进行了系统性观测验证，通过贝叶斯MCMC分析比较了十六种模型与Planck 2018和ACT数据，发现哈勃参数化形式而非耦合函数决定数据偏好，所有模型均能产生与CMB一致的标量扰动红谱倾斜。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究使用现象学参数选择确认了该理论框架的可行性，但缺乏系统性观测验证。本研究首次通过贝叶斯MCMC分析，系统性地将无鬼弦启发模型与Planck 2018和Atacama Comsology Telescope观测数据进行对比验证。

Method: 采用Cobaya代码进行贝叶斯MCMC分析，构建了十六种扩展模型：将四种哈勃参数化类型与幂律、指数、混合及逆对数耦合函数$h(χ)$组合。混合耦合$h(χ) = γe^{b_1χ}χ^{b_2}$允许在幂律和指数形式间插值，为控制不同暴胀阶段的高斯-博内贡献提供额外灵活性。

Result: 所有十六种模型均能产生与宇宙微波背景观测一致的标量扰动红谱倾斜，在$N = 60$ e-fold时得到$n_s \approx 0.97$。数据偏好系统性取决于哈勃参数化选择而非耦合函数。参数$μ\approx0.1$在所有配置中保持稳定，表明其在无鬼形式体系中的基本作用。

Conclusion: 该研究首次对无鬼弦启发$f(R,\mathcal{G})$模型进行了系统性观测验证，确认了理论框架与当前宇宙学观测的一致性。哈勃参数化形式对数据偏好的决定性作用以及稳定参数$μ$的发现，为理解该形式体系的基本特征提供了重要线索。

Abstract: In this article we present a systematic observational verification of the ghost-free string-inspired $f(R,\mathcal{G})$ model, where the Gauss-Bonnet invariant is non-minimally coupled to an auxiliary scalar field $χ$ through the coupling function $h(χ)$. Previous studies confirmed the theoretical viability of this framework using phenomenological parameter choices. In this work, for the first time, a systematic comparison with observational data from Planck 2018 and the Atacama Comsology Telescope is carried out via a Bayesian MCMC analysis using the Cobaya code. We explore an extended set of sixteen models constructed from four types of the Hubble parameter combined with power-law, exponential, hybrid, and inverse logarithmic coupling functions $h(χ)$. The hybrid coupling $h(χ) = γe^{b_1χ}χ^{b_2}$, introduced in this context, allows for interpolation between the power-law and exponential forms, providing additional flexibility in controlling the Gauss-Bonnet contribution at different stages of inflation. All sixteen models reproduce the red spectral tilt of scalar perturbations consistent with CMB observations, yielding $n_s \approx 0.97$ at $N = 60$ e-folds. We find that the preference for the dataset is systematically determined by the choice of Hubble parametrization rather than by the coupling function. The parameter $μ\approx0.1$ remains stable in all configurations, suggesting its fundamental role within the ghost-free formalism.

</details>


### [98] [The Flat Critical Branch Between Nariai and Bertotti-Robinson Geometries as a Solution of Cosmological Einstein-Maxwell Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19168)

We focus on the critical configuration for which the Lorentzian curvature vanishes. At this balance point between the cosmological curvature and the Maxwell stress, the longitudinal geometry becomes exactly flat while the transverse sphere radius is fixed algebraically by the conserved flux. We refer to this geometry as the critical Maxwell flux string: a homogeneous flux-supported geometry curved only in the transverse directions and invariant along a two-dimensional null worldvolume. It represents the algebraic midpoint interpolating between the Nariai $(dS_2\times S^2)$ and Bertotti-Robinson $(AdS_2\times S^2)$ spacetimes. A qualitative structural change occurs precisely at this midpoint. The spacetime is Petrov type-D with constant scalar curvature invariants, placing it in the degenerate Kundt/CSI class. Because the curvature structure reduces any polynomial rank-two tensor to a linear combination of the metric and the Maxwell stress tensor, the same configuration solves a broad class of algebraic higher-curvature gravity theories. In this sense, the critical flux string and its aligned deformations constitute almost universal solutions.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用正则分析（canonical analysis）方法，基于arXiv:2401.07307和arXiv:2010.07725的框架，设置Barbero参数β=0且不约束时移（lapse）和位移（shift）函数。通过场分解和场方程投影推导方程系统。

Conclusion: 所得框架与爱因斯坦方程的标准3+1分解完全一致，且不需要对时移和位移函数施加任何约束。该结果为圈量子引力形式向更高维度的推广提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We perform a canonical analysis of the Holst model for General Relativity, within the framework laid out in arXiv:2401.07307 and arXiv:2010.07725, distinguishing our approach by setting the Barbero parameter to $β=0$ and leaving the lapse and shift functions unconstrained. The $β= 0$ choice is of particular interest because it is viable across all dimensions, providing a necessary foundation for extending the Loop Quantum Gravity formalism beyond $3+1$ dimensions.
  Through field decomposition and the projection of the field equations, we derive a system of 37 equations (10 differential constraints, 21 algebraic constraints, and 6 evolution equations) exactly matching the 37 field components to be determined. Moreover, leaving the gauge unfixed reveals that three equations, which are typically identically satisfied under normal evolution, are actually differential constraints whose triviality depends on specific gauge choices. The resulting framework remains fully consistent with the standard $3+1$ decomposition of the Einstein equations without requiring any constraints on the lapse and shift functions.

### [100] [Extrinsic geometry and Hamiltonian analysis of symmetric teleparallel gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19310)
*Salvatore Capozziello,Dario Sauro*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在分析非度量性存在时叶状结构的性质，推导广义高斯-科达齐关系，并将其应用于非度量几何的远平行框架研究。这为理解非度量几何中的约束条件和动力学自由度提供了理论基础。

Result: 推导出完全一般性的广义高斯-科达齐关系，发现外禀对称二阶张量在非度量几何中扮演黎曼几何（Riemannian geometry）中外曲率（extrinsic curvature）的角色，且无其他几何对象能引入新的动力学自由度。获得了适定且定义良好的柯西问题（Cauchy problem）的边界项，并证明对称远平行等价广义相对论与黎曼几何对应理论具有相同数量的自由度。

Conclusion: 论文成功建立了非度量几何中叶状结构的完整理论框架，推导了广义高斯-科达齐关系，分析了变分原理中的边界项，并构建了对称远平行等价广义相对论的哈密顿量，证明该理论与黎曼几何版本具有相同的自由度数量。

Abstract: We analyze the properties of foliations in presence of non-metricity, deriving the generalized Gauss-Codazzi relations in full generality. These results are employed to study the teleparallel framework of non-metric geometry, obtaining constraints on the extrinsic and intrinsic tensors. In particular, an extrinsic symmetric two-tensor plays the role of the extrinsic curvature in Riemannian geometry, whereas no other geometric object can induce new dynamical degrees of freedom. Furthermore, we analyze the variational principle in presence of non-metricity, obtaining the boundary terms for the well-posed and well-defined Cauchy problem. Finally, we exploit the previous results to construct the Hamiltonian of the symmetric teleparallel equivalent of General Relativity, providing a proof that this theory shares the same number of degrees of freedom with its Riemannian counterpart.

### [101] [Quantum Spacetime, Quantum Gravity and Gravitized Quantum Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19418)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过论证时空的量子本质（包括经典时空的非对易对偶伴体）是量子理论内在概率性和固定玻恩规则（Born rule）的原因，提出在量子引力中量子理论被"引力化"为背景无关结构。

Result: 该提议暗示在大量子探针背景下存在内在的三重及更高阶干涉（intrinsic triple and higher-order interference），这为理解弦理论（string theory）、观测到的真空能量以及基本粒子质量提供了新视角。

Conclusion: 时空的量子本质是量子理论内在概率性和语境性的根源，量子引力将量子理论转化为背景无关结构，这一框架对理解弦理论、真空能量和粒子质量具有重要意义。

Abstract: General relativity is a background-independent theory of a dynamical classical spacetime geometry. Quantum theory is formulated in a classical spacetime, as an intrinsically probabilistic, contextual theory of non-classical, interfering probabilities, with a fixed Born rule for computing those probabilities. We argue that the quantum nature of spacetime, which includes a non-commutative dual companion to the (observed) classical spacetime, is the reason behind an intrinsically probabilistic and contextual nature of quantum theory, with the fixed Born rule. In quantum gravity, we claim, quantum theory is gravitized into a background-independent structure with dynamical and contextual quantum probabilities. This proposal implies intrinsic triple and higher-order interference in the context of massive quantum probes, which sheds light on string theory and the observed vacuum energy as well as the masses of elementary particles.

### [102] [Viability of Big Bang Nucleosynthesis in Some Generalized Horizon Entropies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19545)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是检验从广义视界熵导出的宇宙学模型在大爆炸核合成（Big Bang Nucleosynthesis, BBN）框架下的可行性。需要评估这些模型在早期宇宙物理过程中的一致性，特别是与观测到的轻元素丰度是否相符。

Method: 研究方法包括分析广义视界熵宇宙学模型导致的膨胀率偏差，并利用BBN约束推导模型参数界限。具体通过冻结温度（freeze-out temperature）、氦（helium）和氘（deuterium）丰度数据来建立参数约束条件。

Result: 结果显示冻结条件提供了最严格的参数约束，而氦和氘的界限在所有模型中保持一致。尽管锂（lithium）约束未得到满足，但这归因于已知的宇宙锂问题（cosmological lithium problem）。晚期宇宙加速所需的参数值完全位于BBN界限内，表明早期与晚期宇宙行为具有一致性。

Conclusion: 结论表明所考虑的广义视界熵宇宙学模型在大爆炸核合成框架内是可行的。早期宇宙的BBN约束与晚期宇宙加速行为之间的一致性得到证实，为这些模型提供了观测支持。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the viability of some cosmological models derived from generalized horizon entropies, using Big Bang Nucleosynthesis (BBN) constraints. By analyzing the deviations in the expansion rate, we derive bounds on the model parameters from freeze-out temperature, helium, and deuterium abundances. Our results show that the freeze-out condition provides the most stringent constraint, while helium and deuterium bounds remain consistent across all models. Although lithium constraints are not satisfied, this discrepancy is attributed to the well-known cosmological lithium problem. Furthermore, the parameter values required for late-time cosmic acceleration are found to lie well within the BBN bounds, demonstrating consistency between early- and late-Universe behavior. These results establish the viability of the considered models within the framework of BBN.

Abstract: Supernovae are one of the most promising gravitational wave sources. But, since the system of the supernovae is nearly spherically symmetric, the expected gravitational waves from them are relatively weak, compared to the case of the compact binary mergers. Thus, at least using the current gravitational wave detectors, only the gravitational waves from a supernova that occurred in our galaxy could be detected. To reliably extract information from gravitational waves originating from such a low event rate, thorough preparation is essential. However, because supernova gravitational waves strongly depend on model parameters, such as progenitor mass and the equation of state for dense matter, it may be difficult to extract physical properties even if the gravitational waves are detected. The universal relations between gravitational-wave signals and physical properties, independent of model parameters, are important for solving this difficulty. ### [104] [Quasinormal modes of charged covariant effective black holes with a cosmological constant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19577)

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the quasinormal modes of two covariant effective black holes characterized by the quantum parameter $ζ$, charge $Q$, and cosmological constant $Λ$, under the scalar perturbation. By employing the pseudo-spectral method, we numerically calculate the quasinormal frequencies and analyze the influence of $ζ$ on the spectra with respect to $Q$. Our results demonstrate that while the quantum parameter $ζ$ significantly modifies the quasinormal frequency spectrum, the non-monotonic behavior and overtone outbursts persist. Notably, the impact of quantum gravity on the overtone outbursts is not merely limited to enhancement or suppression; instead, it introduce additional spectral features. Furthermore, a comprehensive analysis of the full quasinormal mode spectrum reveals rich interactions between complex and purely imaginary modes, including damping-rate crossings and merging-splitting behavior. These phenomena typically accompany overtone outbursts in near-extremal regimes, suggesting a potential connection between mode interactions and overtone outbursts. This work emphasizes the necessity of analyzing the full quasinormal frequency spectrum rather than focussing solely on fundamental modes, and provides novel insights into its underlying spectral structures.

### [106] [Fundamental Cosmic Anisotropy and its Ramifications II: Perturbations in Bianchi spacetimes, and fixed in the Newtonian gauge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19706)

TL;DR: 该研究发展了广义Bianchi模型的线性扰动理论，推导了牛顿规范下的扰动方程，并应用于Einstein-de Sitter宇宙和Bianchi I宇宙的密度对比度公式化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准宇宙学模型面临日益增多的观测挑战，促使研究者探索可能的修正方案。本研究关注放弃宇宙各向同性（仅保持均匀性）的Bianchi模型，旨在通过研究其扰动特性来理解此类宇宙的观测特征。

Method: 研究发展了广义Bianchi模型的线性扰动理论，在使度规分量仅依赖于宇宙时间的框架下工作。推导了牛顿规范（Newtonian gauge）下任意度规的标量和纯张量扰动的能量密度、压力、动量密度和各向异性应力的扰动方程。

Result: 对于标量扰动，密度和压力方程被组合得到Bianchi模型中等价于Mukhanov-Sasaki方程的表达式。针对特定度规和流体流选择，还公式化了Bianchi模型的Friedmann方程。最终将结果应用于Einstein-de Sitter宇宙和Bianchi I宇宙的密度对比度公式化。

Abstract: The standard cosmological model is challenged by an ever-growing collection of observations, which invites (and stimulates) inquiry into possible additions and/or alterations. One such alteration comes from letting cosmic isotropy -- as demanded by the cosmological principle -- go, whilst maintaining only homogeneity. This study concerns Bianchi models, a class of anisotropic, homogeneous spacetimes, and in particular their perturbations. Knowledge of their properties under perturbations (such as allowed wavemodes) aids in understanding cosmological signatures of such universes, e.g. CMBs, and thus allows for comparsion to observation and the theory of the standard model. This study develops linear perturbation theory of general Bianchi models, by working in a frame such that metric components depend solely on (cosmic) time. Perturbation equations in the Newtonian gauge, but for arbitrary metric, are derived for energy density $ρ$, (relativistic) pressure $p$, momentum density $q$, and anisotropic stress $π$, for the case of scalar and pure tensor perturbations. For the former, the equations for density and pressure are combined to yield the equivalent of the Mukhanov-Sasaki equation for Bianchi models. For a specific choice of metric and fluid flow $u$, the Friedmann equations for Bianchi models are also formulated, as this knowledge is necessary to fully formulate the perturbation equations. Finally, the obtained results are applied to the formulations of density contrasts in an Einstein-de Sitter universe and a Bianchi I universe.

</details>


### [107] [Black holes of multiple horizons without mass inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.12646)
*Changjun Gao,Toktarbay Saken*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了双视界时空中的质量暴胀（mass inflation）现象，通过构建非线性麦克斯韦场下的多视界黑洞解，使内视界重合以消除表面引力，从而构造出无质量暴胀的多视界黑洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质量暴胀是双视界时空内视界附近发生的现象，会导致初始小扰动质量指数增长，表明黑洞内视界对扰动不稳定。鉴于质量暴胀由内视界表面引力决定，研究旨在寻找消除质量暴胀的黑洞解。

Method: 基于Carballo-Rubio等人的结论，即消除内视界表面引力可避免质量暴胀的指数增长特性，本文寻找非线性麦克斯韦场（nonlinear Maxwell field）下的多视界黑洞解。通过使内视界相互重合，使每个内视界的表面引力为零。

Result: 成功构造了无质量暴胀的多视界黑洞（black holes of multiple horizons without mass inflation）。通过使内视界重合消除了表面引力，从而避免了质量暴胀的指数增长特性。

Conclusion: 通过构建非线性麦克斯韦场下的多视界黑洞解，并使内视界重合以消除表面引力，可以有效构造出无质量暴胀的多视界黑洞，为解决内视界不稳定性问题提供了新途径。

Abstract: Mass inflation is a phenomenon happened in the vicinity of inner horizon in two-horizon spacetime. It is shown that the mass of initially small perturbations will grow exponentially as they approach the inner horizon. This implies that black hole inner horizon is unstable to the perturbations. In view of the fact that the mass inflation is determined by the surface gravity of inner horizon, Carballo-Rubio et al. showed that if one makes the surface gravity of inner horizon vanish, then the exponential growth character of mass inflation is not present. Basing on this conclusion, we look for the black hole solutions of multiple horizons with nonlinear Maxwell field. Then we make the inner horizons to coincide with each other such that the surface gravities of every inner horizon vanish. By this way, black holes of multiple horizons without mass inflation are constructed.

</details>

### [108] [Competition and coexistence of superconductivity and nematic order in a two-dimensional electron gas with quadrupolar interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18777)
*Nei Lopes,Guilherme da Silva do Vale,Daniel G. Barci*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究了二维电子气中超导性与向列序（nematic order）的相互作用，通过包含s波和d波配对通道的模型，揭示了不同相互作用强度下相图的竞争与共存关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解关联电子系统中超导性与向列序之间的相互作用，特别是在具有竞争性配对和四极前向散射相互作用的二维电子气中，探索这些有序态如何相互影响并形成复杂的相结构。

Method: 研究方法包括构建包含s波和d波超导通道的模型，计算平均场自由能密度，并通过求解一组耦合的自洽方程来确定相互作用强度和温度函数的相图。

Result: 研究结果显示：在零温下，向列序与d波超导强烈竞争，导致直接的一级相变；而与s波配对则允许共存相，其特征是具有均匀超导能隙的各向异性费米面。在有限温度下，四极相互作用促进了额外超导分量的出现，产生了s波、d波和向列序共存的区域。

Conclusion: 结论强调了对称性和相互作用强度在塑造相结构中的关键作用，并提供了一个描述关联电子系统中交织的向列和超导相的最小框架，为理解这些复杂有序态之间的相互作用提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We investigate the interplay between superconductivity and nematic order in a two-dimensional electron gas with competing pairing and quadrupolar forward-scattering interactions. The model includes both $s$-wave and $d$-wave superconducting channels. We compute the mean-field free energy density and determine the phase diagrams as functions of interaction strengths and temperature by solving a set of coupled self-consistent equations. At zero-temperature, we find that the nematic order competes strongly with $d$-wave superconductivity, leading to a direct first-order phase transition, while its interplay with $s$-wave pairing allows for a coexistence phase characterized by an anisotropic Fermi surface with a uniform superconducting gap. At finite-temperatures, quadrupolar interactions promote the emergence of additional superconducting components, giving rise to regimes where $s$-wave, $d$-wave, and nematic orders coexist. Our results highlight the role of symmetry and interaction strength in shaping the phase structure and provide a minimal framework to describe intertwined nematic and superconducting phases in correlated electron systems.

</details>


### [109] [Stripping Symmetry: Electrochemical Oxidation to a Superconducting Polar Metal in Au2Pb0.914P2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18843)
*Scott B. Lee,Stephanie R. Dulovic,Joseph W. Stiles,Xin Zhang,Fatmagül Katmer,Sudipta Chatterjee,Jaime Moya,Allana G. Iwanicki,Abby N. Neill,Chris Lygouras,Tieyan Chang,Tyrel M. McQueen,Yu-Sheng Chen,Leslie M. Schoop*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过电化学拓扑脱嵌（electrochemical topotactic deintercalation）从中心对称母体化合物Au₂PbP₂中移除Pb，制备出极性金属Au₂Pb₀.₉₁₄P₂，该材料在1.52 K以下转变为具有非中心对称超导间隙结构的II型超导体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极性金属（polar metals）和非中心对称超导体（noncentrosymmetric superconductors）极为罕见，但其破缺的反演对称性（broken inversion symmetry）能够产生混合单重态-三重态超导配对（mixed singlet-triplet superconducting pairing）等新兴电子现象。由于已知化合物中此类材料极少，需要超越传统晶体生长的合成策略来获取新实例。

Method: 采用电化学拓扑脱嵌（electrochemical topotactic deintercalation）方法从中心对称母体化合物Au₂PbP₂中移除Pb，通过同步辐射单晶X射线衍射（synchrotron single-crystal X-ray diffraction）解析完整的(3+1)D调制结构，并利用非线性电子输运（nonlinear electronic transport）确认极性归属。

Result: 成功制备出极性金属Au₂Pb₀.₉₁₄P₂，其结构锁定在极性非中心对称超空间群Ama2(01g)ss0。该材料在T_c = 1.52 K以下转变为II型超导体（type-II superconductor），其热容（heat capacity）和交流磁化率（AC susceptibility）均表现出幂律行为（power-law behavior），表明超导间隙结构受宿主晶格破缺的反演对称性调控。

Conclusion: 这项工作确立了电化学氧化（electrochemical oxidation）作为通过化学定向对称破缺（chemically directed symmetry-breaking）制备亚稳态非中心对称超导体的理性途径。部分Pb的移除触发了由二阶Jahn-Teller效应（second-order Jahn-Teller effect）和立体化学活性孤对电子（stereochemically active lone pairs）介导的协同电子与几何重排。

Abstract: Polar metals and noncentrosymmetric superconductors are exceptionally rare, yet their broken inversion symmetry can give rise to emergent electronic phenomena including mixed singlet-triplet superconducting pairing. As only a few such materials have been found among known compounds, accessing new examples requires synthetic strategies that go beyond conventional crystal growth. Here, we use electrochemical topotactic deintercalation to remove Pb from the centrosymmetric parent compound Au$_2$PbP$_2$, producing the polar metal Au$_2$Pb$_{0.914}$P$_2$. Unlike conventional chemical doping, this transformation actively drives structural symmetry-breaking: the partial removal of Pb triggers a cooperative electronic and geometric rearrangement, mediated by a second-order Jahn-Teller effect and stereochemically active lone pairs, that locks the product into a polar, noncentrosymmetric superspace group Ama2(01g)ss0. We solve the complete (3+1)D modulated structure by synchrotron single-crystal X-ray diffraction and confirm the polar assignment through nonlinear electronic transport. Below T$_c$ = 1.52 K, Au$_2$Pb$_{0.914}$P$_2$ becomes a type-II superconductor whose heat capacity and AC susceptibility both exhibit power-law behavior, suggestive of a gap structure governed by the broken inversion symmetry of the host lattice. This work establishes electrochemical oxidation as a rational route to metastable noncentrosymmetric superconductors through chemically directed symmetry-breaking.

</details>


### [110] [AngstromPro: A versatile software for massive N-dimensional STM data management, visualization and in-depth analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18962)
*Huiyu Zhao,Jiahao Yan,Catherine Dawson,Haitao Yang,Hong-Jun Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: AngstromPro是一款基于Python的开源软件，专为扫描隧道显微镜（STM）大数据集的管理、可视化和分析而设计。该软件采用模块化架构，分离图形界面与数据处理算法，整合了多种标准和新近发展的STM数据分析方法，旨在提升分析效率、可靠性和可重复性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扫描隧道显微镜（STM）数据分析工作流程通常较为分散，缺乏统一的平台来整合数据处理、维护详细处理历史，并支持新方法的快速开发。现有工具往往难以兼顾易用性、可扩展性和算法的最新发展。

Method: AngstromPro采用模块化架构设计，包含顶层模块管理全局变量列表和子模块列表。每个子模块配备本地变量列表以保持工作空间整洁，支持特定任务定制。软件将图形用户界面（GUI）组件与数据处理算法分离，增强代码可读性、可维护性和可扩展性。

Result: 该软件整合了STM数据分析中常用及新近发展的算法，包括背景扣除（background subtraction）、完美晶格校正（perfect lattice correction）、Lawler-Fujita校正和亚原子精度配准（sub-atomic precision registration）等标准数据处理流程。提供内置模块如多二维图像可视化分析器（Multiple 2D Images Visualizer and Analyzer）。

Conclusion: AngstromPro通过整合分散的STM工作流程、维护详细处理历史并提供灵活定制平台，显著提升了STM数据分析的效率、可靠性和可重复性。其设计支持从使用内置工具的用户到开发自定义算法或扩展新模块的开发者的广泛用户群体。

Abstract: We present AngstromPro, a versatile, modular and open-source software built on Python for managing, visualizing and analyzing large datasets acquired via Scanning Tunneling Microscopes (STM). Its robust architecture features a top-level module that manages a Global Variables List and a sub-modules List. Each sub-module, equipped with its own Local Variables List to maintain a tidy workspace, can be tailored for specific tasks, including built-in modules like the Multiple 2D Images Visualizer and Analyzer. These modules support step-by-step data processing and extensibility for custom algorithms and functions. AngstromPro's design supports a wide range of users, from those relying on built-in tools to developers creating custom algorithms or extending the platform with new modules. In its implementation, AngstromPro separates graphical user interface components from data processing algorithms, a strategy that enhances code readability, maintainability, and extensibility. The embedded algorithms reflect commonly adopted and recently developed approaches in STM data analysis, including background subtraction, perfect lattice correction, Lawler-Fujita correction, and sub-atomic precision registration, along with additional standard data processing routines. By consolidating fragmented STM workflows, maintaining detailed processing histories, and providing a flexible platform for customization, AngstromPro enhances both the efficiency, reliability, and reproducibility of STM data analysis, while enabling the rapid development of new methods and modules.

</details>


### [111] [Pseudogap and Condensation in Cuprate Superconductors from NMR Shifts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19215)
*Abigail Lee,Juergen Haase*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究基于铜氧化物高温超导体（high-temperature superconducting cuprates）的核磁共振（NMR）数据，通过分析铜的两个超精细耦合（hyperfine couplings）对称性，分离出两种不同的位移（shift）组分，揭示了赝能隙（pseudogap）温度与A、B自旋耦合的关系，以及自旋单重态配对（spin singlet pairing）的规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高温超导铜氧化物的电子性质编码在复杂的核磁共振数据中，但缺乏微观理论使得可靠的核磁共振现象学分析成为迫切需求。早期分析仅关注少数材料，发现了自旋单重态配对和神秘的赝能隙，但无法建立位移和弛豫的连贯现象学。

Method: 基于铜的两个超精细耦合（各向异性的Aα和各向同性的B）的对称性，对铜位移进行解耦分析。该方法仅依赖于对称性分析，不依赖具体微观理论，从而识别出两种不同的位移组分。

Result: 掺杂过程中，在赝能隙温度以上产生金属性B自旋，与金属性A自旋共存。进一步掺杂降低赝能隙温度并增加B自旋，但对A自旋影响较小。B自旋态密度随掺杂的线性增长率在x≈0.20处增加近三倍，此时赝能隙消失，A和B转变为超导金属态。赝能隙温度反映了A和B之间的耦合强度。

Conclusion: 赝能隙温度是A和B耦合强度的度量，抑制位移但不影响核弛豫。自旋单重态配对遵循三个简单的凝聚规则。最佳Tc需要A和B之间的特殊匹配，且涉及具有赝能隙的系统。最高Tc并非编码在位移中，而是与核弛豫以及平面Cu和O之间的电荷共享相关。

Abstract: The electronic properties of the high-temperature superconducting cuprates are encoded in complex sets of NMR data, but without microscopic theory, reliable NMR phenomenologies are in demand. Early analyses of NMR could only focus on very few materials and discovered spin singlet pairing and the enigmatic pseudogap. However, a coherent phenomenology of shift and relaxation could not be established, as incoming data from other cuprates complicated the picture. Today, due to work of many groups worldwide, planar copper and oxygen NMR data are available for most cuprates. Here, based only on symmetry of the two Cu hyperfine couplings, an anisotropic $A_α$ and isotropic $B$, the Cu shifts are disentangled, and two different shift components emerge. Upon doping the cuprates, metallic B-spins are created above the pseudogap temperature which is shared with metallic A-spins. Further doping decreases the pseudogap temperature and increases the B-spin, but less so the A-spin. The apparent linear rate of increase in density of states of the B-spin with doping increases nearly threefold above about $x=0.20$, where the pseudogap has disappeared and A and B turn into superconducting metals, i.e. they disappear rapidly at $T_\mathrm{c}$. The pseudogap temperature is a measure of the coupling between A and B, which suppresses the shifts but not nuclear relaxation. Spin singlet pairing involves A and B according to three simple rules for condensation which will be discussed. The optimal $T_\mathrm{c}$ demands a special match between A and B and involves systems with a pseudogap. However, the highest $T_\mathrm{c}$ of all cuprates is not encoded in the shift, but rather in nuclear relaxation and charge sharing between planar Cu and O. Relations to other probes are discussed.

</details>


### [112] [Unveiling the Superconducting Ground State of Heusler alloy Pd2ZrIn via muon spin relaxation and rotation measurement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19283)
*Kavita Yadav,Anoop M Divakaran,Jumpei G. Nakamura,Tsunehiro Takeuchi,K. Mukherjee*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: Pd2ZrIn是一种具有立方L21结构的全赫斯勒合金（full Heusler alloy），在2.2 K温度下表现出体相II类超导性（bulk type-II superconductivity）。该材料具有完全能隙、无节点的s波超导态，且保持时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry），属于弱耦合、脏极限（dirty-limit）的常规超导体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Pd2ZrIn合金旨在探索无序（disorder）对超导配对（superconducting pairing）的影响，特别是B2型反位无序（B2-type antisite disorder）在赫斯勒合金超导体中的作用机制。该材料为研究无序与超导基态（emergent ground states）之间的相互作用提供了独特平台。

Method: 通过电输运测量（electrical resistivity）和磁化率研究（magnetic susceptibility）确认体相超导性；利用零场μSR（zero-field μSR）探测时间反演对称性；采用横向场μSR（transverse-field μSR）分析涡旋晶格（vortex lattice）形成和超流密度（superfluid density）。通过Uemura图（Uemura plot）评估超导特性。

Result: 实验证实Pd2ZrIn在TC ~ 2.2 K时发生超导转变，具有II类超导特征。零场μSR显示无自发内磁场，表明时间反演对称性保持完好。超流密度分析支持完全能隙、无节点的s波配对态，超导能隙Δ(0) ~ 0.33 ± 0.01 meV。TC/TF比值表明该合金位于常规超导区域。

Conclusion: Pd2ZrIn被确认为一种弱耦合、脏极限的II类超导体，具有完全能隙、无节点的序参量（order parameter）且保持时间反演对称性。这些发现为理解无序赫斯勒合金中的超导机制提供了重要实验依据。

Abstract: Full Heusler alloys XInPd2 (X= Zr, Hf and Ti) have recently attracted significant attention owing to their symmetry-driven electronic structure and also due to the interplay between disorder and emergent ground states. Within this family, Pd2ZrIn serves as a unique platform to study the effect of disorder on superconducting pairing. This alloy crystallizes in a cubic L21 structure with significant B2-type antisite disorder. Electrical resistivity and magnetic susceptibility studies confirm bulk type-II superconductivity with a transition temperature TC ~ 2.2 K. Zero-field μSR results reveal no evidence of spontaneous internal magnetic fields below TC, confirming the preservation of time-reversal symmetry. Transverse-field μSR spectra show the formation of a vortex lattice, consistent with type-II superconductivity, and the superfluid density is well described by a fully gapped, nodeless s-wave state with superconducting gap Δ (0) ~ 0.33 \pm 0.01 meV. Furthermore, the estimated ratio of transition temperature and Fermi temperature (TC/TF) indicates that this alloy lies within the conventional superconducting regime on the Uemura plot. These results establish Pd2ZrIn as a weakly coupled, dirty-limit, type-II superconductor; with a fully gapped, nodeless order parameter and preserved time-reversal symmetry.

</details>


### [113] [Competing Constraints on Superconductivity in Thick FeSe films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19443)
*Ya-Xun He,Xing-Jian Liu,Qun Wang,Ting Chen,Hassan Ali,Jia-Ying Zhang,Bao-Juan Kang,Zheng Zhang,Jun-Yi Ge*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种高通量离轴脉冲激光沉积策略，通过将羽流不均匀性转化为组合式FeSe薄膜库，结合可解释机器学习，揭示了铁基超导薄膜中晶格参数、化学计量比和缺陷散射之间的竞争关系，实现了厚FeSe薄膜17.1 K的超导转变温度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁基超导体中压缩应变已知能提高FeSe薄膜的转变温度（Tc），但即使在相同衬底上报道的Tc值也存在很大差异，表明应变之外的因素至关重要。超导薄膜的优化面临多个生长参数复杂相互作用的挑战。

Method: 开发了高通量离轴脉冲激光沉积（off-center pulsed laser deposition）策略，将羽流不均匀性转化为具有连续梯度的组合式FeSe薄膜库。系统表征了80个厚薄膜（>50 nm），并结合可解释机器学习（interpretable machine learning）进行分析。

Result: 发现最大Tc并不与羽流中心重合，而是可能偏移到离轴位置，揭示了有利的c轴膨胀、化学计量比（stoichiometry）和缺陷散射之间的竞争关系。除了c轴晶格参数与Tc的强相关性外，化学计量比和缺陷散射对可达到的转变温度施加了关键约束，定义了狭窄的优化窗口而非简单的单调关系。

Conclusion: 该框架在厚FeSe薄膜中实现了Tconset=17.1 K，并建立了一个将组合合成与机器学习相结合的一般框架，用于揭示复杂功能材料中的约束优化景观（constrained optimization landscapes）。

Abstract: Superconducting films emerge from the complex interplay of multiple growth parameters, making their optimization challenging. In iron-based superconductors, compressive strain is known to enhance the transition temperature (Tc) of FeSe films, yet reported Tc values vary widely even on identical substrates, indicating factors beyond strain are critical. Here, we develop a high-throughput off-center pulsed laser deposition strategy that transforms plume inhomogeneity into combinatorial FeSe film libraries with continuous gradients in lattice parameter, composition, and disorder. We discover that the maximum Tc does not coincide with the plume center but can shift off-center, revealing a competition between favorable c-axis expansion, stoichiometry, and defect scattering. Systematic characterization of 80 thick films (>50 nm), combined with interpretable machine learning, shows that besides the strong correlate of c-axis lattice parameter to Tc, the stoichiometry and disorder scattering impose critical constraints on the achievable transition temperature, defining a narrow optimization window rather than a simple monotonic relationship. This framework yields Tconset=17.1 K in thick FeSe films and establishes a general framework combining combinatorial synthesis with machine learning to uncover constrained optimization landscapes in complex functional materials.

</details>


### [114] [Spatially-resolved voltage-reversal due to Bernoulli potentials in dissipative Bi$_2$Sr$_2$CaCu$_2$O$_{8+x}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19467)
*Sharadh Jois,Gregory M. Stephen,Samuel W. LaGasse,Genda Gu,Aubrey T. Hanbicki,Adam L. Friedman*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 在Bi₂Sr₂CaCu₂O₈₊ₓ霍尔棒器件中，观察到临界电流以上时，两侧边缘的纵向微分电压大小相当但符号相反，这一现象归因于移动涡旋中的粒子-空穴对称性破缺和相反伯努利势的形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究层状超导体中耗散电流的组成和流动机制，特别是临界电流以上时边缘电压的异常行为，这对于理解高温超导体的基本物理性质具有重要意义。

Method: 在Bi₂Sr₂CaCu₂O₈₊ₓ霍尔棒（Hall bar）器件中测量磁输运和临界电流，观察外加磁场中临界电流以上的纵向微分电压分布，特别关注具有侵入式电压接触（invasive voltage contacts）的器件。

Result: 观察到临界电流以上时，一侧边缘的纵向微分电压与另一侧边缘大小相当但符号相反；该现象不受外加磁场反转的影响，且似乎为具有侵入式电压接触的器件所特有。

Conclusion: 该行为源于移动涡旋中的粒子-空穴对称性破缺（particle-hole symmetry breaking）以及由于侵入式接触在边缘处产生热点导致快速涡旋成核和磁通流动时，相反涡旋速度形成的相反伯努利势（Bernoulli potentials）。

Abstract: We measure magneto-transport and critical currents in Bi$_2$Sr$_2$CaCu$_2$O$_{8+x}$ Hall bar devices. Above critical current in an applied magnetic field, we observe longitudinal differential voltage along one edge comparable in magnitude but opposite in sign to the other edge. This phenomenon is unaffected by reversal of the applied field, and seems unique to devices with invasive voltage contacts. We attribute the source of this behavior to particle-hole symmetry breaking in moving vortices and the formation of opposite Bernoulli potentials due to opposing vortex velocities at the edges where the invasive contacts create hotspots for rapid vortex nucleation and flux flow. These results are fundamental to the composition and flow of dissipative currents in layered superconductors.

</details>


### [115] [Observation of field-odd and field-free superconducting diode effects in $\mathrm{Mo}_2\mathrm{C}$ nanoflakes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19525)
*Wei Gao,Kaixuan Fan,Menghan Li,Jinhao Cheng,Qing Zhang,Shuaishuai Ding,Wenping Hu,Fan Yang,Dechao Geng,Hechen Ren*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究在传统认为中心对称的Mo₂C纳米片中发现了超导二极管效应（SDE），包括场奇偶依赖型和零场型两种模式，为液氦温度下的非互易超导电子学提供了理想平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导二极管效应（superconducting diode effect, SDE）具有实现超低功耗量子电子学的巨大潜力，但通常需要材料具有固有的对称性破缺。本研究旨在探索在传统认为中心对称的材料中实现SDE的可能性。

Method: 研究采用化学气相沉积（chemical vapor deposition, CVD）生长的二碳化钼（Mo₂C）纳米片作为实验材料。通过输运测量（transport measurements）在垂直面内磁场和零场条件下表征SDE特性，并通过面外磁场扫描确认其本征性质。

Result: 实验发现Mo₂C纳米片中同时存在场奇偶依赖型（field-odd）和零场型（field-free）SDE。场奇偶依赖型SDE在4K温度下效率可调且超过40%，而另一样品中零场型SDE在零场和场冷却条件下均保持稳定。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，畴边界超电流（domain-boundary supercurrents）或电荷密度波（charge density wave, CDW）类有序可能驱动了这种意外的对称性破缺组合。空气稳定的Mo₂C为液氦温度下工作的非互易超导电子学提供了理想平台，并将SDE的探索扩展到名义上的中心对称超导体中。

Abstract: The superconducting diode effect (SDE) enables nonreciprocal supercurrent flow, holding immense potential for ultra-low-power quantum electronics. Intrinsic SDE typically requires materials with inherent symmetry breakings. Here, we report the discovery of SDE in chemical vapor deposition-grown molybdenum carbide ($\mathrm{Mo}_2\mathrm{C}$) nanoflakes, a material traditionally considered centrosymmetric. Strikingly, this system uniquely hosts both field-odd and field-free SDEs. Transport measurements reveal a field-odd SDE with tunable efficiency exceeding 40% at 4 K under a perpendicular in-plane magnetic field. In a separate sample, a robust field-free SDE persists under zero-field and field-coolings. Out-of-plane field sweeps confirm the intrinsic nature of these phenomena. We propose that domain-boundary supercurrents or charge density wave-like orders drive this unexpected combination of symmetry breakings. Our findings establish air-stable $\mathrm{Mo}_2\mathrm{C}$ as an ideal platform for nonreciprocal superconducting electronics operating at liquid-helium temperatures, expanding the search for SDE into nominally centrosymmetric superconductors.

</details>

### [116] [Logarithmic Entanglement and Emergent Dipole Symmetry from a Strongly Coupled Light-Matter Quantum Circuit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18670)
*Luiz H. Santos*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过将Power-Zienau-Woolley变换重新解释为光-物质量子电路，建立了非局域腔光子与量子材料强耦合系统的精确可解框架，揭示了从弱耦合到超强耦合过程中光-物质纠缠的结构与标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子材料与非局域腔光子强耦合的混合系统已成为控制和探测量子关联的新前沿，但非局域耦合产生的光-物质纠缠的结构与标度行为仍缺乏深入理解。

Method: 通过将Power-Zienau-Woolley（PZW）变换重新解释为光-物质量子电路，建立精确可解框架，其中光子位置正交$X$与一维量子链的多体偶极矩$\mathcal{P}$耦合，推导出适用于所有耦合强度的约化密度矩阵封闭表达式。

Result: 在弱耦合下，约化密度矩阵呈现Lindbladian形式，纠缠熵由偶极矩方差控制；在超强耦合下，密度矩阵在偶极矩扇区精确块对角化，反映光子场动态施加的涌现偶极对称性。应用于半填充Su-Schrieffer-Heeger链时，强耦合下光-物质纠缠和光子修饰物质态的空间纠缠均随系统尺寸对数标度$S_\infty \sim \frac{α}{2}\log L$。

Conclusion: 该框架揭示了非局域光-物质耦合系统中纠缠的结构与标度行为，对数标度源于光子解析单个集体坐标$\mathcal{P}$，其涨落以$L^{α/2}$增长，这与一维临界系统的对数纠缠机制不同。

Abstract: Hybrid systems where a quantum material strongly couples to a nonlocal cavity photon mode have emerged as a new frontier for controlling and probing quantum correlations, yet the structure and scaling of light-matter entanglement produced by the nonlocal coupling remains poorly understood. We address this problem through an exactly solvable framework based on reinterpreting the Power--Zienau--Woolley (PZW) transformation as a \textit{light-matter quantum circuit} that couples the photonic position quadrature $X \sim a + a^\dagger$ to the many-body dipole $\mathcal{P}$ of a one-dimensional quantum chain. We derive a closed-form expression for the reduced density matrix valid at all coupling strengths, in which off-diagonal elements between matter states of unequal dipole are suppressed by a Gaussian factor encoding the full weak-to-ultrastrong coupling crossover. At weak coupling, the reduced density matrix takes a Lindbladian form with $\mathcal{P}$ as the jump operator, and the entanglement entropy is controlled by the dipole variance. At ultrastrong coupling, the density matrix becomes exactly block-diagonal in dipole sectors, reflecting an \textit{emergent dipole symmetry} dynamically imposed by the photon field, with entanglement entropy given exactly by the Shannon entropy of the dipole-sector weight distribution. Applying this framework to a half-filled Su--Schrieffer--Heeger chain, we show that, at strong coupling, both the light-matter entanglement and the spatial entanglement of the photon-dressed matter state scale logarithmically with system size, $S_\infty \sim \fracα{2}\log L$, robust across the SSH phase diagram. The logarithm originates from the photon resolving a single collective coordinate $\mathcal{P}$ whose fluctuations grow as $L^{α/2}$, a distinct mechanism from the logarithmic entanglement of critical one-dimensional systems.

</details>


### [117] [Hatsugai-Kohmoto-like Models for Altermagnets and Odd-Parity Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18684)
*Konstantin Rickelt,Denis Sedov,Mathias S. Scheurer*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出广义Hatsugai-Kohmoto多轨道模型，研究其相图和物理性质。该模型在微扰下展现丰富的谱函数，包括非常规磁体行为，并发现动量空间中的对称性破缺不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Hatsugai-Kohmoto-like模型作为非常规磁体（unconventional magnets）的丰富平台。通过引入广义多轨道模型，探索在微扰存在下的相图和物理性质，特别是消除基态简并后的对称性破缺行为。

Method: 引入广义Hatsugai-Kohmoto多轨道模型，并添加微扰以消除基态简并。将空间局域多轨道Hubbard相互作用的一阶研究映射到动量空间的Heisenberg模型。另外添加一种允许精确求解的动量空间相互作用类型。

Result: 模型展现出丰富的谱函数，包括非常规磁体区域。在弱耦合下即出现对称性破缺不稳定性，但平移对称性破缺序（如反铁磁性）被排除。观察到铁磁性、非常规p波和d波磁体，其特征是底层方晶格键上的自旋序。添加动量空间相互作用可稳定非简并单重态基态，同时保留非常规磁体的自旋分裂特征。

Conclusion: Hatsugai-Kohmoto-like模型为非常规磁体研究提供了丰富的平台。这些模型能够展示多种对称性破缺行为，包括动量空间中的Heisenberg模型映射和独特的自旋序模式，为理解非常规磁性开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We introduce a generalized Hatsugai-Kohmoto multi-orbital model and study its phase diagram and physical properties in the additional presence of perturbations that lift any extensive ground-state degeneracies. The unperturbed, exactly solvable model already displays a rich set of spectral functions, including regimes reminiscent of unconventional magnets. We map the first-order study of additional spatially local multi-orbital Hubbard interactions to a Heisenberg model in momentum space, which leads to symmetry-breaking instabilities already at weak coupling. Interestingly, translational-symmetry breaking orders, such as antiferromagnetism, are excluded. Instead, in addition to ferromagnetism, unconventional $p$-wave and $d$-wave magnets occur, characterized by spin order on the bonds of the underlying square lattice. Adding another type of momentum-space interaction, which still allows to solve the model exactly, is shown to stabilize a non-degenerate singlet ground state that retains the spin splitting characteristic of unconventional magnets. We discuss its impact on the spin structure factor. Taken together, our findings show that Hatsugai-Kohmoto-like models provide a rich playground for unconventional magnetism.

### [118] [Exploring Entropic Orders: High Temperature Continuous Symmetry Breaking, Chiral Topological States and Local Commuting Projector Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18694)
*Po-Shen Hsin,Ryohei Kobayashi*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出构建量子晶格模型的新解析方法，实现了高温下的熵序（entropic order），包括1+1维的连续对称性破缺和2+1维的拓扑超导态，这些熵序能够规避传统热力学限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为高温会破坏有序态，但近期研究表明熵序（entropic order）可以通过与玻色子耦合在经典晶格模型和量子场论中实现。本文旨在开发新的解析方法来构建具有熵序的量子晶格模型。

Method: 提出两种通用构造方法：将具有低温有序相的给定晶格模型与有序玻色子耦合，或对于局部对易投影哈密顿量（local commuting-projector Hamiltonians），与更一般的玻色子自由度耦合。

Result: 成功构建了1+1维高温连续对称性破缺的量子晶格模型，阐明了熵序如何规避Hohenberg-Mermin-Wagner定理；在2+1维构建了具有温度无关任意子关联函数的高温熵序p+ip手性拓扑超导态；获得了广泛的高温熵序非手性拓扑序家族。

Conclusion: 熵序拓扑序在高温下具有强高阶形式对称性（higher form symmetries），与传统拓扑序不同，这些对称性会发生自发破缺。这些结果为高温有序态的研究提供了新的理论框架和构造方法。

Abstract: High temperature is usually expected to destroy order: as the Gibbs state approaches the infinite-temperature limit, it becomes an equal-weight ensemble over all states and the system is generically disordered. Recent works showed that entropic order can violate this expectation through coupling to bosons in classical lattice models and quantum field theories, where the ordered states have higher entropy. Here we present new analytic methods for constructing quantum lattice models that exhibit entropic orders. In particular, we construct quantum lattice models with continuous symmetry breaking at high temperature in 1+1 dimensions and clarify how entropic order can evade the Hohenberg-Mermin-Wagner theorems. We also construct high-temperature entropic $p+ip$ chiral topological superconducting states in 2+1 dimensions with temperature-independent anyon correlation functions. In addition, we obtain a broad family of high-temperature entropic non-chiral topological orders. We show that the entropic topological orders have strong higher form symmetries at high temperature unlike the conventional topological orders, and the symmetry is spontaneously broken. These results follow from two general constructions that couple a given lattice model with a low-temperature ordered phase either to ordered bosons or, for local commuting-projector Hamiltonians, to more general bosonic degrees of freedom.

### [119] [Conformal Data for the $O(2)$ Wilson-Fisher CFT in $(2+1)$-Dimensional Spacetime from Exact Diagonalization and Matrix Product States on the Fuzzy Sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18705)
*Arjun Dey,Loic Herviou,Christopher Mudry,Slava Rychkov,Andreas Martin Läuchli*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在零温下研究模糊球上的微观量子自旋-1模型，该模型在量子临界点实现了(2+1)维时空中的O(2) Wilson-Fisher共形场论。通过精确对角化和矩阵乘积态技术结合共形微扰理论，提取了包括标度维度和算子乘积展开系数在内的共形数据，验证了共形自举预测和大电荷展开预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于利用模糊球正则化（fuzzy-sphere regularization）来研究O(2) Wilson-Fisher共形场论，该方法保留了CFT的完整空间SO(3)旋转对称性，使得态-算子对应（state-operator correspondence）成为可能，从而能够将能量本征态直接映射到CFT算子。

Method: 采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization, ED）和矩阵乘积态（matrix product state, MPS）技术，结合共形微扰理论（conformal perturbation theory, CPT）来提取共形数据。通过模糊球正则化保持空间旋转对称性，利用态-算子对应关系进行分析。

Result: 识别了32个原初算子（primary operators）及其后代（descendants），这些算子按守恒的O(2)电荷S^z和空间角动量L进行组织。最低原初算子的标度维度（scaling dimensions）数值结果与共形自举（conformal bootstrap）预测吻合良好，并验证了大电荷展开（large charge expansion）的预测。

Conclusion: 该研究成功实现了O(2) Wilson-Fisher共形场论在模糊球上的微观实现，验证了态-算子对应关系的有效性，并将有序相中的Goldstone模物理与临界点的声子原初算子（phonon primaries）联系起来，展示了数值方法与解析预测的一致性。

Abstract: We study at zero temperature a microscopic quantum spin-1 model on the fuzzy sphere that realizes the $O(2)$ Wilson-Fisher conformal field theory (CFT) in $(2+1)$-dimensional spacetime at a quantum critical point. Here, we use the fuzzy-sphere regularization as it preserves the full spatial $SO(3)$ rotational symmetry of the CFT, enabling the state-operator correspondence that maps energy eigenstates directly to CFT operators. Using exact diagonalization (ED) and matrix product state (MPS) techniques combined with conformal perturbation theory (CPT), we extract conformal data including scaling dimensions and operator product expansion (OPE) coefficients. We identify 32 primary operators and their descendants, organized by the conserved $O(2)$ charge $S^{z}$ and spatial angular momentum $L$. Our numerical results for the scaling dimensions of the lowest primary operators show good agreement with conformal bootstrap predictions. We verify predictions from the large charge expansion, which provides systematic predictions for operators carrying large $U(1)$ charge, connecting the Goldstone mode physics in the ordered phase to phonon primaries at the critical point.

</details>


### [120] [Dynamical magnetism in the disordered cubic lattice material $γ$-${\rm Ba}_{3}{\rm CoNb}_{2}{\rm O}_{9}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18794)
*Fanjun Xu,Ralf Feyerherm,Cecilie Glittum,Thomas J. Hicken,Hubertus Luetkens,Jonas A. Krieger,Cintli Aguilar-Maldonado,Sven Luther,Lucy K. Saunders,Clemens Ritter,Peter Fouquet,Margarita Russina,Karel Prokes,A. T. M. Nazmul Islam,Bella Lake*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验和理论方法揭示了γ-Ba₃CoNb₂O₉中无序简单立方自旋-1/2晶格的特殊行为，该系统接近磁性有序的位点渗流阈值，表现出宽热力学交叉、短程磁关联和持续快速自旋动力学，形成了一种区别于经典自旋玻璃和几何阻挫量子自旋液体的无序驱动动力学态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究γ-Ba₃CoNb₂O₉的动机在于探索无序简单立方自旋-1/2晶格在接近位点渗流阈值（site-percolation threshold）时的量子磁性行为。该系统因Co²⁺离子随机占据三分之一晶格位点而具有特殊无序性，为研究稀释和量子涨落如何影响三维磁性提供了理想平台。

Method: 研究方法结合了实验测量和理论计算：实验方面采用比热（specific-heat）、磁化率（susceptibility）、中子自旋回波（neutron spin-echo）和μ子自旋旋转（muon spin-rotation）技术；理论方面运用蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）和精确对角化（exact diagonalization）稀释S=1/2海森堡模型（Heisenberg model）。

Result: 结果显示系统存在宽热力学交叉（broad thermodynamic crossover）、短程磁关联（short-range magnetic correlations）和持续至0.1K以下的快速自旋动力学（fast spin dynamics），未观察到静态有序或传统自旋玻璃冻结（spin-glass freezing）。蒙特卡洛模拟得到孤儿自旋（orphan spins）、有限团簇和无限网络的分布，孤儿自旋分数（≈8.8%）与磁化测量推断值（≈8.2%）吻合良好。

Conclusion: 结论表明自旋-1/2量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）结合稀释效应和接近渗流阈值的条件，能够在三维系统中支持一种具有短程关联的无序驱动动力学态（disorder-driven dynamical state）。这种态既不同于经典自旋玻璃，也区别于几何阻挫量子自旋液体（geometrically frustrated quantum spin liquids）。

Abstract: $γ$-${\rm Ba}_{3}{\rm CoNb}_{2}{\rm O}_{9}$ realizes a disordered simple-cubic spin-$1/2$ lattice in which Co$^{2+}$ ions randomly occupy one third of the sites, placing the system close to the site-percolation threshold for magnetic order. Specific-heat, susceptibility, neutron spin-echo, and muon spin-rotation measurements reveal a broad thermodynamic crossover, short-range magnetic correlations, and persistent fast spin dynamics down to at least 0.1~K, with no evidence for static order or conventional spin-glass freezing. Monte Carlo simulations yield a broad distribution of orphan spins, finite clusters, and an infinite network. The calculated orphan-spin fraction ($\approx 8.8\%$) agrees well with the weakly correlated spin fraction inferred from magnetization ($\approx 8.2\%$). Exact diagonalization of a diluted $S = 1/2$ Heisenberg model captures the broad magnetic specific-heat anomaly and supports the coexistence of weakly and strongly correlated spin environments. These results support a picture in which spin-$1/2$ quantum fluctuations, together with dilution and proximity to the percolation threshold, can support a disorder-driven dynamical state with short-range correlations in three dimensions, distinct from both classical spin glasses and geometrically frustrated quantum spin liquids.

</details>


### [121] [Room-temperature multistage metastability in a moiré superstructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18998)
*B. Q. Lv,Yifan Su,Alfred Zong,Karna Morey,Bryan T. Fichera,Qiaomei Liu,Dong Wu,Yongchang Ma,Dupeng Zhang,Faran Zhou,Makoto Hashimoto,Dong-Hui Lu,Donald A. Walko,Haidan Wen,Jiarui Li,Suchismita Sarker,Jacob P. C. Ruff,N. L. Wang,Nuh Gedik*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究报道了在EuTe₄块体材料中观察到电驱动的室温非易失性亚稳态，这些状态具有离散电阻平台和强电场敏感性，适用于高温多比特存储器应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚稳态（metastability）不仅对相序和相变至关重要，也对从存储器件到金属玻璃等现代技术具有广泛意义。电荷密度波（charge density waves, CDWs）因其对外部刺激的敏感性，为探索亚稳态提供了多功能平台，但大多数CDW亚稳态仅在低温下稳定，限制了实际应用。

Method: 研究通过系统输运测量（systematic transport measurements）揭示了离散电阻平台和强电场敏感性。通过整合光电子能谱（photoemission spectroscopy）、衍射（diffraction）和原位输运测量（in-situ transport measurements），深入分析了亚稳态的物理机制。

Result: 在EuTe₄中观察到了电驱动的室温非易失性亚稳态，这些状态在宽温度窗口内的大滞后回线（giant hysteresis loop）中易于诱导，适合高温多比特存储器应用。研究发现这些亚稳态并非源于新有序相的出现或非公度周期性的变化，而是表现为原始CDW振幅的抑制和相关长度的减小。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了莫尔超结构（moiré superstructure）中电场诱导的垂直CDW相切换机制，不仅为具有堆叠电子序的莫尔系统中的亚稳态现象提供了关键见解，也确立了EuTe₄作为开发室温多比特存储器件的有前景平台。

Abstract: Metastability is fundamental not only to phase ordering and transitions, but also to a broad range of modern technologies, from memory devices to metallic glasses. In condensed-matter physics, charge density waves (CDWs) offer versatile platforms for accessing metastable states due to their sensitivity to external stimuli. However, most metastable CDW states are stabilized only at low temperatures, limiting their practical utility. In this study, we report the observation of electrically driven, room-temperature, nonvolatile metastable states in the bulk form of EuTe$_4$, a recently discovered compound that hosts an innate moiré superlattice characterized by the stacking of incommensurate monolayer and bilayer CDWs. Systematic transport measurements reveal discrete resistivity plateaus and strong electric-field sensitivity, with a large number of metastable states readily induced across a wide temperature window within a giant hysteresis loop, making them well-suited for high-temperature, multi-bit memory applications. By integrating photoemission spectroscopy, diffraction, and in-situ transport measurements, we uncover that these metastable states do not stem from conventional mechanisms such as the emergence of new ordered phases or changes in incommensurate periodicity. Instead, they are characterized by a suppression of the original CDW amplitude and a reduction in correlation length, pointing to a unique electric-field-induced switching of out-of-plane CDW phases in the moiré superstructure. Our findings not only provide critical insights into metastable phenomena in moiré systems with stacked electronic orders but also establish EuTe$_4$ as a promising platform for developing room-temperature, multi-bit memory devices.

</details>


### [122] [Energy relaxation due to two-phonon scattering of electrons: Breakdown of the energy diffusion model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19037)
*Joshua Covey,Dmitrii L. Maslov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究分析了在单声子散射被对称性或动量守恒禁止、而双声子散射允许的情况下，关联电子系统中的能量弛豫机制。研究发现，在布洛赫-格吕奈森温度以上，双软横光学声子的能量弛豫率超过单声子过程，且呈线性温度依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期太赫兹光谱对量子顺电体SrTiO₃和高Tc铜氧化物的研究重新激发了人们对关联电子系统中能量弛豫的兴趣。研究关注单声子散射被禁止而双声子散射允许的特殊情况，旨在理解此类系统中的能量弛豫机制。

Method: 通过求解玻尔兹曼方程（Boltzmann equation），分析单声子散射被对称性或动量守恒禁止条件下的能量弛豫过程。特别关注双软横光学声子（two soft transverse optical phonons）的散射机制及其温度依赖关系。

Result: 在布洛赫-格吕奈森温度（Bloch-Grüneisen temperature）以上，双声子散射的能量弛豫率超过单声子过程：单声子散射率按1/T变化，而双声子散射率呈线性T依赖。在布洛赫-格吕奈森温度以下，能量弛豫率按单粒子速率变化，软声子情况下为T³。对于各向异性电子能带，在两个布洛赫-格吕奈森温度之间出现中间区域，其中允许的单声子和双声子过程均按T²变化。

Conclusion: 双声子散射的主导地位否定了由于亚热声子频繁散射导致的能量扩散通常图像；相反，能量通过涉及热声子的稀有散射事件弛豫。这一发现对理解关联电子系统中的能量弛豫机制具有重要意义。

Abstract: Recent THz spectroscopy of the quantum paraelectric SrTiO$_3$ (arXiv:2501.15771) and a high-$T_c$ cuprate (arXiv:2503.15646) has renewed interest in energy relaxation in correlated electron systems. We consider a situation in which single-phonon scattering is forbidden by symmetry or momentum conservation, while two-phonon scattering is allowed. Solving the Boltzmann equation, we show that above the Bloch-Grüneisen temperature the energy relaxation rate from two soft transverse optical phonons exceeds the single-phonon one: while the latter scales as $1/T$, the former is linear in $T$. This dominance of two-phonon scattering invalidates the usual picture of energy diffusion due to frequent scattering by subthermal phonons; instead, energy relaxes via rare scattering events involving thermal phonons. Below the Bloch-Grüneisen temperature, the energy relaxation rate scales as the single-particle rate, namely as $T^3$ for soft phonons. For anisotropic electron bands, an intermediate regime appears between two Bloch-Grüneisen temperatures, in which both allowed single-phonon and two-phonon processes scale as $T^2$.

</details>

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了隐身超均匀（stealthy hyperuniform）键分布对蜂窝晶格上哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）电子和磁性质的影响，发现这种特殊无序结构能调控电子态密度并影响磁相变临界点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超均匀结构（hyperuniform structures）因其对密度涨落的异常抑制特性而备受关注，但它们在强关联系统中的影响尚不清楚。本研究旨在探索隐身超均匀键分布如何调控哈伯德模型的电子态和磁性质。

Method: 通过对角化非相互作用哈密顿量（noninteracting Hamiltonian）分析电子态密度，并应用实空间哈特里近似（real-space Hartree approximation）研究哈伯德模型的磁性相变。同时与准周期蜂窝铺砌（quasiperiodic honeycomb tiling）进行比较。

Result: 研究发现线性态密度（linear density of states）稳定出现，而键分布的隐身特性改变了高能区波函数扩展性并显著修饰带边附近的态密度。磁相变始终发生在半金属态和反铁磁有序态之间，其临界相互作用强度对隐身特性敏感。

Conclusion: 隐身超均匀无序为调控强关联系统中的电子态和磁相变提供了新途径，与准周期结构的比较进一步凸显了结构关联性的重要作用。

Abstract: We investigate the effects of stealthy hyperuniform bond distributions on the electronic and magnetic properties of the Hubbard model on the honeycomb lattice. Hyperuniform structures, distinct from random and quasiperiodic ones, have recently attracted considerable interest due to their anomalous suppression of density fluctuations. By diagonalizing the noninteracting Hamiltonian, we show that a linear density of states (DOS) robustly emerges, while the stealth property of the bond distribution changes the wave functions in the higher-energy region extended and significantly modifies the DOS near the band edge. To clarify the impact on magnetism, we apply the real-space Hartree approximation to the Hubbard model. We find that, the phase transition always occurs between semimetallic and antiferromagnetically ordered states and its critical interaction strength is sensitive to the stealth property. A comparison with the quasiperiodic honeycomb tiling further highlights the role of structural correlations. These results demonstrate that stealthy hyperuniform disorder provides a novel route to controlling electronic states and magnetic phase transitions in correlated systems.

*Thomas M Henderson,Guo P. Chen,Gustavo E. Scuseria*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: seniority-zero方法在描述强关联电子系统方面已显示出巨大潜力，但其他seniority区域尚未充分探索。特别是最大seniority区域与zero seniority具有相同的代数结构，这为开发新的计算方法提供了理论基础。

Method: 引入了一种seniority本征态组态相互作用（seniority eigenstate configuration interaction）方法，通过将轨道划分为具有seniority zero的配对集和具有seniority one的自旋集，约束波函数对每个配对轨道具有良好固定的局域seniority。同时展示了如何构建该ansatz的有效哈密顿量。

Result: 高seniority波函数在强关联费米系统中表现出出乎意料的优异精度。对于Hubbard模型和氮分子解离过程，其精度与seniority zero方法相当甚至更优，这为强关联系统的计算提供了新的有效途径。

Conclusion: 研究表明高seniority波函数在强关联系统中具有重要应用价值，其精度表现挑战了传统认知，为开发基于seniority约束的高效计算方法开辟了新方向。

Abstract: Zero-seniority methods have shown great promise for the description of strongly-correlated electronic systems. Other seniority sectors have been much less explored, and in particular the maximal seniority sector and zero seniority have the same underlying algebraic structure. We introduce a seniority eigenstate configuration interaction in which the wave function is constrained to have good fixed local seniority for each paired orbital, by which we mean we partition orbitals into a pairing set with seniority zero, and a spin set with seniority one. We show how to build the effective Hamiltonian for this ansatz, and demonstrate that high-seniority wave functions have unexpectedly excellent accuracy for strongly-correlated fermionic systems, with accuracy competitive with or better than seniority zero for the Hubbard model and for the dissociation of the nitrogen molecule.

Conclusion: 研究揭示了局域Mn 3d与周围B 2p轨道间存在有效的配体场（ligand field），这是近藤效应的表现。粒子-空穴不对称性促使重新思考核心能级光谱学中的关联和屏蔽效应，为理解巡游电子系统中的电子关联提供了新视角。

Abstract: Correlations between the localized and conductive spins/charges have been the central issue of various fascinating quantum phenomena found on itinerant electron systems. Here, the obvious multiplet structures are presented on the Mn 2$p$ to 3$d$ x-ray absorption for a heavy fermion $α$-(Yb,Lu)(Al$_{1-x}$Mn$_x$)B$_4$, indicating that the unoccupied electronic structure of the Mn site is described as the correlated high-spin 2+, even though magnetic measurements show the Mn sites to be nonmagnetic. This apparently paradoxical result demonstrates that a ligand field can effectively appear between localized Mn 3$d$ and surrounding B 2$p$ orbitals, which has been anticipated as a manifestation of a Kondo effect but not been clearly confirmed for most itinerant metals in spectroscopy. By contrast, the Mn 2$p$ photoemission indicates that the occupied Mn$^{2+}$ 3$d$ electrons still exhibit itinerant and nonlocally screened nature also owing to the Kondo-like correlation with the conductive B 2$p$, and heavier Yb 4$f$ and 5$d$ bands below the Fermi energy. The asymmetry on the particle-hole stimulates a reconsideration of the correlation and screening effects in the core-level spectroscopies.

Result: 局域磁化（local magnetization）在三角形晶胞（triangle plaquette）单元内呈现完全补偿的亚铁磁模式（fully compensated ferrimagnetic pattern），导致磁振子（magnon）和电子能带中出现s波型自旋分裂（s-wave-type spin splittings）。这实现了绝缘系统中的零场反铁磁自旋塞贝克效应（antiferromagnetic spin Seebeck effect）和金属系统中的填充控制极化态（filling-controlled polarized states）。

Abstract: Spin-selective band splitting without net magnetization and spin-orbit couplings serves for a next-generation spin-current generator, and its typical platforms are altermagnets and compensated ferrimagnets as well, where the existence of a crystal asymmetry or nonequivalent sites is essential. Here, we theoretically demonstrate that such a splitting can be realized in a triple-{\bf Q} 12-sublattice state emerging in a $J_3$-dominant kagome antiferromagnet, without the help of the crystal asymmetry. Reflecting the multi-sublattice nature, a local magnetization reveals a fully compensated ferrimagnetic pattern in units of a triangle plaquette, leading to $s$-wave-type spin splittings in magnon and electron bands. ### [127] [Spin-orbit-induced quantum chiral phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19161)

Method: 研究采用自旋-1/2三角晶格模型，包含XXZ相互作用、自旋轨道诱导的交换相互作用和外磁场。使用无限密度矩阵重整化群（iDMRG）方法全面绘制模型相图，并通过详细的磁振子分析（magnon analysis）探究SSC的量子起源。

Abstract: The scalar spin chirality (SSC), whose nonzero value $\langle {\bf S}_i \cdot ({\bf S}_j \times {\bf S}_k) \rangle \neq 0$ implies the breaking of time-reversal and certain point-group symmetries in the ground state, is a key quantity characterizing chiral magnetism in both classical and quantum settings. The classical SSC is manifested, for instance, in skyrmion crystal phase, while the quantum SSC is still highly sought after in various frustrated spin-1/2 models. An interesting possibility that has not been explored so far is the case in which SSC is symmetry-wise allowed, yet remains zero classically due to the collinear or coplanar arrangement of spins, but is generated by virtue of quantum fluctuation. We demonstrate the existence of precisely such a phase in a spin-1/2 triangular-lattice model with XXZ interaction, spin-orbit-induced exchange interactions, and an external magnetic field. Using iDMRG, we thoroughly map out the phase diagram of the model and identify several phases with coexisting magnetic order and SSC. The nonzero SSC arises despite the classical magnetic order being collinear or coplanar. We provide detailed magnon analysis to ascribe its origin to quantum fluctuations around classical magnetic order. The estimate of SSC from magnon analysis agrees with iDMRG results quantitatively. We map out the magnon spectrum and its Berry curvature, culminating in the prediction of finite thermal Hall conductivity in these phases with SSC.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析2×2×4 CDW的堆叠能量学，采用实空间金兹堡-朗道自由能（Ginzburg-Landau free energy）方法。首先在每层强制采用固定三重对称三六角构型的极限下进行分析，然后放松这一刚性层约束，采用与从头算（ab initio）计算参数一致的物理意义方式。

Abstract: The kagome superconductor CsV$_3$Sb$_5$ is the only one in the AV$_3$Sb$_5$ family (A=K,Rb,Cs) that shows a $2\times2\times4$ charge-density-wave (CDW) ground state competing with the more common $2\times2\times2$. In addition, it is also the only one that shows second-harmonic transport and thus broken inversion symmetry, suggesting these two features are connected. In this work, we test whether the $2\times2\times4$ CDW can break inversion symmetry by analyzing its stacking energetics with a real-space Ginzburg-Landau free energy. In the limit where each layer is forced to adopt a fixed, threefold symmetric tri-hexagonal configuration, we find an analytical phase diagram mostly occupied by inversion preserving AB and ABCD stacked solutions. Relaxing this rigid layer constraint in a physically meaningful way consistent with \emph{ab initio}--calculated parameters, we find several new phases including an AABC solution and a distorted ABCD solution, which break inversion and all mirrors and are thus chiral. However, these phases occupy only small fractions of phase space, suggesting other mechanisms for inversion symmetry breaking may be at play in CsV$_3$Sb$_5$.

We study the superconducting regime of the model in the presence of a Hubbard attractive interaction by tuning the magnetic flux across its critical value. We determine the phase diagram in the plane of the coprime pairs parametrizing the magnetic flux. We show that the system exhibits two distinct regimes separated by a critical flux $Φ_c$: for $Φ>Φ_c$, a semimetal-to-superconductor quantum phase transition occurs at a finite interaction strength ($U_c\neq0$), while for $Φ<Φ_c$ superconductivity arises for arbitrarily weak attraction, with a BCS-like exponential scaling of the gap due to the finiteness of the density of states. Close to the transition, we study the scaling behavior and identify the critical exponents. Our results highlight the interplay between magnetic band topology and attractive pairing in three-dimensional Hofstadter systems.

</details>

Abstract: We report low-temperature $^{115}$In nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR) study of the prototypical heavy-fermion compound CeIrIn$_5$ in high magnetic fields applied close to the crystallographic $c$ axis. For this orientation, a field-induced transition was previously reported to take place at about 28 T. Although we do not observe any change of the NMR spectrum above the transition, the intensity of the NMR lines drastically decreases as a consequence of a considerable shortening of the $T_2$ relaxation time. In addition, $1/T_1$ shows a pronounced maximum at the transition. Taking into account previous high-field de Haas-van Alphen results in conjunction with band-structure calculations, our NMR results are most naturally explained by the field-induced transition into an antiferromagnetic state with the propagation vector $\mathbf{Q} = (1/2, 1/2, 0)$ and magnetic moments aligned antiferromagnetically along the $c$ axis. This makes CeIrIn$_5$ a unique case where the application of the magnetic field induces an ordered state with moments antiferromagnetically aligned along the field direction.

### [131] [Hydrodynamics of the viscous electron fluid in cadmium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19416)
*Xiaodong Guo,Xiaokang Li,Benoît Fauqué,Alaska Subedi,Lingxiao Zhao,Zengwei Zhu,Kamran Behnia*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用聚焦离子束微结构加工技术调控有效厚度，在有限窗口内检测低温尺寸依赖的电阻率上升。该窗口位于弹道（ballistic）和扩散（diffusive）输运机制之间，通过电导率对样品尺寸和温度的双重二次依赖关系来识别流体动力学流动特征。

Result: 在镉中观测到电导率同时呈现对样品尺寸和温度的二次依赖关系，这是流体动力学流动的指纹特征。研究量化了电子流体的运动学粘度和动力学粘度的幅度及温度依赖性。与石墨烯和³He不同，镉中动量守恒的e-e碰撞速率不由主费米能级决定，而是由微小能量尺度和谷间瓶颈效应控制。

Conclusion: 该研究在三维元素金属镉中实现了Gurzhi效应的典型实例，证实了电子流体动力学输运的存在，并揭示了镉中动量守恒碰撞速率的独特机制，为理解金属中的电子流体行为提供了新见解。

Abstract: Thanks to electron-electron ($e$-$e$) collisions conserving momentum, metallic electron fluids are viscous. Yet, this viscosity is rarely detectable in bulk transport. Here, we report on the canonical realization of the Gurzhi effect in an elemental three-dimensional metal: cadmium. Using focused ion beam microstructuring to tune the effective thickness, we detected a low-temperature size-dependent resistivity upturn in a finite window sandwiched between ballistic and diffusive regimes. Within this window, the electrical conductivity displays a simultaneous quadratic dependence on both sample size and temperature -- fingerprint of a hydrodynamic flow. This leads us to quantify the amplitude and the temperature dependence of kinematic and dynamic viscosity of the electron fluid. In cadmium, in contrast with graphene and $^3$He, the rate of momentum-conserving $e$-$e$ collisions is not set by the main Fermi energy, but by Lilliputian energy scales and inter-valley bottlenecks.

In particular, we determine the QCD equation of state by computing the baryon density as well as the pressure as functions of the baryon chemical potential and the temperature. Potential issues with wrong convergence of complex Langevin dynamics are under control and we indeed find agreement with previous lattice studies working at smaller chemical potentials, as well as with perturbative hard-thermal-loop calculations at high temperatures.

### [134] [Equation of state for the edge flow of chiral colloidal fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18708)
*Jessica Metzger,Cory Hargus,Julien Tailleur,Frédéric van Wijland*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索非平衡被动和主动手性胶体流体（nonequilibrium passive and active chiral colloidal fluids）在边界处产生的边缘流（edge flows），理解这些复杂界面电流的物理机制。

Method: 通过建立状态方程（equation of state）将边缘通量（edge flux）与体相可观测量（bulk observables）联系起来，对于受限流体，边缘通量由流体中的平均奇应力（average odd stress）给出；对于相分离系统，界面通量由奇应力在界面两侧的跳跃（jump of the odd stress across the interface）决定。

Result: 研究结果表明，边缘流通量可以通过奇应力这一体相可观测量来表征，并利用该状态方程揭示了被动和主动系统中边缘电流的微观起源（microscopic origins）及其对比差异。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了非平衡手性流体边缘流的普适描述框架，通过奇应力连接了宏观通量与微观机制，为理解被动与主动系统中边界流动的物理本质提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We explore the edge flows that emerge at boundaries in nonequilibrium passive and active chiral colloidal fluids. We show that these complex interface currents obey an equation of state that relates their fluxes to bulk observables. For confined fluids, the edge flux is given by the average odd stress in the fluid. In phase-separated systems, the flux along the interface is given by the jump of the odd stress across the interface. We then use the equation of state to reveal, and contrast, the microscopic origins of the edge currents in passive and active systems.

### [135] [Tunable turbulence in driven microscale emulsions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18802)
*Majid Bahraminasr,Anand Yethiraj*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种可调控的非平衡油包油乳液模型系统，通过电导率作为单一控制参数，实现了从可控液滴变形到多尺度湍流状流动的转变，并提供了电水动力学湍流转变的实验证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

By utilizing a miscible mixture of silicone and motor oils as the continuous phase and the immiscible castor oil as the droplet phase, we isolate electrical conductivity as a single experimental control parameter, varying it by over two orders of magnitude while keeping viscosity and permittivity nearly constant. This high degree of control allows us to systematically traverse the electrohydrodynamic (EHD) phase diagram with dielectric constant and conductivity as control parameters. We validate small-deformation theory at low fields before driving the system into a regime of multiscale, unsteady flows at high fields. We employ three complementary approaches on the same system (particle image velocimetry (PIV), used to map velocity fields, and rheometry and differential dynamic microscopy (DDM), two techniques used to probe viscosity and diffusion) to quantify the emergence of scale invariance in the energy spectra with increasing field strength. Above a threshold field, we find that the spatio-temporal energy spectra obtained by PIV analysis of droplet dynamics display power-law scaling, $E(k) \sim k^{-α_k}$, where $α_k$ approaches the inertial turbulence exponent of $5/3$ at high fields.
