Abstract: Knitted fabrics exemplify a broad class of architected materials capable of large deformations, enabling shape morphing, mechanical biocompatibility, and embedded multifunctionality without material damage. Although geometric nonlinearity has been intuitively utilized in their design, a quantitative description of stitch-resolved deformation and its temporal evolution remains lacking. Here, we introduce a geometric quantification framework that reconstructs smooth yarn centerlines and fabric surfaces from sparse yarn-level representations and extracts interpretable descriptors across dimensions. Applied to representative knitted structures, this framework resolves how global deformation is distributed among stitch reorientation, loop bending, surface bending, and dilation. Moreover, it reveals how regions of large geometric variation emerge, persist, and redistribute over time. Rather than directly measuring stress, these geometric descriptors define a unified geometric state space for comparing knitted structures and identifying candidate regions of mechanical localization. The framework provides a quantitative language for nonlinear deformation in knits and establishes a geometry-based representation that can be coupled to constitutive models, experimental measurements, and graph-based inverse-design workflows.

Combining experiments, theory and simulations, we show that pusher-type micrsowimmers are attracted towards a meniscus corner, followed by transient trapping and eventual escape. We demonstrate that hydrodynamic interactions with the wall-interface corner intimately dictate the attraction and trapping or escape of the microswimmer on the basis of its strength. We show that the swimming trajectory at the meniscus corner can be tuned depending on the type of the microswimmer, the corner geometry and the viscosity ratio for the liquid interface. Motivation: 剪纸艺术在现代机械超材料（mechanical metamaterials）设计中得到广泛应用，但能否基于最简单的铺砌形式——单调铺砌（monotile patterns）来创建可展开的剪纸结构，这是一个自然且尚未解决的问题。

Method: 通过显式构造（explicit constructions）证明周期性（periodic）和非周期性（aperiodic）单调铺砌剪纸结构的存在性，并对这些结构在展开过程中的形状和尺寸变化进行理论和计算分析。

Result: 构建了覆盖所有17种壁纸群（wallpaper groups）的周期性单调铺砌剪纸结构，以及覆盖各种准晶（quasicrystal）图案和多风筝（polykite）铺砌的非周期性结构，为更广泛的形状变形超材料（shape-morphing metamaterials）设计提供了新途径。

Conclusion: 本研究为更广泛的形状变形超材料（shape-morphing metamaterials）的设计和分析开辟了新途径，证明了基于单调铺砌的可展开剪纸结构的可行性。

Abstract: Kirigami, the art of paper cutting, has been widely used in the modern design of mechanical metamaterials. In recent years, many kirigami-based metamaterials have been designed based on different planar tiling patterns and applied to different science and engineering problems. However, it is natural to ask whether one can create deployable kirigami structures based on the simplest forms of tilings, namely the monotile patterns. In this work, we answer this question by proving the existence of periodic and aperiodic monotile kirigami structures via explicit constructions. In particular, we present a comprehensive collection of periodic monotile kirigami structures covering all 17 wallpaper groups and aperiodic monotile kirigami structures covering various quasicrystal patterns as well as polykite tilings. We further perform theoretical and computational analyses of monotile kirigami patterns in terms of their shape and size changes under deployment. Altogether, our work paves a new way for the design and analysis of a wider range of shape-morphing metamaterials.

</details>

### [139] [Asymptotic Stability of Hartree--Fock Homogenous Equilibria in $\mathbb{R}^d$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18952)
*Toan T. Nguyen,Chanjin You*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明了具有非对角交换算符（off-diagonal exchange operator）的含时Hartree-Fock方程中一大类平移不变稳态解的非线性Landau阻尼和渐近稳定性，该算符出现在大费米子系统的平均场理论中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究包含交换算符的Hartree-Fock方程稳态解的稳定性问题，该算符虽然属于次阶算子，但会扰动经典的Schrödinger色散关系，并导致背景电子对空间密度的线性响应变得复杂。

Method: 开发了非线性迭代方案，基于详细的预解式（resolvent）分析，利用Fourier空间中的输运型色散，并在加权的$L^\infty_{k,p}$范数中传播相位混合（phase mixing）和Landau阻尼。

Result: 在$\mathbb{R}^d$（$d\ge 3$）全空间中，建立了具有交换算符的Hartree-Fock方程平移不变稳态解的非线性Landau阻尼和渐近稳定性，克服了动量依赖的回波共振（momentum-dependent echo resonances）等困难。

Conclusion: 通过创新的分析方法成功处理了交换算符引入的复杂色散关系和共振现象，为包含非对角交换算符的Hartree-Fock方程稳定性理论提供了严格数学框架。

Abstract: In this paper, we establish nonlinear Landau damping and asymptotic stability of a large class of translation-invariant steady solutions to the time-dependent Hartree--Fock equations in the presence of an {\em off-diagonal exchange operator}, which arises naturally in the meanfield theory of a large fermionic system, in the whole space $\mathbb{R}^d$, $d\ge 3$. Despite being a sub-order operator, the inclusion of the exchange term disturbs the classical Schrödinger dispersion and causes a complex linear response from the background electrons to the space density whose dispersion relation is no longer a Fourier multiplier as in the classical Vlasov and Hartree theory. In addition, the group velocity of each elementary waves involves a mixture of all other Fourier modes, leading to delicate {\em momentum-dependent echo resonances}. To overcome the issues, we develop a nonlinear iterative scheme that relies on a detailed resolvent analysis, makes use of a transport type dispersion in Fourier spaces, and propagates phase mixing and Landau damping in weighted $L^\infty_{k,p}$ norms.

</details>

Result: 成功证明了任意维度晶格上分层安德森-伯努利模型的安德森局域化，并展示了该方法在概率性唯一延拓问题中的适用性。

### [142] [Particle Dynamics Driven by Charge Exchange](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19603)
*Adrian Schmautz,Rico Zacher*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文提出并分析了一个描述电荷交换相互作用产生粒子动力学的数学模型，该模型将已有的交换驱动增长模型扩展到整个整数格点上的粒子密度，揭示了两个模型在定性行为和数学分析上的显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在建立一个描述电荷交换（charge-exchange）相互作用产生粒子动力学的数学模型。该研究扩展了先前多个工作中已建立的交换驱动增长模型（exchange-driven growth model），允许粒子密度定义在整个整数格点（integer lattice）上。

Method: 在碰撞算子（collision operator）核函数满足适当假设的条件下，建立了具有有限一阶矩的非负密度类中的全局适定性（global well-posedness）。此外，在细致平衡条件（detailed balance condition）下，利用熵方法（entropy methods）研究平衡态的结构并分析其稳定性。

Result: 尽管两个模型存在许多相似之处，但在定性行为和数学分析方面都出现了实质性差异。研究证明了模型在适当条件下的数学适定性，并通过熵方法获得了关于平衡态结构及其稳定性的分析结果。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了一个扩展的电荷交换动力学模型，揭示了其与原有模型的重要差异，并提供了关于模型适定性、平衡态结构及稳定性的完整数学分析框架。

Abstract: We introduce and analyse a mathematical model describing the dynamics of particles generated by charge-exchange interactions. The model extends the well-established exchange-driven growth model, previously studied in several works, by allowing for particle densities defined on the entire integer lattice. Despite the many similarities between the two models, substantial differences arise both in their qualitative behaviour and in their mathematical analysis. Under suitable assumptions on the kernel in the collision operator, we establish global well-posedness in the class of nonnegative densities with finite first moment. Moreover, under a detailed balance condition, we investigate the structure of equilibria and analyse their stability by means of entropy methods.

### [143] [Painlevé Asymptotics of the Focusing Nonlinear Schrödinger Equation with a Finite-Genus Algebro-Geometric Background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19506)
*Ruihong ma,Engui Fan*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究聚焦非线性薛定谔方程（focusing NLS equation）在代数几何拟周期解背景下的柯西问题，采用Riemann-Hilbert方法和非线性最速下降法分析长时间渐近行为，根据背景Riemann曲面亏格奇偶性分别得到Painlevé II超越函数和抛物柱函数的渐近表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究聚焦非线性薛定谔方程在代数几何拟周期解（algebro-geometric quasi-periodic solutions）作为渐近边界条件下的柯西问题，旨在分析此类初值问题解的长时间渐近行为。

Method: 采用Riemann-Hilbert（RH）方法结合Deift-Zhou非线性最速下降法（nonlinear steepest descent method），根据背景超椭圆Riemann曲面（hyperelliptic Riemann surface）的亏格（genus）奇偶性分两种情况进行分析。

Result: 当背景解对应奇亏格（n=2s+1）时，在(x,t)平面不同区域（由ξ=x/t参数化）的渐近行为由第二Painlevé超越函数（second Painlevé transcendent）描述；当对应偶亏格（n=2s）时，渐近行为由抛物柱函数（parabolic cylinder functions）描述，并建立了显式误差界。

Conclusion: 该研究系统分析了聚焦NLS方程在代数几何拟周期解背景下的长时间渐近行为，根据背景Riemann曲面亏格奇偶性获得了不同类型的渐近表达式，为理解此类非线性演化方程提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate the Cauchy problem for the focusing nonlinear Schrödinger (NLS) equation \begin{equation}
  iq_t(x,t)+q_{xx}(x,t)+2|q(x,t)|^2q(x,t)=0,\quad x\in\mathbb{R},\quad t\ge0,\nonumber \end{equation} subject to initial data $ q(x,0)$ satisfying the asymptotic boundary conditions \begin{equation}\label{eq:boundary} q(x,0) \sim q^{alg}(x,0) \quad \text{as} \quad x \to \pm\infty,\nonumber \end{equation} where $q^{alg}(x,t)$ denote finite-genus algebro-geometric quasi-periodic solutions of the focusing NLS equation. Employing the Riemann--Hilbert (RH) approach combined with the Deift--Zhou nonlinear steepest descent method, we analyze the long-time asymptotic behavior of solutions to this Cauchy problem. Our analysis distinguishes between two cases based on the genus $n$ of the underlying hyperelliptic Riemann surface:
  (i) Odd genus backgrounds: When the background solutions $q^{alg}(x,0)$ correspond to hyperelliptic curves of odd genus $n = 2s+1$ $(s \in \mathbb{N}_0)$, we identify distinct asymptotic regions in the $(x,t)$-plane characterized by the variable $ξ= x/t$, within which the leading-order asymptotics is expressed in terms of the second Painlevé transcendent.
  (ii)Even genus backgrounds: When the background solutions $q^{alg}(x,0)$ correspond to hyperelliptic curves of even genus $n = 2s$ $(s \in \mathbb{N})$, the asymptotic behavior in regions selected by $ξ$ is described in terms of parabolic cylinder functions.
  Specifically, we derive the leading-order asymptotics and establish explicit error bounds for the solution $q(x,t)$ as $t \to +\infty$, uniformly for $x \in \mathbb{R}$.

</details>


### [144] [Fuzzy Geometries with an Internal Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19549)
*John W. Barrett,Joseph Burridge*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了非对易矩阵谱三元组与二维内空间的乘积，将其解释为包含带电狄拉克费米子及其反粒子的非对易时空。通过计算真空狄拉克算符的内涨落，得到了规范场的非对易类比、时空几何涨落以及依赖于粒子电荷的导数算符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索非对易矩阵谱三元组与简单二维内空间的乘积结构，将其解释为包含带电狄拉克费米子及其反粒子的非对易时空模型，旨在理解此类非对易几何结构中的物理内涵。

Method: 采用标准技术计算真空狄拉克算符的内涨落，具体运用Connes一形式方法。该方法基于非对易几何框架，通过内涨落分析来推导相应的物理结构。

Result: 计算得到了规范场的非对易类比，以及时空几何的涨落。此外，涨落还包括一个依赖于粒子电荷的导数算符。通过对模型中费米子的积分计算，还得到了一些新颖的诱导玻色项。

Conclusion: 研究表明，非对易矩阵谱三元组与二维内空间的乘积能够自然地产生规范场和时空几何涨落，同时揭示出依赖于电荷的导数算符和诱导玻色项，为非对易几何在粒子物理中的应用提供了新的见解。

Abstract: The product of a non-commutative matrix spectral triple with a simple two-dimensional internal space is considered. This is interpreted as a non-commutative spacetime that contains one charged Dirac fermion and its antiparticle. The inner fluctuations of a vacuum Dirac operator are calculated, using the standard technique of Connes' one-forms. This results in the non-commutative analogue of a gauge field, as expected, and also fluctuations of the spacetime geometry. In addition, the fluctuations include a derivative operator that depends on the particle charge. The integral over the fermions in the model is calculated, leading to some novel induced bosonic terms.

</details>


### [145] [The bosonic Hubbard model on a three dimensional flat band lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19703)
*Leon Haag-Fank,Andreas Mielke*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了立方晶格线图（line graph）上具有周期边界条件的跳跃矩阵（hopping matrix）最低本征态，发现其形成高度简并的平带（flat band）且具有局域化特性。在排斥性玻色-哈伯德模型（repulsive bosonic Hubbard model）中，可通过将粒子置于互不重叠的局域化单粒子基态来构造精确多粒子基态，直至临界粒子数N_c。研究发现，在N_c处基态熵呈亚广延性（subextensive）∝N_c^{2/3}，而较低密度下熵为广延性（extensive）。该问题与具有周期边界条件的立方晶格的4-循环分解（4-cycle decompositions）数量相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究立方晶格线图上跳跃矩阵最低本征态的简并性与局域化特性，及其在排斥性玻色-哈伯德模型中的物理意义。探索通过局域化单粒子基态构造多粒子基态的可能性，并分析临界粒子数附近的熵标度行为。

Method: 分析具有周期边界条件的立方晶格线图上的跳跃矩阵本征态，利用其高度简并的平带和局域化特性。在排斥性玻色-哈伯德模型中，通过将粒子置于互不重叠的局域化单粒子基态来构造精确多粒子基态。采用数学证明方法分析临界粒子数N_c处的熵标度行为。

Result: 证明了在临界粒子数N_c处，基态熵呈亚广延性，标度为∝N_c^{2/3}。在低于临界密度的区域，熵表现为广延性。建立了该物理问题与立方晶格4-循环分解数量之间的数学联系。

Conclusion: 立方晶格线图上跳跃矩阵的最低本征态形成高度简并的平带且具有局域化特性，这为排斥性玻色-哈伯德模型提供了构造精确多粒子基态的方法。临界粒子数处的熵标度行为呈现亚广延特性，揭示了系统在特定填充下的特殊统计性质。该物理问题与立方晶格的组合数学结构（4-循环分解）存在深刻联系。

Abstract: The lowest eigenstates of the hopping matrix on the line graph of a cubic lattice with periodic boundary conditions are highly degenerate, they form a lowest flat band. Further, these states are localized. If one considers a repulsive bosonic Hubbard model on this lattice it is possible to construct exact multi-particle ground states simply by putting particles in the localized single particle ground states such that they avoid each other. This can be done up to a certain critical particle number $N_c$. We prove that at this particle number the ground state entropy is subextensive $\propto N_c^{2/3}$. For lower densities the entropy is extensive. We further show that the problem is related to the number of 4-cycle decompositions of the cubic lattice with periodic boundary conditions.

</details>

### [146] [Three-dimensional recoil-electron reconstruction using combined optical imaging and waveform readout for electron-tracking Compton cameras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19051)
*Tomonori Ikeda,Tatsuya Sawano,Naomi Tsuji,Yoshitaka Mizumura*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种实用的三维反冲电子方向重建方法，通过结合高分辨率二维光学图像、一维波形信号和深度学习技术，在无需完整三维读出系统的情况下提升电子追踪康普顿相机（ETCC）的成像性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确重建反冲电子方向对于提升电子追踪康普顿相机（electron-tracking Compton cameras, ETCCs）在伽马射线成像中的点扩散函数至关重要。虽然完整的三维读出系统能实现高精度重建，但由于数据量巨大，不适用于大面积探测器。

Method: 本研究提出了一种实用的替代方法，通过模拟结合高分辨率二维光学图像、一维波形信号和基于深度学习的方法来推断康普顿散射中的三维反冲电子方向。该方法使用Geant4和MAGBOLTZ模拟生成的伪实验数据，应用于氩基气体时间投影室。

Result: 在40-50 keV能量范围内，所提方法实现了约44°的反冲电子方向角分辨率，相比之前基于条带读出的方法提高了约1.3倍。此外，在5-50 keV电子能量范围内，电子径迹起始点分辨率也优于先前方法。

Conclusion: 结果表明，来自横向图像和纵向波形的互补信息能够有效恢复三维径迹拓扑结构，而无需完整的三维读出系统。该方法为改善ETCC成像性能提供了一条现实可行的途径。

Abstract: Accurate reconstruction of recoil-electron directions is critical for enhancing the point-spread function of electron-tracking Compton cameras (ETCCs) in gamma-ray imaging. Although full three-dimensional (3D) readout systems achieve high-precision reconstruction, they are impractical for large-area detectors because of the enormous data volume. This study proposes and demonstrates a practical alternative for inferring the 3D recoil-electron direction in Compton scattering. This method combines a high-resolution two-dimensional optical image, a one-dimensional waveform signal, and a deep-learning-based method through simulations. The proposed method achieved an angular resolution of approximately $44^\circ$ for the recoil-electron direction in the 40-50 keV range, corresponding to an improvement of a factor of about 1.3 compared with our previous strip-readout approach using pseudo-experimental data generated by Geant4 and MAGBOLTZ simulations for an argon-based gas time projection chamber. In addition, the starting-point resolution of the electron track was improved over the previous method across the 5-50 keV electron energy range. These results demonstrate that complementary information from the transverse image and longitudinal waveform can effectively recover the 3D track topology without requiring full 3D readout. The proposed approach provides a realistic pathway for improving ETCC imaging performance.

</details>


### [147] [Drift Correction of Scan Images by Snapshot Referencing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19384)
*Zac Thollar,Kanto Maeda,Tetsuya Kubota,Taka-aki Yano,Qiwen Tan,Takumi Sannomiya*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为"快照参考（snapshot-referencing, SSR）"的漂移校正方法，用于消除扫描电子显微镜中长时间光谱映射时的图像漂移问题，该方法基于扫描过程的时间特性，利用快速扫描的"快照"作为无漂移参考来校正分析图谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扫描（透射）电子显微镜（S(T)EM）中的可靠定量分析常因长时间光谱映射过程中的图像漂移而受阻，这种漂移会影响元素分析或材料功能表征的准确性。

Method: 提出快照参考（SSR）漂移校正方法，这是一种基于扫描过程时间特性的回顾性方法；利用高信号、快速扫描的"快照"作为无漂移参考，计算扫描模式（如蛇形或光栅）归一化时间场中每个像素的连续漂移向量，以指导同时获取的分析图谱的校正。

Result: 在实验阴极发光（CL）数据集上证明了该方法的有效性，表明它能有效恢复高光谱数据立方体的空间完整性，且无需专用硬件。

Conclusion: 这种灵活的软件解决方案广泛适用于任何基于探针的分析技术，只要能够同时记录快速成像信号和慢速光谱数据。

Abstract: Reliable quantitative analysis in scanning (transmission) electron microscopy (S(T)EM) is often hindered by image drift during long-duration spectral mapping for elemental analysis or for various material functions. We here present snapshot-referencing (SSR) drift correction, a retrospective approach to eliminate spatial distortions based on the temporal nature of the scanning process; A continuous drift vector for every pixel is calculated for a normalized time-field of the scan pattern (e.g., serpentine or raster) utilizing a high-signal, fast-scan "snapshot" as a drift-free reference to guide the correction of simultaneously acquired analytical maps. To describe the drift, we employed Bezier basis functions to model smooth thermal or mechanical drifts and piece-wise linear basis for high-frequency "spiky" shifts such as those caused by charging. We demonstrate the efficacy of this approach on experimental cathodoluminescence (CL) datasets, showing that it effectively restores spatial integrity to hyperspectral data cubes without the need for specialized hardware. This flexible, software-based solution is broadly applicable to any probe-based analytical technique where a fast imaging signal can be recorded alongside slow spectroscopic data.

</details>

### [148] [Localization and universality of three-dimensional pseudospin-$s$ fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18690)
*Arpan Gupta,Gargee Sharma*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文建立了三维无序费米子中半经典输运与量子干涉的统一理论框架，揭示了赝自旋（pseudospin）依赖的Drude电导率与量子干涉修正的普适性之间的对比关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然弱局域化（weak localization, WL）和弱反局域化（weak antilocalization, WAL）现象在传统薛定谔和狄拉克-外尔（Dirac-Weyl）费米子中已被充分理解，但在更广泛的多重手性费米子（multifold chiral fermions）类别中，这些现象的命运仍未得到充分探索。

Method: 作者发展了一个统一框架，用于研究具有任意赝自旋s的三维无序费米子中的半经典输运和量子干涉。从一般短程矩阵无序M出发，推导了任意赝自旋下考虑多带效应的弹性寿命和梯状顶点修正（ladder vertex corrections）的紧凑表达式。

Result: 在标量无序极限下，Drude电导率强烈依赖于赝自旋和螺旋度（helicity），而领先的量子干涉修正则表现出显著的普适性：其大小与传统扩散金属和外尔费米子相同，其符号仅由2s的奇偶性决定。对于s=3/2的情况，通过求解耦合的Bethe-Salpeter方程，发现通道混合（channel mixing）会抑制WAL并驱动向局域化的交叉。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了跨越整个赝自旋层次结构的局域化一般理论，揭示了内部几何结构、对称性类别和输运普适性之间的相互作用。

Abstract: Quantum interference of electrons in disordered conductors is a sensitive probe of the internal structure of quasiparticles, revealing universal signatures of symmetry through weak localization (WL) and weak antilocalization (WAL). While these phenomena are well understood for the conventional Schrödinger and Dirac-Weyl fermions, their fate in the broader class of multifold chiral fermions remains largely unexplored. We develop a unified framework for semiclassical transport and quantum interference in three-dimensional disordered fermions with an arbitrary pseudospin $s$. Starting from a general short-range matrix disorder $\mathcal{M}$, we derive compact expressions for elastic lifetimes and ladder vertex corrections for arbitrary pseudospin with multiband effects, and then show that in the scalar-disorder limit while the Drude conductivity is strongly pseudospin and helicity dependent, in contrast, the leading quantum interference correction exhibits a striking universality: its magnitude remains identical to that of conventional diffusive metals and Weyl fermions, while its sign is determined solely by the parity of $2s$, placing half-integer pseudospins in the symplectic class (WAL) and integer pseudospins in the orthogonal class (WL). We also analyze the role of interband and intervalley scattering for $s=3/2$. By solving the resulting coupled Bethe-Salpeter equations, we demonstrate that channel mixing suppresses WAL and drives a crossover toward localization. Our results establish a general theory of localization across the full pseudospin hierarchy, revealing an interplay between internal geometry, symmetry class, and transport universality.

</details>


### [149] [$P$-wave Orbital Magnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18695)
*Yantao Li,Pavlo Sukhachov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新型的p波轨道磁性（p-wave orbital magnetism）概念，该磁性源于环电流（loop currents）诱导的轨道纹理（orbital texture），而非传统的非共线自旋结构。这种奇宇称（odd-parity）磁性受平移与时间反演联合对称性保护，其拓扑性质可通过环电流强度调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统非常规奇宇称磁体（unconventional odd-parity magnets）的实现通常依赖于晶格的非共线自旋结构（noncollinear spin textures）。本文旨在探索超越自旋自由度的新平台，建立轨道自由度（orbital degrees of freedom）作为实现p波磁性（p-wave magnetism）的替代途径。

Method: 作者提出了一个二维（2D）晶格模型（lattice model）来具体化这一概念。该模型的能谱包含狄拉克点（Dirac points），其非平凡拓扑性质（nontrivial topology）由环电流（loop currents）的强度控制。由于奇宇称磁性排斥宏观磁化，建议通过轨道霍尔电导率（orbital Hall conductivity）进行测量。

Result: 该模型展示了由环电流诱导的轨道纹理产生的p波轨道磁性，其奇宇称分量受平移与时间反演联合对称性保护，当对称性破缺时则产生偶宇称（even-parity）分量。模型的拓扑性质可通过环电流强度进行调控。

Conclusion: 本研究确立了轨道自由度作为超越非共线自旋纹理实现非常规p波磁性的新平台，并在连接奇宇称磁性与拓扑（bridging odd-parity magnetism and topology）方面迈出了重要一步。

Abstract: Realization of unconventional odd-parity magnets usually requires noncollinear spin textures of the underlying lattice. We propose a different concept of $p$-wave magnetism that originates from an orbital texture induced by loop currents. The resulting $p$-wave orbital magnetism is protected by the combined translation and time-reversal symmetry, with even-parity components arising when the symmetry is broken. Our proposal is exemplified by a two-dimensional (2D) lattice model whose energy spectrum contains Dirac points and which is characterized by a nontrivial topology controlled by the magnitude of the loop currents. Since the odd-parity magnetism precludes macroscopic magnetization, we suggest measuring it via orbital Hall conductivity. Our work establishes orbital degrees of freedom as an additional platform for unconventional $p$-wave magnetism beyond noncollinear spin textures, as well as makes a step forward to bridging odd-parity magnetism and topology.

</details>


### [150] [Large Scale Optimization of Disordered Hubbard Models through Tensor and Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18711)
*Jacob R. Taylor,Sankar Das Sarma*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于视觉神经网络的方法，用于调谐随机无序的二维量子点网格（quantum-dot grids）中的自旋量子比特平台。该方法利用张量网络生成的电荷稳定性数据训练神经网络，通过局部3×3窗口的信息来调谐更大阵列中的中心点，避免了大规模系统基态计算的指数复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 调谐随机无序的二维量子点网格中的自旋量子比特平台面临计算挑战，因为获取大规模系统的基态需要处理指数级增长的希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）。需要开发一种实用方法，能够避免这种计算上不可行的需求。

Method: 采用基于视觉的神经网络（vision-based neural networks），在张量网络生成的电荷稳定性数据上进行训练。提出滑动窗口方法（sliding-window approach），利用可模拟的局部3×3窗口信息来调谐中心点，然后将该窗口平移至整个晶格以校准更大设备。

Result: 在仅点内无序（on-site disorder）未知的实验相关情况下，神经网络在3×3设置中预测相关参数具有极高保真度（R² > 0.99）。经过少量大设备样本微调后，对5×5晶格（plaquette）中心点仍保持高精度（R² ≈ 0.98）。当所有点参数未知时，点内无序预测依然稳健（3×3和5×5的R² > 0.9），尽管其余参数更难从相同电荷稳定性数据中推断。

Conclusion: 研究表明，即使在全无序设置中，对于计算困难的5×5阵列，调谐中最具实际重要性的无序参数仍可可靠推断。这验证了滑动窗口方法的有效性，为大规模量子点网格的实用调谐提供了可行方案。

Abstract: We theoretically demonstrate a practical method for tuning randomly disordered 2D quantum-dot grids underlying spin qubit platforms using vision-based neural networks trained on tensor-network generated charge-stability data. We show that a simulatable local $3\times 3$ window already contains sufficient information to tune the central dot within a much larger array, thereby validating a sliding-window approach in which one tunes a local region and then translates that window across the lattice to calibrate a larger device. This avoids the computationally intractable necessity for obtaining the ground states for large systems with exponentially large Hilbert space. For the experimentally relevant case where only the on-site disorder is unknown, the neural network predicts the relevant parameters with very high fidelity in the $3\times 3$ setting [$R^2 >0.99$], and after fine tuning on only a small number of larger-device samples, it retains high accuracy for the central dot of a $5\times 5$ plaquette [$R^2\approx 0.98$]. When all the dots parameters are treated as unknown, prediction of the on-site disorder remains robust [$R^2>0.9$ for both $3\times 3$ and $5\times 5$], although the remaining parameters are substantially more difficult to infer from the same charge-stability data. This shows that the most practically important disorder parameter for tuning can still be inferred reliably even in the fully disordered setting for the computationally difficult 5x5 arrays.

</details>


### [151] [Proximitized Topological Insulator Charge Island Fabricated via In Situ Multi-Angle Stencil Lithography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18736)
*Benedikt Frohn,Tobias Schmitt,Vanessa Serrano,Anne Schmidt,Michael Schleenvoigt,Albert Hertel,Benjamin Bennemann,Abdur Rehman Jalil,Detlev Grützmacher,Peter Schüffelgen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种全原位、多角度模板光刻技术，用于制造拓扑绝缘体（TI）中的邻近超导电荷岛，解决了传统界面制备中拓扑绝缘体表面易降解的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合超导体-拓扑绝缘体（hybrid superconductor-topological insulator）纳米结构是研究拓扑保护表面态中邻近诱导超导性的有前景平台，但关键障碍在于实现清洁可控的超导体-TI界面，因为TI表面在环境条件下会迅速降解。

Method: 引入了一种全原位、多角度模板光刻技术（fully in situ, multi-angle stencil lithography），结合了(Bi,Sb)$_2$Te$_3$纳米带的选择性区域生长和角度控制的扩散阻挡层、超导Al以及超薄氧化物隧道势垒的沉积，无需后生长处理即可实现混合纳米结构的可扩展制造。

Result: 低温输运测量显示出稳健的库仑阻塞（Coulomb blockade）和低能电导的显著抑制，该抑制随磁场消失，这与岛中的邻近诱导超导性（proximity-induced superconductivity）一致。

Conclusion: 该技术建立了一个多功能纳米制造平台，使得能够探索先前未研究的基于TI的混合量子器件，并为研究拓扑纳米结构中的超导性开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Hybrid superconductor-topological insulator (TI) nanostructures constitute a promising materials platform for exploring proximity-induced superconductivity in systems with topologically protected surface states. A key obstacle has been the realization of clean and well-controlled superconductor-TI interfaces, as TI surfaces rapidly degrade under ambient conditions. Here, we introduce a fully in situ, multi-angle stencil lithography technique that enables the fabrication of proximitized charge islands in TIs. The approach combines selective-area growth of (Bi,Sb)$_2$Te$_3$ nanoribbons with angle-controlled deposition of diffusion barriers, superconducting Al, and ultrathin oxide tunnel barriers, allowing scalable fabrication of hybrid nanostructures without post-growth processing. Low-temperature transport measurements reveal robust Coulomb blockade and a pronounced suppression of low-energy conductance which vanishes with magnetic field, consistent with proximity-induced superconductivity in the island. These results establish a versatile nanofabrication platform that enables access to previously unexplored TI-based hybrid quantum devices and opens new routes for investigating superconductivity in topological nanostructures.

</details>


### [152] [Emergence of rigid Polycrystals from atomistic Systems with general Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19239)
*Leonard Kreutz,Timo Ziereis*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过Γ收敛（Γ-convergence）方法，证明了具有有限表面能标度的粒子系统从离散到连续极限的收敛性，建立了描述多晶结构形成的连续介质理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究一类粒子系统中多晶结构（polycrystalline structures）的形成机制，其中原子能量被建模为粒子能量之和，这些能量倾向于原子局部等距于参考晶格（reference lattice）。

Method: 采用Γ收敛方法分析具有有限表面能标度（finite surface-energy scaling）的构型，建立离散到连续极限（discrete-to-continuum limit），得到的连续理论由描述构型局部取向的分段常数场表示。

Result: 极限能量集中在晶界（grain boundaries）上，对应于微观构型具有恒定取向的区域之间的界面，能量密度取决于两个晶粒的取向以及界面的法向。

Conclusion: 由于刚性相互作用假设，具有插值边界层的固-固相变在能量上不利，因此能量密度分解为固-真空相变能量密度的两倍。

Abstract: We investigate the formation of polycrystalline structures in a class of particle systems. The atomistic energy is modeled as a sum of particle energies that favor atoms being locally isometric to a reference lattice. The discrete frame invariant energy allows for particle configurations in which no underlying lattice is assumed a priori.
  We prove a discrete-to-continuum limit for configurations with finite surface-energy scaling by means of $Γ$-convergence. The resulting continuum theory is described by piecewise constant fields encoding the local orientation of the configuration. The limiting energy is concentrated on grain boundaries, corresponding to the interfaces between regions where the microscopic configuration has constant orientation. The associated energy density depends on the orientations of the two grains as well as on the normal to the interface.
  Due to our assumptions on the rigid interactions, solid-solid phase transitions with interpolating boundary layers are not energetically favorable; the energy density therefore decomposes into twice the energy density for solid-vacuum transitions.

</details>


### [153] [Landau levels and magneto-optics in 30$^\circ$ quasi-periodic twisted bilayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18854)
*Masaru Hitomi,Takuto Kawakami,Mikito Koshino*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究为30°转角准周期双层石墨烯中的朗道能级（Landau levels）建立了理论框架，揭示了其独特的谱学特征和角动量选择规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解缺乏平移对称性但具有12重旋转对称性的准周期扭转双层石墨烯（quasi-periodic twisted bilayer graphene）在磁场下的量子行为，为这类准晶范德华（van der Waals）系统的体量子磁光（bulk quantum magneto-optics）研究提供理论基础。

Method: 采用准带（quasi-band）形式体系，通过在零场哈密顿量（zero-field Hamiltonian）中进行常规动量替换来引入磁场。该方法将朗道能级与准带结构直接关联，使其可理解为准带口袋（quasi-band pockets）的量子化轨道。

Result: 揭示了独特的谱学特征，包括弱磁场依赖的近平坦带（nearly flat bands）以及由12个偏离中心的口袋产生的高度简并能级。朗道能级由两个量子数分类：朗道能级指数（Landau-level index）和与底层准晶对称性相关的角动量。磁光导率（magneto-optical conductivity）计算表明光学跃迁遵循12重对称性强制的角动量选择规则（angular-momentum selection rules）。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一个基于对称性且计算高效的框架，用于准晶范德华系统的体量子磁光研究，预测了可在高场红外和太赫兹（THz）实验中观测到的谱学特征。

Abstract: We develop a theoretical framework for Landau levels in quasi-periodic twisted bilayer graphene at a $30^\circ$ twist angle, a system without translational symmetry but possessing 12-fold rotational symmetry. Using a quasi-band formalism, we incorporate the magnetic field through a conventional momentum substitution in the zero-field Hamiltonian. This approach provides a transparent physical interpretation by directly relating the Landau levels to the quasi-band structure, allowing them to be understood as quantized orbits of quasi-band pockets. By using this method, we reveal distinctive spectral features, including nearly flat bands with weak magnetic-field dependence and highly degenerate levels arising from twelve off-center pockets. The resulting Landau levels are classified by two quantum numbers: the Landau-level index and the angular momentum associated with the underlying quasicrystalline symmetry. We also compute the magneto-optical conductivity and show that optical transitions follow angular-momentum selection rules enforced by the 12-fold symmetry. Our approach provides a symmetry-based and computationally efficient framework for bulk quantum magneto-optics in quasicrystalline van der Waals systems, predicting spectroscopic signatures accessible in high-field infrared and THz experiments.

</details>


### [154] [Ultrafast Light-Induced Magnetoelectric Effect in van der Waals Magnetic Semiconductor Heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19080)
*Wenyi Zhou,Ravi Kumar Bandapelli,Hari Paudyal,Bangzheng Han,I-Hsuan Kao,Ziling Li,Yuqing Zhu,Durga Paudyal,Jyoti Katoch,Simranjeet Singh,Roland K. Kawakami*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究发现在WS₂/CrGeTe₃范德华异质结中，超快光激发产生的电荷转移改变了垂直磁各向异性，从而产生与孤立CrGeTe₃薄膜相反的磁扭矩符号，为范德华异质结中的超快磁操控提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究范德华（van der Waals, vdW）磁体与半导体原子尺度异质结中的磁动力学，探索不同于传统光热激发机制的新型磁操控方式。

Method: 采用时间分辨磁光克尔效应（time-resolved magneto-optic Kerr effect, TR-MOKE）进行实验观测，结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）和朗道-利夫希茨-吉尔伯特（Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert, LLG）模拟进行理论分析。

Result: 超快光激发WS₂/CrGeTe₃双层结构产生与孤立CrGeTe₃薄膜相反的磁扭矩符号；界面处光生载流子的电荷转移改变了垂直磁各向异性（perpendicular magnetic anisotropy），进而产生磁扭矩触发进动磁动力学；WS₂向CrGeTe₃的光生自旋流也能通过角动量转移触发进动动力学。

Conclusion: 该研究为具有II型能带排列（type-II band alignments）的范德华异质结中超快磁操控提供了新机制，揭示了电荷转移调控磁各向异性作为磁扭矩产生的新途径。

Abstract: Atomic-scale heterostructures of van der Waals (vdW) magnets and semiconductors provide a unique environment for exploring magnetic dynamics. In contrast to typical photothermal excitation of precessional magnetization dynamics by a pump laser pulse, we find that ultrafast optical excitation of a WS$_2$/CrGeTe$_3$ (CGT) bilayer produces an opposite sign of magnetic torque compared to an isolated CGT film. Experimental observations by time-resolved magneto-optic Kerr effect (TR-MOKE) and theoretical analysis by density functional theory (DFT) and Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert (LLG) simulations support a mechanism in which charge transfer of photoexcited carriers across the interface alters the perpendicular magnetic anisotropy, which in turn generates a torque on the magnetic layer to trigger precessional magnetization dynamics. These results provide new avenues for ultrafast manipulation of magnetization in vdW heterostructures with type-II band alignments. Lastly, we show that optically-generated spin currents from WS$_2$ into CGT can also trigger precessional dynamics via angular momentum transfer.

</details>


### [155] [Coherent Microwave Driving of Domain Wall Depinning in a Ferrimagnetic Garnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19164)
*Hanchen Wang,Laura van Schie,Adam Erickson,Lauren J. Riddiford,Davit Petrosyan,Christian L. Degen,Richard Schlitz,William Legrand,Pietro Gambardella*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究展示了通过微波场对铁石榴石薄膜中钉扎畴壁的线性和非线性动力学进行共振激发，实现了畴壁在降低外磁场条件下的脱钉扎，为通过局域非线性动力学操控磁结构提供了新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 畴壁动力学的相干控制为实现超越热激活运动的快速磁结构操控提供了途径。研究旨在探索通过共振激发钉扎畴壁的动力学来操控磁纹理的机制。

Method: 采用扫描氮空位磁力测量（scanning nitrogen-vacancy magnetometry）和非局域自旋泵浦测量（nonlocal spin-pumping measurements）来表征畴壁动力学。通过Pt条带线定义的钉扎线（pinning line）来限制畴壁，并使用微波场驱动。同时进行微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulations）来揭示动力学过程。

Result: 在磁振子间隙（magnon gap）内识别出低频模式，源于畴壁在钉扎线附近的局域振荡运动。当微波驱动进入非线性区域时，该模式使畴壁在降低的外磁场下实现脱钉扎（depinning）。微磁模拟显示随着驱动功率增加，畴壁从局域振荡到部分重定位，最终完全逃离钉扎区域的渐进过程。

Conclusion: 研究确立了在工程化钉扎位点对畴壁进行共振激发作为一种通过局域非线性动力学操控磁结构（magnetic textures）的机制。这为超越传统热激活方法的快速磁纹理操控提供了新途径。

Abstract: Coherent control of domain wall dynamics offers a route to fast manipulation of magnetic textures beyond thermally activated motion. We demonstrate resonant excitation of linear and nonlinear dynamics of a pinned domain wall in a ferrimagnetic garnet thin film driven by a microwave field. Using scanning nitrogen-vacancy magnetometry and nonlocal spin-pumping measurements, we identify a low-frequency mode inside the magnon gap, originating from the localized oscillatory motion of a domain wall across a pinning line defined by a Pt stripline. Upon increasing the microwave drive into the nonlinear regime, this mode enables domain wall depinning at reduced external magnetic fields. Micromagnetic simulations reveal a progression from localized oscillations to partial relocation between pinning sites and, ultimately, complete escape from the pinning region with increasing driving power. These results establish resonant excitation of domain walls at engineered pinning sites as a mechanism for manipulating magnetic textures via localized nonlinear dynamics.

</details>

TL;DR: 该研究分析了Nb$_{2n+1}$Si$_n$Te$_{4n+2}$范德华层状材料的线性光学电导率，揭示了其准一维节线态（quasi-one-dimensional nodal-line state）导致的各向异性Drude权重和线性频率依赖的光学响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用解析方法研究零温下的线性光学电导率，分析Drude权重（Drude weight）的各向异性特征，并进一步计算了有限温度对带内和带间光学电导率的修正。

Result: 零温下Drude权重表现出强各向异性：沿节线方向在电荷中性点保持有限值，而横向方向随费米能量（Fermi energy）呈二次方消失。带间光学电导率在纵向和横向均呈现线性频率依赖，仅斜率方向相关。

Conclusion: 有限温度分析表明，零温结果在实验相关温度范围内保持有效，为理解该材料家族的光学性质提供了理论基础，并揭示了其准一维节线态导致的独特各向异性光学响应。

Abstract: We study the linear optical conductivity of the Nb$_{2n+1}$Si$_n$Te$_{4n+2}$ family of layered van der Waals materials, which has recently gained considerable attention owing to its dimensionality-tunable electronic structure with a quasi-one-dimensional nodal-line state. At zero temperature, we analytically show that the Drude weight exhibits strong anisotropy: along the nodal-line direction it is finite at charge neutrality, whereas in the transverse direction it vanishes quadratically with Fermi energy. On the other hand, the interband optical conductivity exhibits the same linear frequency dependence along both the longitudinal and transverse directions, with only a direction-dependent slope in the low-frequency regime. We further analyze the leading finite-temperature corrections to the intraband and interband optical conductivities, showing that the zero-temperature results remain valid up to experimentally relevant temperatures.

### [157] [When heat goes astray -- non-local heating in a semiconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19203)
*Mahmoud Elhajhasan,Elena Trukhan,Katharina Dudde,Guillaume Würsch,Jana Lierath,Ian Rousseau,Raphaël Butté,Nicolas Grandjean,Nakib Haider Protik,Giuseppe Romano,Gordon Callsen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了半导体器件中热源与热点在微米尺度上的非局域性（non-local）加热现象，挑战了传统傅里叶热传导定律（Fourier's law）的局域性假设，并发现弹道声子输运（ballistic phonon transport）在远高于低温的温度下仍能显著影响热管理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半导体器件发热会限制其性能与寿命，传统热管理基于热源与热点局域重合的假设。该研究旨在验证当热源尺寸超过声子（phonons）平均自由程时，这一局域性范式（paradigm of heat locality）是否仍然成立。

Method: 研究采用横向结构化的半导体薄膜（laterally structured semiconductor membranes），通过聚焦良好的激光（well-focussed laser）进行加热，并利用拉曼测温法（Raman thermometry）绘制晶格温度分布图。

Result: 实验表明，在跨越数微米的长度尺度上，热局域性范式失效，出现了与傅里叶定律（Fourier's law）相矛盾的非局域加热现象。值得注意的是，非局域加热效应甚至可能超过激光诱导的局部加热。

Conclusion: 研究将观察到的非局域加热现象归因于远高于低温（cryogenic temperatures）下的弹道声子输运（ballistic phonon transport），这一发现对半导体器件的热管理策略具有重要启示。

Abstract: Heating of semiconductor devices limits their performance and lifetime, which must be addressed by thermal management starting at the heat source. It is a common assumption that the heat source and the resulting heat spot locally coincide, if their size exceeds the mean free paths of the main heat carriers, the phonons. We show that this paradigm of heat locality breaks down on length scales spanning several micrometers. As a consequence, non-local heating occurs in contradiction to Fourier's law. Therefore, we heat laterally structured semiconductor membranes that feature a rising number of interfaces with a well-focussed laser and map-out lattice temperatures by Raman thermometry. Remarkably, the non-local heating can exceed the laser-induced local heating, which we attribute to ballistic phonon transport far above cryogenic temperatures.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索外部场（激光调制势垒）、能隙、标量势和单轴之字形应变对石墨烯电子输运的联合调控效应，为光电器件应用提供新视角。

Method: 采用转移矩阵方法（transfer-matrix approach）结合边界条件，推导了传输概率作为不同系统参数的函数表达式，系统分析了能隙、标量势、应变、激光场参数的影响。

Result: 无应变时，增大能隙或势垒通常降低中心及下边带的传输；适中之字形应变产生显著的法诺型振荡（Fano-type oscillations），大应变时消失；激光场振幅增强传输，而频率升高抑制传输；上边带中，入射能量使共振峰右移，势垒宽度增加产生特征振荡模式。

Conclusion: 研究结果为通过外部场、应变和标量势调控带隙石墨烯的电子输运提供了新视角，在光电器件中具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: Electron transport in graphene under a laser-modulated barrier is studied in the presence of an energy gap, a scalar potential, and a uniaxial zigzag strain. The transfer-matrix approach is used with the boundary conditions to derive the transmission probabilities as functions of different system parameters. Without strain, raising either the energy gap or the potential generally reduces transmission in the central and lower sidebands. Moderate zigzag strain generates pronounced Fano-type oscillations that vanish at large strain, while transmission increases for low potential and decreases for high values. In the upper sideband, the incidence energy shifts the resonance peaks to the right, and growing the barrier width generates characteristic oscillatory patterns. Furthermore, increasing the laser field amplitude enhances transmission, whereas higher laser frequencies tend to suppress it. These findings offer new perspectives on controlling electronic transport in gapped graphene via external fields, strain, and potential applications in optoelectronic devices.

Abstract: Magnetic domain walls have long been pursued as carriers of classical information for storage and processing. In particular, the experimentally demonstrated high mobility of domain walls makes them not only suitable as stationary qubits but also as flying qubits, which may offer advantages over currently explored quantum computing platforms. In this Perspective, we outline our current understanding of the essential ingredients and key requirements for realizing universal quantum computation based on magnetic domain walls. We highlight promising concrete material platforms and identify the experiments that are still needed to advance this concept. Abstract: Two-dimensional halide perovskites host strongly bound excitons whose fine structure controls polarization selection rules and radiative recombination, yet several spectral features in (PEA)$_2$PbI$_4$ remain controversially assigned. Here, polarization-resolved low-temperature photoluminescence combined with first-principles G$_0$W$_0$+BSE calculations resolves both the intralayer and interlayer excitonic fine structure of this prototypical n=1 Ruddlesden-Popper perovskite. The low-energy multiplet is consistently described as a purely excitonic intralayer fine structure governed by crystal symmetry, octahedral distortions, and the two-layer unit cell, without invoking Rashba or exciton-polaron mechanisms as the primary origin. Although the static calculations underestimate their oscillator strength and do not reproduce the observed orthogonal polarizations, distortion-induced mixing with bright intralayer excitons strongly enhances interlayer optical activity and provides a plausible explanation for their visibility. ### [161] [Josephson diode effect in multichannel Rashba nanowires: role of inter-subband coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19385)
*Ardamon Sten,Sudeep Kumar Ghosh*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究通过分析多通道Rashba纳米线约瑟夫森结，重点关注子带间耦合（inter-subband coupling）的作用。该方法考虑了多通道系统中子带杂化（subband hybridization）对器件特性的影响。

Conclusion: 多通道杂化是实现和优化实验相关混合半导体纳米线约瑟夫森结中非互易超导输运的关键因素，为实际器件的设计和性能优化提供了重要理论指导。

Abstract: The Josephson diode effect (JDE) has attracted considerable attention for its ability to enable directional, dissipationless supercurrents in quantum devices. While hybrid semiconductor-superconductor nanowire Josephson junctions provide a canonical platform, most theoretical treatments assume the single-channel limit of the nanowire; however, realistic devices are inherently multichannel due to transverse confinement. Here, we investigate the JDE in multichannel Rashba nanowire Josephson junctions, focusing on the role of inter-subband coupling. We show that subband hybridization qualitatively modifies both the topological phase diagram and the JDE response of the device. In contrast to the single-channel case, the topological phase is restricted to a finite window of Zeeman fields, within which Majorana bound states lead to a strong enhancement of the diode efficiency. Crucially, inter-subband coupling enables a finite JDE even when the Zeeman field is aligned purely along the spin-orbit direction-- a mechanism absent in independent-channel and strictly one-dimensional systems. Furthermore, multichannel coupling enhances spectral asymmetry and significantly increases the diode efficiency compared to single-channel junctions. These results identify multichannel hybridization as a key ingredient for realizing and optimizing nonreciprocal superconducting transport in experimentally relevant hybrid semiconductor nanowire Josephson junctions.

### [163] [Photonic Chirality for Braiding and Readout of Non-Abelian Anyons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19456)
*Netzer Moriya*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于光学腔的方案，利用光子手性（photonic chirality）在分数量子霍尔平台上控制编织（braiding）并读取非阿贝尔任意子（non-Abelian anyons）。该方案通过反向传播的腔模与经典参考音调干涉产生旋转钉扎景观，将编织响应映射到腔模间相干性上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前非阿贝尔任意子的读取通常依赖于脆弱的电子干涉条纹（electronic interference fringes），这限制了实验的可操作性和鲁棒性。需要发展一种不依赖此类脆弱干涉效应的新读取方案。

Method: 提出基于光学腔的方案，利用反向传播腔模与经典参考音调干涉产生旋转钉扎景观（rotating pinning landscape）。光子循环方向决定景观旋转方向，使相反的光子分支驱动相反的任意子回路，实现分支条件编织操作（branch-conditioned braid operation）。

Result: 在有效理论层面推导了旋转钉扎项和读取关系，确定了由亚能隙驱动（subgap driving）、绝热输运（adiabatic transport）、局域化和腔相干性设定的操作窗口。在最小的四任意子Ising实现中，主要信号简化为校准相位；更一般地，当相对编织算符非标量时，相同的读取结构变为态依赖的。

Conclusion: 该方案提供了一条通过光学腔进行非阿贝尔任意子编织敏感读取的途径，无需依赖脆弱的电子干涉条纹，为实验实现非阿贝尔统计提供了更稳健的测量方法。

Abstract: We propose a cavity-based scheme that uses photonic chirality to control braiding and read out non-Abelian anyons in a fractional quantum Hall platform. Counter-propagating cavity modes interfere with a classical reference tone to create a rotating pinning landscape whose direction is set by photon circulation, so that opposite photonic branches drive opposite anyon loops. This realizes a branch-conditioned braid operation and maps the resulting braid response onto cavity intermode coherence. We derive the rotating pinning term and the readout relation at the effective-theory level, identify an operating window set by subgap driving, adiabatic transport, localization, and cavity coherence, and provide phenomenological diagnostics of transport locking. In the minimal four-anyon Ising realization, the leading signal reduces to a calibrated phase; more generally, the same readout structure becomes state dependent when the relative braid operator is non-scalar. The scheme provides a cavity route to braid-sensitive readout of non-Abelian anyons without relying on fragile electronic interference fringes.

</details>


### [164] [Nonequilibrium Kramers Turnover in a Kerr Parametric Oscillator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19527)
*Daniel K. J. Boneß,Gabriel Margiani,Wolfgang Belzig,Alexander Eichler,Oded Zilberberg*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究在克尔参量振荡器（Kerr parametric oscillator）这一非平衡驱动耗散系统中，通过理论分析和实验测量，首次观测到了类似Kramers turnover的激活速率预因子（prefactor）非单调依赖现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统平衡态双势阱系统中，热激活切换速率（thermally activated switching rate）的预因子表现出对环境耦合的非单调依赖关系，即Kramers turnover现象。本研究旨在探索这一基础交叉现象在非平衡驱动耗散系统中的类似表现。

Method: 首先通过理论分析在克尔参量振荡器中建立非平衡条件下的turnover物理机制。为解决激活势垒（activation barrier）与固有阻尼（intrinsic damping）之间的强相关性对turnover物理的掩盖，研究者重新标度旋转框架动力学（rescaling the rotating-frame dynamics），引入完全由参量驱动控制的可调有效摩擦（tunable effective friction）。

Result: 在微机电系统（micro-electromechanical device）中测量噪声诱导的相位滑移（noise-induced phase slips），观测到预因子温度依赖关系的明显交叉现象（distinct crossover）。这一结果明确分离了非平衡turnover区域，并揭示了耗散与涨落之间的竞争对激活动力学的深刻影响。

Conclusion: 研究结果不仅明确分离了非平衡turnover区域，还强调了耗散与涨落之间的竞争对激活动力学（activation dynamics）的深刻影响，这种影响超越了传统平衡态框架。

Abstract: Activation processes govern noise-induced switching between long-lived states. In an equilibrium double well, the thermally activated switching rate exhibits a prefactor with a nonmonotonic dependence on environmental coupling, a foundational crossover known as Kramers turnover. Here, we demonstrate a Kramers turnover analogue in a Kerr parametric oscillator, a driven-dissipative nonlinear system featuring two stable phase states. First, we analytically establish turnover physics in this out-of-equilibrium setting. There, the strong physical correlation between the activation barrier and intrinsic damping fundamentally obscures the underlying turnover physics. To overcome this limitation, we rescale the rotating-frame dynamics and introduce a tunable effective friction controlled entirely by the parametric drive. This rescaling comes at the cost of a concurrent rescaling of the effective temperature. Exploiting this simultaneous scaling, we leverage the effective temperature to extract the turnover directly from temperature-dependent observations. Subsequently, measuring noise-induced phase slips in a micro-electromechanical device, we observe a distinct crossover in the prefactor's temperature dependence. Our results unambiguously isolate the out-of-equilibrium turnover regime and highlight that the competition between dissipation and fluctuations profoundly shapes activation dynamics also beyond equilibrium.

</details>


### [165] [Landauer-based study of transport in Chern insulator heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19581)
*J. Luna-Ramos,A. Martín-Ruiz*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过连续Qi-Wu-Zhang模型分析平庸-拓扑-平庸结的电荷输运，发现克莱因隧穿（Klein tunneling）现象存在于体谱隙中，并推导了线性和非线性电导的解析表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索平庸-拓扑-平庸结中的电荷输运特性，特别是拓扑区域存在静电势垒时的克莱因隧穿现象，以及非线性输运响应与贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的关联。

Method: 采用连续Qi-Wu-Zhang模型描述二维陈绝缘体（Chern-insulating）相，通过波函数匹配方法获得角度和能量分辨的透射概率，并纳入朗道尔-布蒂克（Landauer-Büttiker）框架分析线性和非线性输运。

Result: 研究证明了尽管存在体谱隙（bulk spectral gap），克莱因隧穿仍然发生，完美透射源于狄拉克质量（Dirac mass）在结处的反转。推导了零温和有限温度下线性和非线性电导的闭合表达式，并展示了退相干（dephasing）抑制法布里-珀罗振荡（Fabry-Pérot oscillations）但不影响整体输运趋势。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了拓扑相变与狄拉克质量反转的对应关系，贝里曲率主导非线性输运响应。通过分析势垒高度、层厚度和拓扑质量参数的相互作用，确定了增强非线性响应中整流效应的最优参数区间。

Abstract: We study charge transport through a trivial-topological-trivial junction described by the continuous Qi-Wu-Zhang model, which realizes a two-dimensional Chern-insulating phase. The central region is tuned into the topological regime, while the adjoining leads remain trivial, and an electrostatic barrier of tunable height and width is applied exclusively to the topological slab. By matching wave functions across the interfaces, we obtain the angle- and energy-resolved transmission probability and demonstrate the occurrence of Klein tunneling despite the presence of a bulk spectral gap. Within the continuum Dirac description, this perfect transmission originates from the inversion of the Dirac mass across the junction, which reflects the band inversion of the central layer relative to the trivial leads. In the Qi-Wu-Zhang model considered here, this mass inversion coincides with the transition between trivial and Chern-insulating phases and is accompanied by finite Berry curvature that governs the nonlinear transport response. The resulting transmission function is then incorporated into a Landauer-Büttiker framework to analyze both linear and nonlinear transport. Closed-form expressions for the linear and nonlinear conductances are derived at zero and finite temperatures. In addition, we investigate the role of dephasing, showing how partial loss of coherence suppresses Fabry-Pérot oscillations while leaving the overall transport trends intact. Finally, we map out the interplay between barrier height, slab thickness, and topological mass parameter, identifying optimal regimes that yield enhanced rectification in the nonlinear response.

</details>


### [166] [Supermoiré domain-resolved effective Hamiltonians and valley topology in helical multilayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19608)
*Kyungjin Shin,Nicolas Leconte,Jeil Jung,Hongki Min*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究建立了螺旋多层石墨烯的理论框架，揭示了超莫尔（supermoiré）弛豫如何重构系统为局部周期性单莫尔畴，并发现低能谱分解为折叠狄拉克（Dirac）扇区，其拓扑响应由局部堆垛家族决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 螺旋三层石墨烯（helical trilayer graphene）已展现出拓扑能带和具有重塑莫尔周期性的关联态，但需要理论框架来理解更厚螺旋多层石墨烯的超莫尔弛豫和低能电子结构。

Method: 采用实空间晶格计算（real-space lattice calculations）研究螺旋多层石墨烯的超莫尔弛豫，通过弛豫重构得到局部周期性单莫尔畴（single-moiré domains），并在此基础上建立连续描述。在每个重构畴内，通过降维第一壳层模型（downfolding the first-shell model）获得狄拉克点附近的有效哈密顿量。

Result: 弛豫将系统重构为局部周期性单莫尔畴，低能谱分解为折叠狄拉克扇区（folded Dirac sectors）。通过评估有效哈密顿量中的谷陈数（valley Chern numbers），获得了与晶格计算一致的畴依赖且栅极可调的拓扑响应。

Conclusion: 研究结果为更厚的螺旋石墨烯堆垛建立了畴分辨的组织原则：折叠狄拉克扇区划分低能谱，而局部堆垛家族（local stacking families）决定相应的能带特征和拓扑响应。

Abstract: Extending moiré graphene beyond twisted bilayers, helical trilayer graphene has shown topological bands and correlated states with reshaped moiré periodicity. Here we develop a theoretical framework for helical multilayer graphene to investigate its supermoiré relaxation and low-energy electronic structure. Using real-space lattice calculations, we find that relaxation reconstructs the system into locally periodic single-moiré domains, which provide the basis for a continuum description. Within each reconstructed domain, downfolding the first-shell model yields effective Hamiltonians near the Dirac points that reveal how the low-energy spectrum decomposes into folded Dirac sectors. We further evaluate the valley Chern numbers encoded in these effective Hamiltonians, obtaining domain-dependent and gate-tunable topological responses consistent with the lattice calculations. Our results establish a domain-resolved organizing principle for thicker helical graphene stacks, in which folded Dirac sectors partition the low-energy spectrum, while local stacking families determine the corresponding band character and topological response.

</details>
